[1/519]
### 1x1x1x1
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/1x1x1x1
Avvisi: Ritual Exclusive.
Non confondere con: 67, 25, Los 67, Los 25, Festive 67, Guerriro Digitale, John Doe or Guest 666
Tagline: Really had value when there was a craft!
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$1.1M/s | Costo=$255.5M | Status=Obtainable (Rituals) | RarestMutation=Cursed(2016) | RarestTrait=Sombrero(40040) | Update=23 | Creator=Shedletsky + Roblox Myth Community | Ritual=Yes | Sounds=1x_1x_1x_1x_1.wav
--- OVERVIEW ---
1x1x1x1 is a Secret brainrot costing $255.5M and generating $1.1M/s.

1x1x1x1 takes the appearance of his toy version, with black limbs and a green, slightly transparent torso, making his ribs visible. 1x1x1x1 has red eyes with white pupils. His grin is closed shut by a zipper that connects to his mouth. 1x1x1x1 wields the Daemonshank, wearing his signature Viridian Domino Crown.

1x1x1x1 is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From the 1x1x1x1 Ritual with a 94% chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
This section is a trivia section. Please relocate any relevant information into other sections of the article.

- This brainrot is based on the Roblox myth 1x1x1x1 (an alternative account of former Roblox admin Shedletsky).
- The myth consisted about rumours of him being a hacker. Roblox themselves stated that it was a hacker in different avatar item descriptions; however, this was only for lore purposes. The account was later terminated.

- People were overpaying for it when it was in craft recipe of La Anniversary Grande.

- His counterpart is Guest 666, who makes $65,555,555/s more income, and John Doe, who makes $6.388.889/s more.

- 1x1x1x1's sound erroneously says "1x1x1x1x1" instead of his original name, containing an extra "x1".

- Alphabetically, 1x1x1x1 is the first Brainrot.

- Its original income when expanded is "$1,111,111/s" but is shortened to "$1.1M/s" to look more visually appealing.

- This brainrot generated some controversy because another Roblox game called "Forsaken" also uses 1x1x1x1 as a character, which made its fanbase believe that Steal a Brainrot copied it from the game, despite it being a popular myth on Roblox for decades before Forsaken even released.

### 25
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/25
Avvisi: Only obtainable from the Advent Calendar, part_of_family
Famiglia: Typographic Family
Non confondere con: 67, Festive 67, W or L, Los 25, or Los 67
Tagline: TWENTY FIVE *bass bosted*
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$2.5M/s | Costo=$600M | Status=Unobtainable (Advent Calendar) | Ritual=No | Sounds=TwentyFiveF4LeakSound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
25 is an anthropomorphic, green version of the number 25. They are wearing 2 santa hats, one for each number. They also have cute eyes. They are holding a blue, yellow-ribboned present, red and white gloves, and santa boots. 

25 is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Advent Calendar after logging in for 25 days straight.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
This section is a trivia section. Please relocate any relevant information into other sections of the article.

- 25's color and costume possibly could reference The Grinch.

- 25 makes $2.5M/s, because it is 25 with a decimal, a reference for its name.

- 25, Please my Present, and Bunnyman are unable to be obtained with Mutations or Traits, since they're instantly spawned on the base after being claimed from Advent Calendar.

- 25 represents the 25th day of December, which is christmas.

### 4th Bros
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/4th_Bros
Avvisi: stub
Non confondere con: Unclito Samito or Pop Pop Sahur
Tagline: Unc and Firework
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$3.75M/s | Costo=$800M | Status=Unobtainable (spawned only one time) | Update=56 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Ritual=No | Sounds=4th_Bros.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
4th Bros takes the design of Pop Pop Sahur and Unclito Samito as a Los duo brainrot. 

4th Bros is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Sammy spawning in the Red carpet once on July 4th 2026

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- 4th Bros are the first instance of a baby Unclito Samito and Pop Pop Sahur

- For some reason, 4th Bros has Unclito Samito having a beard, despite him being supposed to be a child.

- This is needed to craft Bufalino Boomberino along with 67 and Money Money Puggy .

- Despite both brainrots Unclito Samito and Pop Pop Sahur being a Brainrot God, on this brainrot it's a secret.
- This is common for most Los brainrots.

- Like Brunito Marsito and Flancito, this brainrot was only spawned once, and will never spawn again.

[4/519]
### 67
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/67
Avvisi: Only obtainable in Admin Abuses., part_of_family
Famiglia: Typographic Family
Non confondere con: Los 67, Festive 67, 25 or Los 25
Tagline: 89
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$7.5M/s | Costo=$1.25B | Status=Obtainable (Admin Lucky Block) | Update=16 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER + Maverick Trevillian, the "6-7 Kid" | Sounds=67_sound_effect.wav,67d.mp3,6776.mp3,67Origin.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
67 is a Secret brainrot that was added during the Extinct event. It costs $1.25B and has a base income of $7.5M/s 

67 is an anthropomorphic number 67 with white gloves and trainers. There are eyes on each digits, and he has no mouth, and it emits particles of each digit. He also has blue skin. 

67 is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting as a rare Brainrot from the Admin Lucky Block.

- Getting as a rare Brainrot from the Sammy's Base Event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- This Brainrot is based on the 67 meme, featuring a blonde boy named Maverick Trevillian (the 67 kid) shouting “Six-Seven!” while constantly shrugging in a crowd at a basketball game. Its idle animation references the gesture featured in the video that people sometimes do whenever mentioning the two numbers. (The original meme came from a YouTube song video seen here)

- 67 is the Brainrot with the shortest name in the game in terms of characters, along with 25.

- 67 has a 1 in 67 reoccurring chance of obtainment in Admin Lucky Block

- When SpyderSammy first spawned 67 for Caylus, it did not have a walking animation. When it was walking, it was T-Posing instead.
- This has been fixed since the update.

- 67 had walk animation 2 times (1st) was for spawning 200k of them in janaury 1st admin abuse, 2nd from its code, for the craft for the Bufalino Boomberino

[5/519]
### Abyssaloco
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Abyssaloco
Avvisi: stub
Non confondere con: Alessio
Tagline: Abyssion, the Forgotten One
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$33.3M/s | Costo=$4.3B | Status=Unobtainable (Backrooms Event) | Update=50 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Sounds=AbyssalocoSound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Abyssaloco is a Secret Brainrot. It makes $33.33M/s and costs $4.3B.

Abyssaloco is a purple Acanthinucella punctulata husk, a type of sea snail commonly associated with hermit crab. A singular eye with blue iris is occupying the operculum. The husk also has a pair of purple pincers.

Abyssaloco is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Backrooms Event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Approximately there are 25,000 Abyssaloco that existed in the world. SpyderSammy once put 20,000 Abyssaloco in the Cyber Craft Machine and spawned 2,500 Abyssaloco in the Backrooms Event during Taco Tuesday, assuming the other 2,500 are spawned naturally.

- Abyssaloco is the second best brainrot obtained from the Backrooms Event, before Rubrikiko.
--- ABYSSALOCO ---
Abyssion, the Forgotten One

[6/519]
### Agarrini la Palini
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Agarrini_la_Palini
Avvisi: This brainrot is now exclusive due to the Fuse Machine gone.
Tagline: if ur an og player, u hate this brainrot.
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$425K/s | Costo=$80M | Status=Unobtainable (Fuse Machine) | RarestMutation=Radioactive(1) | RarestTrait=Disco(20660) | Update=10 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Ritual=No | Sounds=Agarrinilapalini.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Agarrini la Palini is a Secret brainrot that was released along with the Fuse Machine as one of the most common Secrets obtainable from the machine itself. It costs $80M and produces $425K/s.

Agarrini la Palini is composed of an iron shovel with a wooden handle and a sad face. Agarrini la Palini can also be seen producing job application particles, similiarily to Job Job Job Sahur.

Agarrini la Palini is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Fusing it in the Fuse Machine

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Agarrini la Palini is a brainrot form of the phrase “agarra la pala”, a Spanish term translates directly to “grab the shovel”.
- In Argentina, "agarra la pala" is a slang for “get a job”, which has root from farmers and construction workers that grabbing the shovel first to start working. This slang is meant to taunt people to start doing something productive, instead slacking off idlely.

- Due to this slang meaning, Agarrini la Palini has particles in the form of job applications.

- Agarrini la Palini spawns as a Gear in your hotbar to dig with during the Grave Digger Event, with the name Agarrini Shovel.
- If not counting the Bat which used to be named Tung Bat after Tung Tung Tung Sahur, Agarrini Shovel is the only Gear that is based after Brainrot.

- If one doesn't count brainrots with names that start with numbers nor the Lucky Blocks, he is alphabetically the first brainrot in order.

- Agarrini la Palini is one of the brainrots thats has 2 1of1s one being Radioactive and the other being Cyber
--- AGARRINI LA PALINI ---
if ur an og player, u hate this brainrot.

[7/519]
### Alessio
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Alessio
Avvisi: Original lyrics contains NSFW content and blasphemy
Non confondere con: Carloo, Matteo, Antonio, Futbolini Skatini, Abyssaloco, or La Stadium Sekolah
Tagline: Futbolini Skatini's Lil Bro
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$85K/s | Costo=$17.5M | Status=Obtainable (Admin Lucky Block) | Update=13 | Creator=@pollonavale | Ritual=No | Sounds=Alessio.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Alessio is the second most common brainrot to get in the Admin Lucky Block. The brainrot was introduced during the Admin Abuse war on August 23rd, 2025.

Alessio can be seen as a humanoid football/soccer ball with humanoid characteristics, such as legs, and a face. It is visually seen not having arms. It can be seen having a cheeky nose, with one eyebrow down and one upright while having a slight smirk. It can be seen having slight pink cheeks, with giraffe legs and brown boots. Alessio can also be seen producing soccer ball particles.

Alessio is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtaining it from the Admin Lucky Block with a 30% chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- For being one of the most common brainrots to get from the Admin Lucky Block, Alessio is hated despite being slightly rarer than Carloo.

- Alessio and Pop Pop Sahur are cousin in the lore, hence their similar face, which become more apparent in their original image. Alessio is also related to Carloo and Matteo.

- On a video which was a competition for most hated brainrot this brainrot placed 1st by Kob3.
--- ALESSIO ---
Futbolini Skatini's Lil Bro

### Anpali Babel
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Anpali_Babel
Avvisi: Exclusive to the Craft Machine and Brainrot Trader.
Tagline: WHY IS LEVEL 1 SO HARD!
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$280K/s | Costo=$48M | Status=Unobtainable (Brainrot Trader and Craft Machine exclusive) | Ritual=No | Sounds=Anpali_Babel_.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Anpali Babel is a Craft Machine/Brainrot Trader Brainrot God brainrot. It costs $48M and generates $280K/s.

Anpali Babel is a charcoal-colored pixelated 3x5 Block Blast tile holding a smartphone with large, grey human-like feet and hands. His face has an evil looking smile with a large nose, paired with bulky black eyebrows and orange, lava-colored eyes.

Anpali Babel is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtaining from the Craft Machine
- Crafting Recipe
- 1x Mastodontico Telepiedone

- 3x Te Te Te Sahur

- Obtaining from the Brainrot Trader.
- Crafting Recipe
- 1x Aquanaut

- 1x Chihuanini Taconini

- or
- 1x Los Gattitos

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- The game on Anpali Babel’s phone can be confused for Tetris. However, it is actually Block Blast.

- Anpali Babel’s name is an Indonesian mispronounciation of the "Unbelievable" sound in Block Blast, the sound when you clear out the entire board.

- During when the trades revamp update was just released, if you were to search up Belula Beluga in the Index, Anpali Babel would show up instead. This glitch has since been fixed.
--- ANPALI BABEL ---
WHY IS LEVEL 1 SO HARD!

[9/519]
### Antonio
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Antonio
Avvisi: Unobtainable (Craft Machine was removed.)
Non confondere con: Appelini, Berryno, Strawberrita, Bananito, Carloo, Matteo, or Alessio
Tagline: BROCCOLI MAN
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$125M/s | Costo=$50B | Status=Unobtainable (Craft Machine) | RarestMutation=Candy(1) | RarestTrait=Ufo(4) | Update=15 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Ritual=No | Sounds=Antoniosssssound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Antonio is a Secret (originally Brainrot God) that was released on 9/6/25.

Antonio is depicted as a broccoli with anthropomorphic characteristics, having arms, legs, and a face. Antonio can be seen wearing a typical uniform, with a dark green tie, a brown belt, dark green pants, and a green suit. Antonio can be seen having a neutral expression, along with glasses. [the hell is that creature]

Antonio is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting it from the Craft Machine, which is no longer available.
- Crafting Recipe:
- 2x Ganganzelli Trulala.

- 1x Bombardiro Crocodilo.

- 1x Frigo Camelo.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Antonio is the fourth Brainrot to have actual human name. The first, second and third being Matteo, Carloo, and Alessio.

- At the time of Antonio's debut, barely anyone has this brainrot, because it required 2x Ganganzelli Trulala, which almost nobody had back then since Ganganzelli Trulala being considered bad in income.
- Ganganzelli Trulala was also a rare Mythic Fuse Machine exclusive, making it even harder to obtain. Furthermore, since Craft Machine was introduced after Fuse Machine, there's no way to obtain new Ganganzelli Trulala for crafting Antonio.

- Crafting Antonio was also considered not worth it, since the comparison between its income and its material income were $-2.9K/s.

- As such, there's only 1,506 existing Antonio. Out of the 1,506 Antonio, Candy mutation only having one in existence. Bloodrot has 2.

- It used to be the worst Brainrot God before being buffed to a Secret doing $125M/s.

- Antonio is one of five buffed brainrots on Update 40.
--- ANTONIO ---
BROCCOLI MAN

- While Aquanaut's name is a portmanteau of astronaut and aqua, aquanaut is a real word for underwater worker that working underwater for prolonged amount of time, known as saturation diving, much like how astronaut are space worker that working in outer space for prolonged amount of time. These workers are named aquanaut since their job is also as risky and lethal as astronaut's job.

STATS: Rarita=Legendary | Income=$1.2K/s | Costo=$290K | Status=Unobtainable (Cyber Craft Machine) | Update=15 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Sounds=BanditosoundAxolito.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Bandito Axolito is an Epic brainrot added on September 6, 2025. 

Bandito Axolito is an anthropomorphic axolotl with brown mustache, black suit, black top hat, and wielding a gun.

Bandito Axolito is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting it from the Craft Machine.
- Crafting Recipe:
- 2x Trippi Troppi.

- 2x Bandito Bobritto.

- Getting it from the Cyber Craft Machine
- Crafting Recipe:
- 1× Bandito Bobritto

- 1× Trulimero Trulicina

- 2× Chef Crabracadabra

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Bandito Axolito's full income is $1,225K/s.

- Bandito Axolito is not on the Aquatic Index and unable to be fished in Fishing Event despite being an aquatic animal.

- Bandito Axolito was buffed during the new Craft Machine from a Epic to a Legendary.

- Bandito Axolito and Bulbito Bandito Traktorito are the only Brainrot in the game that wielding an actual gun.

- This brainrot recieved the smallest buff behind Love Love Bear.

[37/519]
### Bicicleteira Family
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Bicicleteira_Family
STATS: Income=$3.5M/s | Costo=$3.5M
--- OVERVIEW ---
Bicicleteira Family are Brainrots based on humanoid gumball machines, usually being a rider. It is named named after "chiclete", Brazilian Portuguese word for gumball, referring to their appearance after gumball machine, and "bicicleta", Brazilian Portuguese word for bicycle. All of Bicicleteira Family Brainrots are Secret Brainrots.

Chicleteira Bicicleteira, the first Bicicleteira Family Brainrot, was made by TikTok and YouTube user @brainbenderchannel. The rest of Bicicleteira Family Brainrots are made by BRAZILIAN SPYDER, usually as reskin of Chicleteira Bicicleteira. Since both @brainbenderchannel and BRAZILIAN SPYDER are Brazilian, this made Bicicleteira Family Brainrots categorized as Brazilian Brainrot.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Chicleteira Noelteira, Chicleteira Cupideira and Chicleteira Surfeiteira are the only members of the Bicicletera Family that don't ride a bicycle.

Bisonte Giuppitere appears to be a planet—Jupiter—with a bison’s head on it. It is wearing shoes; however, it doesn’t have legs, so it looks like it’s floating above the shoes.

- His Halloween version is Mummy Ambalabu.

[50/519]
### Brainrot Trader
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Brainrot_Trader
Avvisi: Machine article
Non confondere con: the Brainrot Dealer, Trade Machine, Trading Plaza, or Los Traders
--- APPEARANCE ---
The Brainrot Trader appears to be a merchant, which is just a retexture of the Brainrot Dealer, He is under a blue cart with a white top. He wears a blue jacket/robe with the lines being white, he also wears a blue shirt with a golden closer and wears black boots and blue pants. He also has pale peach skin and a hat. He also seems to resemble the Brainrot Dealer, but that could be just because of the same/new white-and-blue color scene. He leans on his cart with one leg while using his hat to cover his eyes
--- TRIVIA ---
- Brainrot Trader is the second one that is not a Fuse or Craft event, with the first being Brainrot Dealer. Despite this, Brainrot Trader is technically a variant of Craft Machine, since both are events that exchanging already existing Brainrots for the new one.
- Mangolini Parrocini, Sigma Girl, Squalanana, Piccionetta Macchina, Anpali Babel, and Belula Beluga are the Brainrots from the Craft Machine that is carried back in the Brainrot Trader. Mangolini Parrocini was accidentally added to the Brainrot Trader by Sammy during admin abuse, but Sammy never removed it.

- The BRAZILIAN SPYDER team added at least one new Brainrot to the Brainrot Trader every Saturday update.
--- BRAINROT TRADER ---
Brainrot Dealer < Brainrot Trader

### How many brainrots

22
--- CHRONOLOGY ---
### Previous Machine

Brainrot Dealer

### Next Machine

Santa's Fuse

### Status

Removed (Replaced by Santa's Fuse)

The Brainrot Trader NPC replaced the Brainrot Dealer on Saturday, November 15th 2025. This was confirmed by Sammy during the November 11th Taco Tuesday Admin Abuse, and was first revealed in the Discord Server 6 hours before the feature's release. It was removed on December 6, 2025 and got replaced by Santa's Fuse.

Every two hours, four trade offers will appear for the user to trade/complete. These trades require existing Brainrots in the game to acquire new ones from the Brainrot Trader.

These trades are server-sided, removing the issue of autoclickers from the Brainrot Dealer's global stock. The Brainrot that are traded in Brainrot Trader has more than one fixed requirements, and each tradeable Brainrot will require a different set of existing Brainrots every two hours.

[51/519]
### Brainrots
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Brainrots
Avvisi: Some brainrots are Exclusive or were Removed from the game.
--- OVERVIEW ---
Collecting Brainrots is the core feature of Steal a Brainrot, hence the name. Below are all documented Brainrots known to have existed inside the game. Along with these, there are signifiers.

There are 499 indexable brainrots in the game, and 14 miscellaneous brainrots (Lucky Blocks, Gold Elf and Gold Egg), bringing the amount of brainrots to 513.

### Signifiers

Signifiers are to be used to give a user a quick glance on how a Brainrot was obtainable or when it was added into the game and how. The current signifiers a Brainrot article can have are:

Icon
| 
Name
| 
Description
| 

| 
Admin Abuse Brainrots
| 
Brainrots that can only be obtained through Admin Abuse.
| 

| 
Event Brainrots
| 
Brainrots that, at one point or another, were part of an event.
| 

| 
Lucky Block Brainrots
| 
Brainrots that are only obtainable from a Lucky Block.
| 

| 
Limited Quantity Brainrots
| 
Brainrots that have a Limited Quantity inside the game, predetermined by the BRAZILIAN SPYDER team.
| 

| 
Machine Brainrots
| 
Brainrots that are only obtainable from a Machine.
| 

| 
Recognized Brainrots
| 
Brainrots that are widely known inside the community to have an "elevated" value compared to other Brainrots in the same rarity.
| 

| 
Depreciated Brainrots
| 
Brainrots that are widely known inside the community to have a "lower or depreciated" value compared to other Brainrots in the same rarity.
| 

| 
Robux Purchasable Brainrots
| 
Brainrots that can be purchased using  Robux.
| 

| 
Ritual Brainrots
| 
Brainrots that are only obtainable from Rituals.
| 

| 
DLC
| 
Brainrots that required a third-party purchase with $ USD to obtain, this being through game merchandise.
| 

| 
Lucky Catch
| 
Brainrots that rarely spawn or have a low chance of being obtained.
| 

| 
Non-Indexable
| 
Brainrots that don't show up in the game's index and are currently either obtainable or unobtainable content.
|
--- TRIVIA ---
- When a Secret (or any kind of Lucky Block spawns, except the Mythic Lucky Block, Festive Lucky Block, and the Heart Lucky Block), it is announced in the chat and its name is shown.

- When an OG and Brainrot God spawns, its name is said but not announced in chat (except for the Brainrot God Lucky Block)

- When an OG appears, it starts a special Event. ( Strawberry for Strawberry Elephant, Skibidi for Skibidi Toilet and Meowl for the Meowl and Headless Horseman is unobtainable, meaning it has no trait or event,)

- Brainrots can get Traits and Mutations which help make the brainrot make more money, with the exception of the Sleepy trait, which halves its multiplier.

- Some brainrots cannot be obtained by normal players and can only be obtained by SpyderSammy . They are the brainrots that have the Admin rarity, excluding the Lucky Blocks.

- Many Brainrots (such as Brainrots from past Events or Machines) are still displayed in the Index, but it is impossible to obtain them without Stealing or trading.
- Few Brainrots even appear in the mutation indexes, and those that do are truly impossible to obtain without glitches.

- OG Brainrots grant the player a specific base skin depending on the Brainrot the player has, as long as the Brainrot is still in the player’s base. The skin will be unequipped if the Brainrot is stolen.

- Despite Gattatino Nyanino being inspired by a meme and song from 2011, it is not an OG.

- The best brainrot currently as of 5/24/26 is Spyder Elephant.

- Many brainrots are food based and they are listed here.

- If you stay AFK in a private server for approximately 16–19 minutes, you will be kicked and automatically rejoined into a public server. This has now been fixed.

- Brainrots are referred to as "Animals" in the game files.

- Headless Horseman is the only Secret to be buffed to an OG.

- Some Brainrot God, Mythic, and Legendary brainrots have been buffed to Secret.

- The worst Brainrot, Noobini Pizzanini, is the only Brainrot unaffected by the Sleepy Trait and the Gold Mutation.

### Brasilini Berimbini
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Brasilini_Berimbini
Avvisi: Admin Abuse Exclusive
Tagline: me when spreading misinformation
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$285K/s | Costo=$55M | Sounds=BrasiliniBerimbini.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Brasilini Berimbini is a Brainrot God that makes $285K/s and costs $55M.
--- APPEARANCE ---
Brasilini Berimbini is a traditional Berimbau in white pants with black sunglasses. Unlike most of the brainrots (or all of them), Brasilini Berimbini has a much more dynamic idle pose instead of simple movements, with its idle pose being a Ginga, a stance in Capoeira.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Brasilini Berimbini was released on September 27, 2025, and is only obtainable through Admin Abuse until the Halloween Update on October 11, 2025.

- Despite being a Brazilian Brainrot, Brasillini Berimbini wasn’t released on the same date the Brazilian Event was added to the game.

- While Brasilini Berimbini was spawned only once in Divine and Cyber, during an Admin Abuse in respective Mutation runtime on every server to help players fill their index—no Default, Gold, Diamond, or Rainbow Brasilini Berimbini has been spawned again since October 11, 2025.

- Contrary to popular belief, Brasilini Berimbini does not spawned in Escape Tsunami LTM.
--- BRASILINI BERIMBINI ---
me when spreading misinformation

[55/519]
### Brri Brri Bicus Dicus Bombicus
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Brri_Brri_Bicus_Dicus_Bombicus
Non confondere con: Brr Brr Patapim or Brr es Teh Patipum
Tagline: this is sparta
STATS: Rarita=Epic | Income=$175/s | Costo=$30K | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | Sounds=BrriBrriBicusDicusBombicus.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Brri Brri Bicus Dicus Bombicus is an Epic Brainrot that costs $30K and generates $175/s.

Brri Brri Bicus Dicus Bombicus is a crow standing with its two feet and donning Roman soldier armor. A necklace made by strawberries and red cape adorns Brri Brri Bicus Dicus Bombicus. 

Brri Brri Bicus Dicus Bombicus is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Brri Brri Bicus Dicus Bombicus has the longest name in the entire game (including spaces) , at 30 characters, 2 ahead of Cuadramat and Pakrahmatmamat, Tracoducotulu Delapeladustuz and Developini Braziliaspidini.
- The name itself can get longer if Brri Brri Bicus Dicus Bombicus has a John Pork Trait, making it the longest displayable name in the entire game, being "Brri Brri Bicus Dicus Bombicus is Calling...". Technically it can be even longer by adding the Radioactive mutation making it "Radioactive Brri Brri Bicus Dicus Bombicus is Calling...".

- In his buying/stealing sound, the "Brri" is pronounced as "Berry"

- Brri Brri Bicus Dicus Bombicus' cape has cloth physics, a special type of rendering used to make an object appear/behave as if it's a cloth.
- The way this is done is to make each part of the cloth a different vertices, basically hundreds of squares instead of one object. That way each "square" can move and act as if it was a real cape.

### Brunito Marsito
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Brunito_Marsito
Avvisi: As stated by SpyderSammy, it was only spawned once
Non confondere con: Brutto Gialutto
Tagline: Not Brutto Gialutto
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$3.5M/s | Costo=$750M | Status=Unobtainable | Sounds=Copy_C2B0B3A6-0DCE-44F0-836E-354986AF96D6.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
SpyderSammy said that he would only ever spawn Brunito Marsito once (during Bruno Mars' in-game concert as part of the 01/17/26 Admin Abuse).

Brunito Marsito's appearance is based off of the attire that Bruno wore in the music video for his 2026 song, "I Just Might". It sporting black afro hair with red bandanna and wears a green suit with gold engravings and buttons adorning it, with matching green pants and brown boots.

Brunito Marsito is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Sammy spawning this during Admin Abuse

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- The addition of Brunito Marsito marks the first official celebrity collaboration in Steal a Brainrot's history.
- Brunito Marsito is also the 3rd Brainrot to be based off of a real life person, after Sammyni Spyderini and Raccooni Jandelini.

- Like Raccooni Jandelini, Brunito Marsito was only spawned once during Admin Abuse.

- Brunito Marsito is floating in the Index.

- Brunito Marsito is impossible to get in any Mutation except Gold, Diamond, and Rainbow, since there were no Mutations running during the only time Brunito Marsito was spawned. This means the rarest mutation Brunito Marsito comes in is Rainbow.

- Brunito Marsito is the first Brainrot to have its exact Exist Counts leaked. After the Bruno Mars event, Roblox published the report of the event, alongside the amount of Brunito Marsito that was distributed during said event.
- While the report initially recorded 5,428,644 Brunito Marsito has distributed after the event, the updated Exist Counts shown the amount of Brunito Marsito in-game has reduced to ~2,320,000, due to players voiding it.

- Despite it being the first brainrot sammy spawned only once, it has barely any value or demand in trading it.
--- BRUNITO MARSITO ---
Not Brutto Gialutto

### Buho del Cielo
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Buho_del_Cielo

--- OVERVIEW ---
Buho del Cielo is a Legendary Brainrot that costs $325K. It generates $1.3K/s.

Buho del Cielo appears as a blue Owl. It has pastel blue feathers except for the belly area and head area, which both are white. It has an orange beak, conic in shape. It has 2 big eyes, appearing as yellow-orange irises with the absence of a sclera. It has pitch-black pupils, with white specs resembling the way light reflects on one's eyeballs. It has 2 plumicorns, blue with white outlines. It has 2 orange feet. It is standing on a white and small cloud.

Buho del Cielo is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Fusing from the Divine Fuse Machine.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Buho del Cielo is very similar to Meowl in design and stance.

- Buho del Cielo means "Sky Owl" in Spanish.

- Owls do not have horns or ears on the tops of their heads, as Buho del Cielo appears to have. They are called Plumicorns, and are actually tufts of feathers.

- Buho del Cielo is a reskin of Buho de Fuego. It is also in the same family as Buho de Noelo and Buho de Volto.

Capitano Moby appears to be a blue dotted whale with a pirate ship on top of it. The top deck of the pirate ship has lanterns hanging on the front, near the mouth of the whale. The bow and beakhead of pirate ship evoking narwhal's horn in Capitano Moby design.

- Capitano Moby is most likely based on Moby Dick, otherwise known as the sperm whale, from the novel Moby Dick By Herman Melville; hence the name Capitano "Moby".

- On February 24th, 2026, at the last Admin Abuse before the Update 40, Capitano Moby was temporarily put in the Fuse Machine by Sammy along with Los 67, Garama and Madundung, and Cerberus. (He almost replaced Hydra Dragon Cannelloni with Meowl, but his scripter told him not to).

- Sammy made a Poll saying "Who's bigger", displaying an option to vote "Steak", or "Capitano Moby". Steak won the poll.

- Capitano Moby is used in the design of Moby Bros despite not being in any of its recipes.

### Caramello Filtrello
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Caramello_Filtrello
Avvisi: Craft Machine Exclusive.
Tagline: miau miau
STATS: Rarita=Legendary | Income=$1K/s | Costo=$255K | Status=Unobtainable (Craft Machine) | RarestMutation=Cursed(2) | RarestTrait=Claws(11) | Update=15 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Ritual=No | Sounds=Caramellosoundiltrello.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Caramello Filtrello is a Legendary Brainrot that was added on 9/6/25. It costs $255K and has a base income of $1K/s.

Caramello Filtrello is based of a dog breed called a Caramel Mongrel Dog. Its torso can be seen encased in a filter made out of clay, along with a collar, and two legs sticking out of it.

Caramello Filtrello is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Crafting it in the Craft Machine
- Crafting Recipe:
- 1x Salamino Penguino

- 1x Bananita Dolphinita

- 1x Burbaloni Loliloli

- 1x Chimpanzini Bananini

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Caramello Filtrello is based to a popular breed of dog in Brazil known as "Cachorro Caramelo", which is also a reference to a common clay water filter. Together, the design of Caramello Filtrello is a visual pun of "dogwater".

- The original creator of the brainrot is @br_brainrot on TikTok, making him one of few Brazilian Brainrots in the game.[1]

- Caylusaurus design is based on his Brainrot representation in Survive Lava for Brainrots, his own game, which is also named Caylusaurus.

- While both he and Steak are the owners of Survive Lava for Brainrots, his Brainrot representation in Steal a Brainrot is directly based on his representation in Survive Lava for Brainrots, in contrast to Steak which making his own brand new Brainrot for Steal a Brainrot.

- All of Caylusaurus' Craft Materials are based on Brainrot with aura vibes. Burrito Bandito is based on gangster, Nuclearo Dinossauro is based on warplane and Tyrannosaurus rex, and Money Money Puggy is based on pile of money.

- Caylusaurus is the first Limited Quantity Brainrots to not have a Brainrot with an income $30M/s+ as its recipe, after the release of Nacho Spyder.

### Celularcini Viciosini
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Celularcini_Viciosini
Avvisi: Unobtainable, exclusive to the Craft Machine.
Tagline: roblox please remove the chat update thank you!!!

--- OVERVIEW ---
Celularcini Viciosini is a Secret brainrot that was released along with the Craft Machine. It costs $2.7B and has a base income of $22.5M/s.

Celularcini Viciosini is an anthropomorphic white smartphone with two cameras. It is grumpy, wearing a watch, and holding a black smartphone. On the phone is a pixelated version of the homepage on Roblox of Steal a Brainrot, during the Strawberry Elephant update.

Celularcini Viciosini is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtaining it via the Craft Machine, which is no longer obtainable as it has been removed as of now.
- Crafting Recipe:
- 1x Pot Hotspot

- 1x Job Job Job Sahur

- 2x La Grande Combinasion

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Celularcini Viciosini was released on September 13th of 2025 and became obtainable in the Craft Machine. Original video can be viewed here.

- On the smaller phone, Celularcini Viciosini is looking at the Roblox homescreen of Steal a Brainrot. This making it the only brainrot to be playing Steal a Brainrot in Steal a Brainrot.

- The original image of Celularcini Viciosini had three cameras, but the in-game version has only two cameras to avoid copyright.
- The original image also had a Apple logo on the smaller phone, but it was removed for the same reason.

- Celularcini Viciosini's name is the brainrot version of "Celular Vicio" which literally translates to Cell Phone addiction.

- For some reason the sound says "Che-loo-lar-chee-NEE-vicho-see-nee" not "Ce-loo-lar-see-NEE-vis-io-see-NEE". This making Celularcini Viciosini one of few Brainrots with mispronounced name, the others are Fishino Clownino, La Extinct Grande, and Vulturino Skeletono.

- In the original image, Celularcini Viciosini is depicted as wearing a Rolex Submariner. However, in-game, he is wearing what looks to be a Patek Phillipe Nautilus.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Cerberus was teased on 6th January 2026 at 6:33PM EST.

- In the game logo, the Cerberus was labeled as "Hellhound", since myths say "It is the Hellhound of the Underworld". Perhaps Hellhound was the old name for Cerberus.

- It is the first brainrot in Steal a Brainrot to have 3 heads, the second being Hydra Dragon Cannelloni and the third being Hydra Bunny.
- Despite Hydra Bunny being a reskin of Cerberus, Hydra Bunny is named after Hydra Dragon Cannelloni.

- Cerberus isn't technically a Brainrot, since it's a Greek mythical creature created long before AI was even a thing (it was created in 1956, AI was officially "created" as a field of study at the 1956 Dartmouth Conference).

- Cerberus is the oldest "Brainrot" to exist, first depicted in 8th — 7th century BC.

- Cerberus has the old Headless Horseman stats.
- Interestingly, they both are part of the oldest "Brainrots" to exist. Cerberus was first depicted in 8th - 7th century BC in ancient times as mentioned above, whereas Headless Horseman was inspired of a 1820s tale titled "The Legend of Sleepy Hollow".

- Cerberus is the second brainrot to represent Hell, with the first being Guest 666.

- On February 6th, Sammy announced that Cerberus would be removed from the Red Carpet and put into the Secret Lucky Block.
- However, Sammy decided not to do this, stating it wouldn't be fair for people that got it before. Celestial Pegasus was then introduced to be successor of it, hence their same stats.

- Sammy replaced Hydra Dragon Canneloni with Cerberus in the Fuse Machine for a few hours during February 24th, 2026 Taco Tuesday.
--- CERBERUS ---
Whose duty it was to guard the entrance – against whom or what does not clearly appear.

[116/519]
### Cocofanto Elefanto
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Cocofanto_Elefanto
Non confondere con: Cocosini Mama, Penguino Cocosino, Strawberry Elephant, Lirilì Larilà, Burbaloni Loliloli or Elefanto Frigo
Tagline: bro is NOT Strawberry Elephant
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$19K/s | Costo=$6.5M | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | Ritual=No | Sounds=Cocofantosoundele.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Cocofanto Elefanto appears to be an elephant fused with a coconut. It has legs going beyond the coconut, and a head with tusks, a trunk and two large eyes. It has 2 large gray ears. Its skin is light grey, similar to other elephants. It has an aura that consists of coconut water coming out of it.

Cocofanto Elefanto is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
This section is a trivia section. Please relocate any relevant information into other sections of the article.

- Cocofanto Elefanto is the lowest income bearing Brainrot God in the game, making only $19K/s per second.

- Cocofanto Elefanto is needed in Rebirth 9. (Formerly Rebirth 8)

- Cocofanto Elefanto has been buffed 2 times; $10K/s to $17.5K/s and then finally $19K/s since some Mythic brainrots´s incomes exceeded or were close to Cocofanto's income.

- Cocofanto Elefanto produces similar effects to Burbaloni Loliloli, since they're coconut-based Brainrots.

- Sammy once spawned this brainrot with the Strawberry trait, which made it look like the Strawberry Elephant, the best Brainrot in the game.
- Uniquely, Cocofanto Elefanto along with other Brainrot Gods also used to be the best Brainrots in the game back in May 2025 when Steal a Brainrot was released, only beaten by Tralalero Tralala.

- This is why they were called Brainrot Gods, and why the text for them was rainbow, to represent the rarity and high value of them (before they were overshadowed by Secrets and OGs)

- After 2 Cocofanto Elefanto's buffs, there aren't any brainrots that make $10K/s or $17.5K/s.
--- COCOFANTO ELEFANTO ---
bro is NOT Strawberry Elephant

[119/519]
### Coffin Tung Tung Tung Sahur
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Coffin_Tung_Tung_Tung_Sahur
Avvisi: stub, Removed due to Copyright.
Non confondere con: the regular Tung Tung Tung Sahur. If you're looking for all Sahurs, click here
Tagline: Triple T is dead AGAIN….
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$0/s | Costo=$500M | Status=Removed (Admin Abuse) | Ritual=No | Sounds=Tung_Tung_Tung_Sahur_OFFICIAL_SOUND.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Coffin Tung Tung Tung Sahur was a Secret brainrot added to the game. This brainrot costs $500M. This brainrot is unique as it has no income and behaves similar to a lucky block. When opened, it becomes Tung Tung Tung Sahur.

Coffin Tung Tung Tung Sahur has the appearance of four Tung Tung Tung Sahurs (possibly family or friends) with a black suit and pants. They appear to be holding a coffin. The coffin seems to be colored brown like any other coffin, and it has a yellow stripe around it referencing the meme called "Coffin Dance", and its song can also be heard while it walks.

Coffin Tung Tung Tung Sahur is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting it spawned by SpyderSammy, and opening it to get Tung Tung Tung Sahur.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Coffin Tung Tung Tung Sahur's animation and model were based on the coffin dance that was made around 2003, but became popular around March 2020.
- Despite this, it is not an OG brainrot.

- This brainrot opens like a Lucky Block.

- Technically, Coffin Tung Tung Tung Sahur is a lucky block. If you go into the games code, Coffin Tung Tung Tung Sahur is shown as a lucky block.

- The sound that Coffin Tung Tung Sahur plays is Astronomia by Vicetone and Tony igy, the link is here.
- This is also the same song played in the Coffin Dance meme.

- Coffin Tung Tung Tung Sahur is the first lucky block with an animation.

- This is the first lucky block to not be shaped like other lucky blocks.

- This is the first Brainrot that can crawl.

- This is the first Lucky Block to have only one brainrot (Tung Tung Tung Sahur) inside it.

- This is the only brainrot to be both openable and not have an income (since it's not Tung Tung Tung Sahur itself), but not be a Lucky Block, Gold Elf dosen't count as it is purely a currency, and therefore, unopenable.
--- COFFIN TUNG TUNG TUNG SAHUR ---
Triple T is dead AGAIN….

Signifiers | 

  |

--------------------------------------------------

### Cooki and Milki
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Cooki_and_Milki
Avvisi: Santa's Fuse exclusive.
Tagline: Dipping cooki on milki
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$155M/s | Costo=$100B | RarestMutation=Cursed(10) | RarestTrait=Taco(2966) | Update=27 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Ritual=No | Sounds=CookiAndMilki.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Cooki and Milki is a Secret Brainrot that costs $100B and generates $155M/s.

Cooki and Milki appears as a grumpy chocolate chip cookie with a chocolate moustache with cookie legs and happy cup of milk with white legs.

Cooki and Milki is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From Santa's Fuse.

- From Red Carpet, a core feature.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Cooki and Milki was the only Brainrot from Santa's Fuse that was obtainable before the release of the Santa Fuse.
- Santa's Fuse released in Update 28, but Cooki and Milki was added in Update 27, and was obtainable from the Red Carpet. When the Santa Fuse was added, though, it was made so it was unable to spawn on the Red Carpet.

- Before the Santa's Fuse was released, Cooki and Milki could be obtained from the Red Carpet with a RoadWeight of 3.00E-13 (0.0000000000003).
--- COOKI AND MILKI ---
Dipping cooki on milki

[126/519]
### Cuadramat and Pakrahmatmamat
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Cuadramat_and_Pakrahmatmamat
Avvisi: Brainrot Trader Exclusive.
Non confondere con: Pakrahmatmamat, Pakrahmatmatina, or Chrismasmamat
Tagline: noteboos
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$1.4M/s | Costo=$400M | Status=Unobtainable (Brainrot Trader) | Sounds=Cuadramat.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Cuadramat and Pakrahmatmamat is a Secret Brainrot that was added on November 22, 2025 3:00PM EST. Which was a Admin Abuse by SpyderSammy.

Cuadramat and Pakrahmatmamat consists of two entities, one being an anthropomorphic purple notebook and another being a pencil, Pakrahmatmamat, which held by the Notebook.

Cuadramat and Pakrahmatmamat is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtaining it from the Brainrot Trader.
- Crafting Recipe:
- 1x Los Cucarachas

- 1x La Vacca Saturno Saturnita

- or
- 1x Graipuss Medussi

- 1x La Cucaracha

- or
- 2x Job Job Job Sahur.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Cuadramamat and Pakrahmatmamat is the second duo brainrot to include a brainrot not yet added, refering to the Cuadramat (Purple Book), the other brainrot was Los Planitos, including the not added yet brainrot "Los Bisontes". Both are Brainrot Trader Brainrots.

- Cuadramamat and Pakrahmatmamat is the least paying duo brainrot, above it being Chipso and Queso.
- This is also the cheapest duo brainrot in the game costing $400M, while other duo brainrots cost $1B or higher.

- The "Cuadramat" is actually derived from the Spanish word "Cuaderno", which when translated to English, means "Notebook".
- Since Pakrahmatmamat's name is derived from Pak Rahmat, a common Indonesian name for teacher, this made Cuadramamat and Pakrahmatmamat's name taken from both Spanish and Indonesian.

- Cuadramamat and Pakrahmatmamat was originally named "Pencook and Book".

- Cuadramamat and Pakrahmatmamat is the only Duo Brainrots which the members have different size from each other.

[133/519]
### Doi Doi Do
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Doi_Doi_Do
Avvisi: Brainrot Trader and Brainrot Dealer exclusive Brainrot
Non confondere con: Dul Dul Dul, Skull Skull Skull, Luv Luv Luv, Dug dug dug, Gold Gold Gold, Frogato Pirato, Frogo Elfo, or Fizzy Soda
Tagline: "Rain, rain, go away, come again another day..."
STATS: Rarita=Epic | Income=$260/s | Costo=$41K | Sounds=Doi_Doi_Doo.mp3,Frogito.mp3,DoiDoiDoiDaDaDoi.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Doi Doi Do is an Epic Brainrot that was added into the game on November 8th, 2025 at 3:00PM EST. It costs $41K and generates $260/s.

Doi Doi Do is a bipedal green frog wearing Indonesian school uniform for male, which is white shirt, red tie, and brown pants. Doi Doi Do can be seen wearing blue backpack and holding a wooden umbrella made out of wood and leaves.

Doi Doi Do is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From the Brainrot Dealer for  29.

- From the Brainrot Trader.
- Crafting Recipe:
- 4x Tric Trac Baraboom.

- or
- 2x Bambini Crostini.

- or
- 2x Tric Trac Baraboom.

- 1x Bambini Crostini.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Doi Doi Do was one of 10 Brainrots to release with the Brainrot Dealer.

- Doi Doi Do might be related to Dul Dul Dul as both are wearing similar uniforms and also both have similar names. It is also possible they go to the same school too.
- It might also be a reference to the popular sound "Doi Doi Doi" by Kai Cenat, and if that's the case, interestingly, Doi Doi Do doesn't have the last "i" on its name.

- This can also be found in the sound for this Brainrot in game.
--- DOI DOI DO ---
"Rain, rain, go away, come again another day..."

[135/519]
### Donkeyturbo Express
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Donkeyturbo_Express
Avvisi: Exclusive to the North Pole Event.
Tagline: rip this brainrots value sammy hit it with a bazooka
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$7.5M/s | Costo=$1.25B | Status=Obtainable (North Pole Event) | Ritual=No | Sounds=Donkey_Express.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Donkeyturbo Express is a Secret brainrot released with the Gingerbread Town. It costs $1.25B and generates $7.5M/s.

Donkeyturbo Express is an animal-vehicle hybrid brainrot. Its concept is about a donkey fused with a train. The train can be seen having colorful colors, such as a mix of green, yellow, and red mostly. The train also has red boots infront of it. It can be seen having the head of a donkey sticking out of it, with a grin and a christmas hat. He also kind of looks like Reinito Sleighito, but has a train as his body.

Donkeyturbo Express is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting it in the North Pole Event. One can instantly summon it if it's on stock with 1500 Candy Canes.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Donkeyturbo Express was mentioned in an announcement by SpyderSammy that said: "good luck finding the donkeyturbo express".

- Donkeyturbo Express is a reference to the Brainrot Express that carries player into the North Pole Event. Both are based on a Christmas movie titled The Polar Express.
--- DONKEYTURBO EXPRESS ---
rip this brainrots value sammy hit it with a bazooka

[136/519]
### Dragon Aquanini
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Dragon_Aquanini
Avvisi: stub, part_of_family
Famiglia: Dragon Family
Non confondere con: Dragon Cannelloni, Dragon Gingerini, Hydra Dragon Cannelloni, Ice Dragon, Arcadragon or Dragon Family
Tagline: when i go into water, i turn into the water!
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$375M/s | Costo=$375B | Status=Obtainable (Summer Fuse) | RarestMutation=Lava(3) | Ritual=No | Sounds=Dragon_aquanini.wav
--- OVERVIEW ---
Dragon Aquanini is a Brainrot that is obtained in the Summer Fuse.

Dragon Aquanini is a turquoise dragon with purple corals, starfishes, and barnacles adorning it. with yellowish spikes on head and nails on hands and feet.

Dragon Aquanini is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from Summer Fuse.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Dragon Aquanini is the only Dragon Cannelloni reskin that has a unique animation, it flaps it's wings as normal for around 10 seconds, then flips around several times, almost like it's swimming.
- Dragon Aquanini is also the only Dragon Cannelloni reskin to flip around.

- Dragon Aquanini is one of the few Aqua brainrots not to be included in the Aquatic Index.
- This is due to the fact that Dragon Aquanini was released after the Aquatic Index was removed.
--- DRAGON AQUANINI ---
when i go into water, i turn into the water!

[137/519]
### Dragon Cannelloni
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Dragon_Cannelloni
Avvisi: part_of_family
Famiglia: Dragon Family
Tagline: I WILL OVERCOME THE SECRETS WHO ARE BETTER THEN ME
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$250M/s | Costo=$250B | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | RarestMutation=Cyber(500) | RarestTrait=Fire(124) | Update=10 | Creator=@name2pictureai | Ritual=No | Sounds=DragonCannelloni_2.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Dragon Cannelloni is a dragon which is made out of pasta, Dragon Cannelloni also has hollowed part in the joints, which is filled with a red color, presumably Sauce, it has bits of orange on its wings and the side of its body, which is probably Cheese sauce, Dragon Cannelloni also has brown horns and claws, It also has white eyes with black pupils, It also has a fiery aura coming out of its wings and Mouth, Dragon Cannelloni also has a yellow-orange type color, it also breathes fire 

Dragon Cannelloni is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Dragon Cannelloni was buffed three times, from $100M/s, to $200M/s, and then finally reaching $250M/s,

- The name of original Italian Brainrot meme is Cannelloni Dragoni.

- Dragon Cannelloni cannot get hit with the fire trait if it spawns on the Red Carpet. This is because Dragon Cannelloni already has fire coming out of it. The only way to obtain Dragon Cannelloni with the fire trait was through the Cyber Craft, where in one admin abuse, he added limited stock to it. You can put brainrots with the fire trait, and will have a chance to get it.

- Dragon Cannelloni's old status has the same status as Cash or Card, La Casa Boo and Fragrama and Chocrama
--- DRAGON CANNELLONI ---
I WILL OVERCOME THE SECRETS WHO ARE BETTER THEN ME

Dragon Family are Brainrots based on dragons. All of them are Secret Brainrots, and are extremely hard to obtain.

Dragon Cannelloni, the first Dragon Family Brainrot, was made by TikTok user @name2pictureai. The rest of Dragon Family Brainrot are made by BRAZILIAN SPYDER, usually as reskin of Dragon Cannelloni, except for Caylusaurus which is made by Caylus.

### Dragon Gingerini
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Dragon_Gingerini
Avvisi: Santa's Fuse exclusive., part_of_family
Famiglia: Dragon Family
Non confondere con: Dragon Aquanini, Dragon Cannelloni, Hydra Dragon Cannelloni, Arcadragon, or its scrapped version Ice Dragon

--- OVERVIEW ---
Dragon Gingerini is a dragon made of gingerbread. It has White icing on the torso, Arms, legs, wings, the Side of it and the feet, Dragon Gingerini's torso has a yellow, green, blue, cyan, green, yellow and purple candy running down its torso, while the neck has, purple, yellow, green and blue candy running down both sides of the neck, The pasta leg holes are filled in with purple and yellow, it's Eyes are blue candy and it's horns and Claws are candy canes, it is similar to Dragon Cannelloni

Dragon Gingerini is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from Santa's Fuse.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Dragon Gingerini is teased as "Christmas Dragon", mentioned in the tease from Sammy as an announcement saying: "also next week we're adding the Christmas Dragon to the Fuse..."
- SpyderSammy made a poll to make people choose between it and Ice Dragon, but the majority preferred this one.

- Being a variant of Dragon Cannelloni, Dragon Gingerini makes $100M/s more and costs $100B more.

- Dragon Gingerini has the largest VFX in the game, taking up the whole space.

- This is the third best secret in the game
- Second being Dragon Aquanini and first being Griffin
--- DRAGON GINGERINI ---
if i eat myself. what would happen?

[140/519]
### Dug dug dug
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Dug_dug_dug
Avvisi: Craft Machine Exclusive.
Non confondere con: Dul Dul Dul, Luv Luv Luv, Skull Skull Skull, Gold Gold Gold, Duggy Bros or Sand Sand Sand
Tagline: In kids toys it’s called Doug
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$35M/s | Costo=$5B | Status=Unobtainable (Craft Machine) | RarestMutation=Bloodrot(6) | RarestTrait=Lightning(11) | Update=17 | Creator=@noxaasht | Ritual=No | Sounds=Dugdugdugdugsound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Dug dug dug takes the appearance of a drum/bedug being colored brown, with a creepy, realistic face that has inflated cheeks and a dead stare. Lastly, it has short legs with four-toed feet.

Dug dug dug is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From the Craft Machine.
- Crafting Recipe
- 3x Matteo

- 1x Extinct Ballerina

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Dug dug dug's name has non-capital initials, similar to To to to Sahur and the former Tralalita Tralala.

- Dug dug dug is an Indonesian Brainrot. It's inspiration is a "bedug", which reminds people that it's time to pray along with adhan.
- Due to this, Dug dug dug was classified as a Sahur, but this was only because media called it "Dug Dug Dug Sahur", which is completely different from Dug dug dug in the Italian Brainrot lore.

- Dug dug dug was released on September 20, 2025, which is the date when the La Cucaracha/Mexico Event was released. It is also released 1 week after Tung Tung Tung Sahur removal, despite both are made by @noxaasht.
- Dug dug dug is the last @noxaasht Brainrot that was added in the game.

- Dug dug dug received a buff in Update 42 that upgraded its income to $35M/s and changed its rarity to Secret. This is because it's crafting recipe requires Extinct Ballerina, which only obtainable from Extinct Event. While Dug dug dug and Extinct Event are held at the same time, it still requires an unobtainable Brainrot to craft it if you missed the Event.
- Prior to Update 42, this brainrot used to be a Brainrot God.

- Some people may find this brainrot creepy due to its unsettling appearance.
--- DUG DUG DUG ---
In kids toys it’s called Doug

### Duggy Bros
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Duggy_Bros

--- OVERVIEW ---
Duggy Bros currently makes $90M/s and costs $30B.

Duggy Bros appears as a baby version of Dug dug dug with blush on its face and cute, glowing eyes. A baby version of Gold Gold Gold can also be seen next to Dug dug dug, with cute, baby-like eyes. They are both baby-like versions that were never added, like Los Cupids.

Duggy Bros is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Cyber Craft Machine.
- Crafting Recipe
- 1x Dug dug dug

- 1x Gold Gold Gold

- Stealing, a Core Feature.

- SpyderSammy joked about it being canceled, then proceeded to leak it moments later.

- Unlike the original Gold Gold Gold, the baby counterpart has black iris in the eyes.

- One Bloodrot Duggy bros exist, which is owned by @노랸이, who is korean youtuber.

- This brainrot does not include Sand Sand Sand because Duggy Bros was released before Sand Sand Sand released.
- If Sand Sand Sand was included in Duggy Bros, it would likely be named Los Duggies, as it would be 3 brainrots instead of 2.
--- DUGGY BROS ---
Just the two of our balalaikas!

[142/519]
### Dul Dul Dul
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Dul_Dul_Dul
Avvisi: Admin Exclusive, also needed for a Ritual.
Non confondere con: Skull Skull Skull, Luv Luv Luv, Dug dug dug, Gold Gold Gold, Yess my examine, or Noo my examine
Tagline: guys i finally finished college, now i can get to work at a mcdonalds just to pay for rent :D
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$375K/s | Costo=$150M | Status=Obtainable (Admin Abuse) | Ritual=Yes | Sounds=Dulduldulsound.mp3,BaldMonkey.mp3
--- APPEARANCE ---
Dul Dul Dul appears as a smiling New World Monkey in Indonesian elementary school uniform, which is white shirt and red pants. It wears a brown belt, red tie, and a black, slightly tinted blue backpack. Unlike normal monkeys, Dul Dul Dul does not have a tail. 

Dul Dul Dul is/was obtained from the following ways:

- During Admin Abuse.

- From the Escape Tsunami LTM.

- From the Backrooms Event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Dul Dul Dul is an Indonesian Brainrot, and is based on the hairstyle "gundul" (bald). Its lore are based on hair check in Indonesian school, where a student with hair longer than the dress code has their hair cutted bald as form of humiliation.

- Dul Dul Dul and Guerriro Digitale are the only Brainrots to have a ritual that doesn’t spawn a Los version of itself.
- Dul Dul Dul Ritual and 1x1x1x1 Ritual Event (from Guerriro Digitale) is also the only ritual which the Brainrot result is dictated by set probability.

- Despite being a New World Monkey, Dul Dul Dul lacks a tail which is makes it technically an ape.

- The Dul Dul Dul in the ritual "speaks' if you approaching it. It seems to just be gibberish however.
--- DUL DUL DUL ---
guys i finally finished college, now i can get to work at a mcdonalds just to pay for rent :D

Signifiers | 

  |
--- RITUAL ---
- Dul Dul Dul has a ritual where if 4 players, each carrying Dul Dul Dul make a square formation at the start of the Red Carpet, the Dul Dul Dul will start building a graduation stand, with the words "BRAINROT SCHOOL" on it, triggering the start of the event.

- When the event starts, 3 of the Dul Dul Dul will walk away, while the last one will stay, and will give a speech. After that, a Yess my examine would spawn, or, with a lower chance, a Noo my examine. During the rest of the event, they would occasionally stop a brainrot from walking and graduate it, giving it the Red Tie trait.

[150/519]
### Elefanto Frigo
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Elefanto_Frigo
Avvisi: Exclusive to the Craft Machine.
Non confondere con: Frigo Camelo, Cocofanto Elefanto, Lirilì Larilà, or Strawberry Elephant
Tagline: Address the elephant in the room...
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$185M/s | Costo=$175B | Status=Unobtainable (Craft Machine) | RarestMutation=Bloodrot(1) | RarestTrait=Fireworks(1) | Update=17 | Creator=@alexey_pigeon | Ritual=No | Sounds=ElefantoFrigosound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Elefanto Frigo appears to be a light gray fridge with big and cute eyes, with a gray handle, a elephant trunk with a light gray and then gray color sequence with pair of tusk. Elefanto Frigo has two elephant ears with gray exterior and peach pink color interior, alongside some wine red lines. Elefanto Frigo also has two knees with the same color pattern as the trunk and two white feets.

Elefanto Frigo is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Crafting in the Craft Machine
- Crafting Recipe:
- 1x Tob Tobi Tobi

- 1x Frigo Camelo

- 2x Rhino Toasterino

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Elefanto Frigo was confirmed in Roblox/Discord along with Dug dug dug.

- At the time of Elefanto Frigo's debut, barely anyone has this brainrot, because it required Tob Tobi Tobi, which almost nobody had back then since Tob Tobi Tobi being considered bad in income.
- Tob Tobi Tobi was also a rare Mythic Fuse Machine exclusive, making it even harder to obtain. Furthermore, since Craft Machine was introduced after Fuse Machine, there's no way to obtain new Tob Tobi Tobi for crafting Elefanto Frigo.

- Crafting Elefanto Frigo was also considered not worth it, since the comparison between its income and its material income are $-600/s.

- As such, there's only 705 existing Elefanto Frigo. Out of them, there's only 18 Elefanto Frigos in the world with the Yin Yang Mutation, and only 1 Elefanto Frigo in the entire world that has a Bloodrot Mutation with it belonging to RbxJaye

- In the original meme, it is named Elefantino Frigorifero, although due to unknown reasons it is renamed in-game.

- Elefanto Frigo has been buffed 2 times, from $14K/s to $85M/s, and from $85M/s to $185M/s.
- This makes Elefanto Frigo go from the worst brainrot that starts with the letter "E" to the best brainrot that starts with the letter "E". Now, the worst brainrot that starts with the letter "E" is Espresso Signora.

- Elefanto Frigo design is inspired by a riddle "How to put an elephant in a fridge?".

- Elefanto Frigo is one of five buffed brainrots on Update 40.

- This Brainrot has the same stats as Hydra Bunny.
--- ELEFANTO FRIGO ---
Address the elephant in the room...

[152/519]
### Esok Sekolah
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Esok_Sekolah
Avvisi: Exclusive to a Lucky Block. (Secret Lucky Block)
Non confondere con: La Casa Boo, La Ginger Sekolah, or Los Sekolahs
Tagline: 9999999999
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$30M/s | Costo=$3.5B | Status=Obtainable (Secret Lucky Block) | RarestMutation=Bloodrot(1889) | Ritual=No | Sounds=EsokSekolah.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Esok Sekolah is a Secret Brainrot that produces $30M/s and costs $3.5B.

Esok Sekolah is a humanoid schoolhouse with limbs and a face, with its tongue sticking out and saliva dripping off of it. The number on the schoolhouse reads '9' and has a sign that says the same number. It produces fire particles and has a steeple with bell on top of the roof.

Esok Sekolah is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Secret Lucky Block with a 3% chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Esok Sekolah is Indonesian for "School Tomorrow". It's original name is "La Esok Sekolah", with the La being omitted. Interestingly, it's counterpart, La Casa Boo and La Ginger Sekolah, maintain the "La" in it.
- The "La" in its full name is meant to be "Lah", Indonesian word for surprise expression, making the translation of the full name is "No Way, School is Tomorrow".

- The "9" number in Top of Esok Sekolah is meaning for 9 April, which is Back to School Day in Indonesia.

- Esok Sekolah actually has a Walking animation, despite in never being seen in game since it comes out of a Secret Lucky Block.
- This also applies to any other brainrot that comes out of a Lucky Block.

- The only way of seeing the animation is if an admin spawns it on the Red Carpet, which has happened during an Admin Abuse (January 1st, 2026), along with other brainrots like 67.

- Esok Sekolah chance to getting it before was 5% before Spaghetti Tualetti released.
--- ESOK SEKOLAH ---
9999999999

- Espresso Signora's name meaning "Lady Espresso". The name is meant to be a contrast with her counterpart, Ballerina Cappuccina, which is portrayed as young and based after cappuccino, an extract made by 1/3 espresso, 1/3 milk foam, and 1/3 steamed milk.

### Eviledon
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Eviledon
Avvisi: Witch Fuse Exclusive.
Non confondere con: Zombie Tralala, Orcaledon or Tralaledon
Tagline: Tralaledon But EVIL!!! lol maybe it the same

- Getting from the Fishing event.

### Fishino Clownino

Tagline: let the show begin 😀

--- OVERVIEW ---
Fishino Clownino has the appearance of a clownfish riding a unicycle, similarly to Tictac Sahur and Gobblino Uniciclino. It also shows resemblance to an actual clown, similarly to Cappuccino Clownino.

Fishino Clownino is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Fishing from the Fishing Event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Fishino Clownino is one of the only brainrots riding a unicycle, besides Tictac Sahur and Gobblino Uniciclino.

- Fishino Clownino is apart of the Aquatic Brainrots' family.

- Fishino Clownino is one of the only brainrots whos audio says the wrong thing, the other example being La Extinct Grande and Vulturino Skeletono.
- The audio of Fishino Clownino in-game says "Fishito Clownito" instead of its actual name, "Fishino Clownino".

- Fishino Clownino was buffed due to how rare it was after 5,129 of it was revealed to be exist. Initially it was a belated addition to the Fishing Event as a rare catch, but not as rare as Tralaledon, Eviledon, Los Primos, Orcaledon, and Capitano Moby.

- Fishino Clownino was the worst Fishing-exclusive brainrot when it was introduced. After the buff, Fishino Clownino is the second-best Fishing-exclusive brainrot, below Capitano Moby.
- Due to it can only be obtained from Fishing, Fishino Clownino is more valuable and has a higher demand than Capitano Moby, since Capitano Moby can also obtained as Red Carpet spawn aside from Fishing.

- It is required to craft Digi Narwhal in the Cyber Craft Machine along with Capitano Moby.

- Sammy did the Fishing Event on Update 53 when the Phantom mutation was introduced. A Fishino Clownino would be extremely rare if it had this mutation. Due to this, alongside Fishing Event seems to have returned in major Admin Abuse like Taco Tuesday in Update 51, and fact of many Fishino Clownino are used for Digi Narwhal recipe, the initial 5,129 Fishino Clownino exist count was inaccurate.

let the show begin 😀

### Foxini Lanternini

--- OVERVIEW ---
Foxini Lanternini is a limited time Brainrot meant to celebrate the end of Ramadan and starting the Eid Celebrations.

Foxini Lanternini is a Brainrot resembling a nine-tail fox AKA Kitsune. 6 lanterns can be seen floating around Foxini Lanternini, along with a blue scarf with a golden crescent symbol, a popular iconography of Eid.

Foxini Lanternini is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Spawning during the Eid Event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Foxini Lanternini is one of the two Brainrots obtainable in the Eid Event, the other being Eid Eid Eid Sahur.

- Foxini Lanternini is the first Fox Brainrot added into the game.

- Foxini Lanternini is based on the mythological creature named "Kitsune". Interestingly, Kitsune is a Japanese mythological creature, while Eid Event is based on Eid al-Fitr, an Islamic festival rooted in Arabic/Indonesian culture.

- Since the Eid Event that spawned Eid Event Exclusive Brainrot was only done three times, this made Foxini Lanternini extremely rare.

- Foxini Lanternini is pronounced as "Foxini Lanterini" in the voice. This makes Foxini Lanternini one of the few Brainrots in the game with a mispronounced name, with the others being Fishino Clownino, La Extinct Grande, Vulturino Skeletono, and Brutto Gialutto.

- Sammy leaked during an Admin Abuse that only 25,000 exist, making it very rare.
--- FOXINI LANTERNINI ---

### Fragrama and Chocrama
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Fragrama_and_Chocrama
Avvisi: Exclusive to the Brainrot Dealer and Brainrot Trader.
Non confondere con: Fragola La La La or other Duo Brainrots
Tagline: "Fragrama is literally worth an elephant and adds" -coolSABdad
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$100M/s | Costo=$40B | Status=Unobtainable (Brainrot Trader) | RarestMutation=Lava(56) | RarestTrait=Indonesia(969) | Update=24 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Ritual=No | Sounds=Fragrama_and_Chocramaa.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Fragrama and Chocrama is a Secret Brainrot from the Brainrot Trader, producing $100M/s and costing $40B. It's an expy of Garama and Madundung.

Fragrama has a light pink milkshake body, a strawberry on top, a red straw, white whipped cream, and a smiling face with blue eyes and pinkish lips.

Chocrama has a light brown milkshake body, chocolate sprinkles and a wafer stick on top, darker eyebrows, and a wide grin.

Fragrama and Chocrama is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Brainrot Dealer.

- Trading for it in the Brainrot Trader.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Fragrama and Chocrama give the same amount of money as Dragon Cannelloni's original income before the buff that made Dragon Cannelloni's income increase to $250M/s.

- Fragrama also has a meme based off of it. During a Livestream a content creator known as coolSABdad claimed it was worth an elephant and adds.

- Fragrama and Chocrama is named after Fragola (Italian for strawberry), Fragrance, Chocolate, and Garama.

Frigo Camelo is a Mythic Brainrot which generates $2K/s (formerly $1.9K/s and $1.4K/s) and costs $350K.

Frigo Camelo takes the appearance of a two compartment fridge and camel hybrid. Their brown neck and head sprout out of the front of the fridge compartment part, while two legs extend from bottom, each wearing brown shoes.

Frigo Camelo is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Frigo Camelo is required for Rebirth 5, alongside Orangutini Ananassini.

- Frigo Camelo, like Talpa Di Fero, had an old sound that was for some reason removed. The voice had more enthusiasm and it was lost, but it has recently been found inside legacy game files. Alongside that, Frigo Camelo used to have different walking animation.
- The old voice and old walking animation was changed to the new one in the Gattatino Nyanino update.

- Frigo Camelo was buffed from $1.4K/s to $1.9K/s due Sigma Girl's addition and the need for more room for Legendaries as there were too many brainrots generating $1K/s - 1.4K/s.
- When Seraphino Gruyero was added and generating the same income which is $1.9K/s, Frigo Camelo was buffed to $2K/s.

[180/519]
### Garama and Madundung
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Garama_and_Madundung
Tagline: The Underappreciated Club: Banned for being TOO ULTIMATELY GLAZED!!
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$50M/s | Costo=$10B | Status=Obtainable | Update=06 | Creator=@noxaasht | Ritual=No | Sounds=Garama_and_Madundung_Sound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Garama and Madundung is a Secret brainrot released on July 5, 2025. It costs $10B and has a base income of $50M/s. 

Garama and Madundung are together a salt shaker and a honey container with a cloth on top. They each have eyes, a mouth, and nose with mustache, both customary to their colors. They have hairy legs and emit an aura of salt for Garama and honey for Madundung.

Garama and Madundung is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- When Sammy spawns them in quantities during Admin Abuse.

- Obtaining it in the Escape Tsunami LTM, which is no longer available.

- Trading for it.

- From Sammy's Base with a low chance.
--- TRIVIA ---
- "Garam" means salt in indonesian and "Madu" means honey, which is how the name Garama and Madundung was formed.

- Being in the La Supreme Combinasion, Garama and Madundung used to make more money than La Supreme Combinasion. However, with La Supreme Combinasion is getting buffed to $200M/s, Garama and Madundung now makes less than La Supreme Combinasion.

- Garama and Madundung are the first Duo Brainrots in-game.

- Garama and Madundung used to be the highest paying brainrot in the game, completely surpassing La Grande Combinasion, the former highest paying brainrot with $40M/s difference, before the Dragon Cannelloni was released.

- Its original name was “Garamararamraramanmararaman dan Madudungdungdung Tak Tuntung Perkuntung”, but it was truncated to simply "Garama and Madundung" since the name is too long.

- Garama and Madundung and Nuclearo Dinossauro have the same chance of spawning on the Red Carpet (They both have a RoadWeight of 1.00E-10, or 1 in 10,000,000,000), even though Nuclearo Dinossauro makes $35M/s less than Garama and Madundung.
- This meant despite Garama and Madundung costs and makes more than Tang Tang Keletang, Ketupat Kepat, Tictac Sahur, Ketchuru and Musturu, and Lavadorito Spinito, their RoadWeights are lower than Garama and Madundung, which later on meant SpyderSammy had to nerf it due to overpopulation.

- Due to this, on 3/17/26 Taco Tuesday, SpyderSammy made a poll if Garama and Madundung should be nerfed, and 2.2M people voted for yes so it was supposed to be nerfed next update. But then on 3/21/26, Sammy ran a new poll due to lots of backlash, yet people still voted in favor of nerfing it.
- Despite the Garama and Madundung nerf not happening at all, people treat it as if it's already been nerfed, making it lose demand for few weeks after the announcement.

- As of July 5th 2026, Garama and Madundung is 1 year old
--- GARAMA AND MADUNDUNG ---
The Underappreciated Club: Banned for being TOO ULTIMATELY GLAZED!!

- its was back but with a new look as a admin abuse exculise

- It can be considered "Neon Cat" instead of "Nyan Cat".

[183/519]
### Gattatino Nyanino
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Gattatino_Nyanino
Non confondere con: Gattatino Neonino, Gattito Tacoto, Los Gattitos, Mi Gatito, or Los Mi Gatitos
Tagline: An image of Gattatino Nyanino
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$35K/s | Costo=$7.5M | Status=Obtainable (Admin Abuse, Backrooms Event) | Ritual=No | Sounds=Nyam_Cat_Sound.wav
--- OVERVIEW ---
Gattatino Nyanino is a Brainrot God that produces $35K/s and costs $7.5M.

Gattatino Nyanino appears to be a remodel of the famous internet meme, Nyan Cat. who is a Russian Blue cat hybrid with a cherry flavoured Pop-Tart as a torso.

Gattatino Nyanino is/was obtained from the following ways:

- SpyderSammy spawning this brainrot on the Red Carpet.

- From the Backrooms Event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Gattatino Nyanino was replaced Gattatino Neonino due to unauthorized usage of Nyan Cat. Gattatino Neonino was later removed and Gattatino Nyanino was re-added after Sammy got permission to add it from Nyan Cat's creator, Christopher Torres.
- Christopher Torres is credited in Steal a Brainrot's description, "🙏 Credit to Chris for letting us use the Nyan Cat!".

- Gattatino Nyanino got buffed from $25K/s to $35K/s.

- Gattatino Nyanino's inspiration, Nyan Cat was made on April 2, 2011 during a charity art drive to help Japan after the Tōhoku earthquake.[1] It started as a pixel cat flying through space and quickly went viral, inspiring tons of fan art, remixes, and parodies.

- Gattatino Nyanino was originally bigger, but it was shrunken when it was re-added because people were performing a glitch where this Brainrot could be stolen through the left and right walls of the Base. The same thing were also happened with Unclito Samito.

- Even though Gattatino Nyanino is older than Meowl with the Nyan Cat meme made in 2011 while Meowl was made in 2013, this brainrot for some reason is not considered an OG, making many people argue that it should.
- The OG rarity wasn't a thing when this brainrot was added, so that might be the reason as to why it is a Brainrot God.

- Unlike most brainrots that have more fluid animations, Gattatino Nyanino has a very rigid and rough animation, likely mimicking that of the original meme.
--- GATTATINO NYANINO ---
An image of Gattatino Nyanino

### Ginger Gerat
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Ginger_Gerat
Avvisi: Machine Brainrot; Part of a Seasonal Event.
Non confondere con: Ginger Cisterna, Ginger Globo, La Ginger Sekolah, Ketupat Kepat, Cloverat Clapat, or Ketupat Bros
Tagline: you cant catch me! Im the gingerbread man!
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$75M/s | Costo=$22.5B | Sounds=GingerGerataSound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Ginger Gerat was an awaited Brainrot by the community since Update 28. They cost $22.5B and produce $75M/s.

Ginger Gerat appears to be a anthropomorphic gingerbread shaped like an Indonesian ketupat. Its mouth appears to have been painted with red frosting and its 2 eyes have pink pupils and pink eyebrows. Its buttons are also pink, and in its walking animation. Unlike Ketupat Kepat, it is seen running instead of walking.

Ginger Gerat is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Purchasing from Santa's Shop for  100 Gold Elves or  9,999.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- One hour before the Santa Fuse Update, there was an empty slot for Ginger Gerat in the index. This happened because its stats had already been added to the Datas/Animals module script — an income of $40M/s and a cost of $7B like Orcaledon, Swaggy Bros, and La Romantic Grande — before it was removed a few hours later due to admin abuse. Its old original name was Gingerat Gerat.

- Ginger Gerat is based of the many stories about a Gingerbread Man running away, which is possibly why its "Walking Animation" is running.

- You can use Ginger Gerat to fuse Ketupat Bros for a 50% chance in 2026 Fuse Machine, and you can add Ketupat Kepat to make the chance become 100%.

- Despite making less than Dragon Cannelloni, Ginger Gerat's value is as worth as Dragon Cannelloni, likely because it required 100, making it rare.
- Ginger Gerat costs 2 times more than Jolly Jolly Sahur, yet only makes 1.5 times more than the Jolly Jolly Sahur.

- In real USD, Ginger Gerat would cost $100 to obtain from Santa's Shop since the amount of Robux required for it costs $100.

- Ginger Gerat’s exist count was thought to be ~500 because of Ketupat Bros the exist count has been revealed to be 8.3k instead of 500.
--- GINGER GERAT ---
you cant catch me! Im the gingerbread man!

--- OVERVIEW ---
GOAT is a Secret brainrot that was added on January 17, 2026 at 3:00 PM EST. He cost $235.5M and had an income of $900K/s before the buff. He currently generates $950K/s and costed $237.6M. 

GOAT is depicted as an anthropomorphic goat, as its name explains it. It can be seen having green pupils, along with yellowish-like hair. It can be seen wearing a green and red tanktop, along with green and red pants accompanied by tennie shoes. GOAT can be seen juggling/dribbling a basketball.

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.

- GOAT is based off "Will Harris" from the movie film called "Goat", directed by Tyree Dillihay and produced by Sony Pictures Animation.
- It's also based off of the famous basketball player, Stephen Curry.

- GOAT itself is a collaboration Brainrot between Steal a Brainrot and Sony Pictures Animation to promote the said movie, which were then-coming soon when GOAT was added.

- The term "GOAT" (or G.O.A.T.) stands for "Greatest Of All Time," which is often credited to having originated from the mid-20th century boxer Muhammad Ali.[1]

- GOAT is the first Brainrot who's name is written in all capitals.

- Between January 17th and January 31th 2026, GOAT could be obtained for the red carpet with a RoadWeight (or odds) of 3.00E-06 (0.000003).

### Gorillo Subwoofero
