--- OVERVIEW ---
Gorillo Subwoofero is a Mythic Brainrot which was added on September 6th, 2025, in the Craft Machine update, that costs $2.7M and generates $7.7K/s.

Gorillo Subwoofero is a black gorilla with car subwoofers adorning its body.

Gorillo Subwoofero is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From the Craft Machine.
- Crafting Recipe
- 2x Spioniro Golubiro

- 2x Orangutini Ananassini

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Considering SpyderSammy leaked exist counts for Gorillo Subwoofero on July 7, 2026, it is resumed that this brainrot has a total of 16.348 exists, making it the 1st rarest Mythic brainrot in the game, with 2nd being Orbi Mochi, and 3rd being Centrucci Nuclucci.

- Gorillo Subwoofero's exist count also suggests a likely buff to this brainrot, due to the buff applied to Dug dug dug on Update Log/Update 42, buffing it to making $255K/s to $35M/s. It can be tought of a possible upgrade for Gorillo Subwoofero, since it haves almost half of the exists that Dug dug dug has (29,288), hinting that it might be buffed too, maybe around $60-70M/s.

- Gorillo Subwoofero is another craft exclusive brainrot like Fragola La La La and Rhino Helicopterino that have a low exist count beacuse of no one really wanting to crafting it. The causes are inferior demand, or probably the low money per second and the minimum profit (or negative) gained from the craft.

- In the image it is based on, It can be seen that in the bottom right there's Google Gemini's symbol, meaning it was made using Gemini for making the brainrot in first place. Same thing is for Signore Carapace.

- Altough in-game it's called "Gorillo Subwoofero", the original video pronounces it as "GorillONE Subwoofero", forming a doubt whether gorillo or gorillone is the right name.

### Graipuss Medussi
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Graipuss_Medussi
Tagline: somehow makes less than the brainrots used in the rebirth before?
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$1M/s | Costo=$250M | Status=Obtainable Red Carpet | Sounds=Graipusmedusi.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Graipuss Medussi is a Secret brainrot that was added on 6/14/25. It costs $250M and has an income of $1M/s

Graipuss Medussi appears as a purple jellyfish with a grape as its body. Unlike its origin, it has a face and eyes and is slightly smiling. However, its alternate variant, as shown in the Italian Brainrot Wiki, also has a face.

Graipuss Medussi is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Rolling it out from the Fishing event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Graipuss Medussi is based off of Graipussi Medussi. The name was changed because of sexual slang that can be found in its name, which is a characteristic of some @alexey_pigeon Brainrots.
- In the original meme, Graipuss Medussi doesn’t have a face.

- Graipuss Medussi is a brainrot that is required in the Aquatic Index, meaning it can be obtained via Fishing.

- You need Graipuss Medussi for Rebirth 18.

- This brainrot has the same stats and income as Bombardiro Vaccariro.
--- GRAIPUSS MEDUSSI ---
somehow makes less than the brainrots used in the rebirth before?

[207/519]
### Guest 666
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Guest_666
Avvisi: Ritual Exclusive.
Non confondere con: 1x1x1x1, John Doe, or Los Hackers
Tagline: Exactly the 666th guest on Roblox before the removal.
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$66.6M/s | Costo=$15.6B | Status=Obtainable | RarestMutation=Phantom(2) | RarestTrait=Nyan(789) | Update=23 | Creator=ObliviousHD | Ritual=Yes | Sounds=Guest_667.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Guest 666 is a dark figure that has red horns with a glowing face and a wide grin alongside angry eyes. It has a ROBLOX cap on its head. It also has the old ROBLOX logo on its body while wielding 2 blood-red swords with black handles. The actual Guest 666 Roblox avatar did not have a sword or glowing eyes.

Guest 666 is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Guerriro Digitale ritual with a 0.5% chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Guest 666 is based on the iconic Roblox myth of the same name that gained fame through its rumoured frequent disruptions and hacking of Roblox games, as well as being featured in a popular YouTube animated series made by 0bliviousHD.
- The myth said that Guest 666 had admin powers in any game it joined, also having the ability to chat (something regular Guests couldn't do).

- Guest 666, 1x1x1x1 and John Doe were in the game Forsaken, before being added to Steal a Brainrot. But it's not from Forsaken, but instead an iconic myth.
- This led to controversy among the Steal a Brainrot community, with Forsaken players saying that Sammy copied Forsaken. This is false as Guest 666, 1x1x1x1 and John Doe were BOTH made before Forsaken and Steal a Brainrot were released. Sammy was simply catering to old Roblox.

- The income of Guest 666 in all his mutations when expanded gives the last number repeated 6 times.

- The number '666' in Guest 666's name and its income, $66.6M/s is a reference of Number of the Beast. This also explained why Guest 666 has a horns in his model, different from its source material.
- This makes Guest 666 as the first character with a reference to hell, with the 2nd one being Cerberus.
--- GUEST 666 ---
Exactly the 666th guest on Roblox before the removal.

[210/519]
### Headless Horseman
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Headless_Horseman
Avvisi: Witch Fuse got removed.
Tagline: my head hurts :(
STATS: Rarita=OG | Income=$600M/s | Costo=$600B | Status=Unobtainable (Witch Fuse) | RarestMutation=Yin Yang(2) | RarestTrait=Indonesia(17) | Update=22 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER + Roblox: Headless Horseman Package | Ritual=No | Sounds=Headless_Horseman_Voice.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Headless Horseman appears as a horseman centaur who, as the name suggests, has no head. The horseman is holding what seems to be a Jack-o-Lantern with a wicked smile; it looks eerily similar to the Pumpkin trait.

Headless Horseman comes from a Halloween story hundreds of years ago, titled "The Legend of Sleepy Hollow" by Washington Irving.

Headless Horseman is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Fusing for it in the Witch Fuse

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Headless Horseman originates from the short story "The Legend of Sleepy Hollow", written by Washington Irving back in 1820, making it technically an OG. It wasn't until Update 40 that Headless Horseman became an OG Brainrot.
- Headless Horseman is also based on the Headless Horseman bundle.

- Headless Horseman is the first OG brainrot to be unobtainable AND the first OG Brainrot not to have its own event. Headless Horseman instead was a Witch Fuse Brainrot, being the best Brainrot from it.
- Even with the best Secrets in the game (when it was obtainable and still a Secret), you would've still only had a 9% max chance to get Headless Horseman.

- Due to this, Headless Horseman is the first OG to not have its own event/trait or spawn animation.

- Headless Horseman was buffed 6 times; in the Gingerbread Town update (December 20, 2025) from $175M/s to $200M/s, in The Return (January 24, 2026) update from $200M/s to $325M/s, in Trade Machine update (February 21, 2025) from $325M/s to $375M/s, in the Divine Admin Machine update (February 28, 2026) to $500M/s, in the Divine Fuse machine update (March 7, 2026) to $550M/s, in the Anniversary Update (May 23, 2026) to $600M/s.

- Sammy leaked that only 75 Headless Horsemen exist, making it the 2nd rarest brainrot in the game, below the Spyder Elephant ($1B/s).
- There is 1 Divine, 2 Yin Yang, 9 Lava, 22 Gold, and 12 Diamond Headless Horsemen, the rest of the Headless Horsemen do not have mutations.
- This means that there are no Bloodrot, Candy, Galaxy, Radioactive, Cursed, Cyber, Phantom or Rainbow Headless Horsemen that exist.

- A French YouTuber named Unchained (aka LeFrenchTacos) has one of the only 2 Yin Yang Headless Horsemen. The second one is owned by Kooda.

- Headless Horseman is currently the only Secret to increase in rarity, now being an OG.

- In Update 40, Headless Horseman got its own Base skin, in similar tradition to other OG.

- During the Summer Update Admin Abuse, SpyderSammy said there was not 138 Headless Horsemen, but it was actually under 100 in existence. Then in Taco Tuesday; SpyderSammy said there are about 75 in existence. Not 138.

[212/519]
### Ho Ho Ho Sahur
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Ho_Ho_Ho_Sahur
Avvisi: stub, Santa's Fuse Exclusive.
Non confondere con: Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur, Ti Ti Ti Sahur, Te Te Te Sahur, To to to Sahur, Cupid Cupid Sahur, Los Cupids, or Ref Ref Ref Sahur
Tagline: Ho ho ho ho ho
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$3.2M/s | Costo=$725M | Status=Unobtainable | RarestMutation=Cyber(5) | Sounds=Ohohohosahur.ogg
--- OVERVIEW ---
Ho Ho Ho Sahur is a Secret Brainrot that was added along with the Santa's Fuse on December 6, 2025. It was added as the second most common Secret in it, being above La Vacca Prese Presente and below Chicleteira Noelteira. It has a cost of $725M and a base income of $3.2M/s.

Ho Ho Ho Sahur appears to be a humanoid metal pole with neutral face akin to To to to Sahur except it now resembling Santa Claus, complete with Santa's hat, beard, and clothes. Its metal pole is now resembling walking cane.

Ho Ho Ho Sahur is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Fusing it in the Santa's Fuse.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- While Los Combinasionas from Fuse Machine has $15M/s income and Los Mobilis from Witch Fuse has $22M/s, Ho Ho Ho Sahur only has $3.25M/s income, despite all of them are Tier II Secret in their respective Fuse Machine. This is because Ho Ho Ho Sahur was introduced after the game offered many ways to obtain Secret Brainrots, which led to easier creations of Tier II Secret and could potentially break the game's economy.

- Ho Ho Ho Sahur actually makes $3.25M/s, but the game doesn't show the second decimal.

- Unlike its original version, To to to Sahur, all of Ho Ho Ho Sahur's name are capitalized.
--- HO HO HO SAHUR ---
Ho ho ho ho ho

### Horegini Boom

Avvisi: stub, Indonesia event

STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$2.75M/s | Costo=$650M | Status=Obtainable (Admin Abuse) | Sounds=HoreginiBoomsound.mp3
--- TRIVIA ---
- 

- Horegini Boom is based on a culture in Indonesia called Sound Horeg. A Sound Horeg refer to a car-carrier that carries massive sound system speakers and playing music across the road, usually playing bass boosted remix of a song. While Sound Horeg is appreciated by many people as source of free entertainment, it has been criticized as a sound pollution, since the music that played is often too loud.
- The similar culture also appeared in Brazil in form of Paredão de Som, which usually playing funk automotivo genre.

- It has the same Cost and Income as Buho de Volto.

Brainrot Wave!!!

He appears as a Cream‑YeIIow, BIocky RobIox Avatar with a YeIIow torso and BIue Jeans. His right arm is heaviIy corrupted, whiIe his Ieft arm is Corrupted and ends in cIaws. His right eye and feet also show Moderate Corruption.

John Doe is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From the 1x1x1x1 Ritual Event with 5% chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
This section is a trivia section. Please relocate any relevant information into other sections of the article.

- John Doe is based off a old Testing Account made in February 2006 by Roblox admins. Around February 2017, a rumor had spread around saying that John Doe would hack People on March 18th every year.
- The ModeI of John Doe in Steal A Brainrot is Copied by Forsaken rendition of John Doe.

- John Doe has a 5% chance to spawn in the 1x1x1x1 Ritual.

- John Doe has the same walk animation as Noobini Santanini.

[227/519]
### John Pork
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/John_Pork
Tagline: John Pork is Calling...
STATS: Rarita=OG | Income=$500M/s | Costo=$500B | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | RarestMutation=Cyber(1) | RarestTrait=Spider(1) | Update=49 | Creator=@john.pork | Ritual=No | Sounds=John_PorkSound.mp3,John_Pork_Spawn_Effect_Sound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
John Pork has a base income of $500M/s and costs $500B, being the 2nd least-generating OG brainrot.

John Pork is an anthropomorphic Pig with a human-like face with blue pupils and a smile. It wears a red flannel with a gray shirt underneath, along with blue jeans and gray shoes, while it holds a phone in its hand.

John Pork is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
This section is a trivia section. Please relocate any relevant information into other sections of the article.

- John Pork is a viral internet meme character known for having a human body and the head of a pig.

- John Pork was previously hinted by SpyderSammy in an Admin Abuse, where, in the global announcements, he posted a pig emoji.
- John Pork was confirmed to be upcoming with an update announcement released by the BRAZILIAN SPYDER team, on 4/25/2026.

- John Pork was originally created in 2018 by the Instagram handle @john.pork. John Pork was added in Steal a Brainrot after the Instagram handle @john.pork gave BRAZILIAN SPYDER permit to adding him in the game.

- John Pork is the first OG brainrot to be added on an odd-numbered month (May), since Strawberry Elephant was first added on August, Meowl was added on October, and Skibidi Toilet was added on December. August, October, and December are even-numbered month.

- John Pork is the newest OG after 4 months, if you're not counting Headless Horseman which was buffed from a Secret to an OG.

- John Pork's Trait is the first and only Trait in the game that changes the name of Brainrot applied to it. Any Brainrots that got this Trait has its name displayed as "(Brainrot name) is Calling..." Example : (Tim Cheese) is Calling..."

- The first ever John Pork spawned was a Gold variant.

- John Pork's spawning sound and trait biome sound is similar to an old phone's ringtone. This is due to John Pork being originated from a meme where he is making a mock-up call.

- This is the second lowest-tier OG.

- He became especially popular through memes showing him calling people on their phones, often with the caption: "John Pork is calling."

- The character originally appeared on Instagram before spreading across TikTok, YouTube, and other social media platforms.

- Many memes joke that ignoring a call from John Pork leads to mysterious or funny consequences.

- His strange mix of realism and absurdity is a big reason why the meme became so popular.

- John Pork is often associated with surreal humor, a style of comedy that became very popular online in the early 2020s.

- Despite the many stories and theories about him, John Pork is a fictional character and not a real person.

- The meme inspired fan art, edits, animations, and even fictional lore created by internet users.

- A limited stock code - JOHNPORKDAPIGGY - was given out during Admin Abuse, which was a code with a limited stock that spawned a John Pork for anyone who redeemed it before it sold out.
--- JOHN PORK ---
John Pork is Calling...

[232/519]
### Karkerkar Kurkur
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Karkerkar_Kurkur
Avvisi: Admin Abuse exclusive
Non confondere con: La Karkerkar Combinasion, Karker Sahur, Chachechi, Trickolino, Please my Present, Karkerheart Luvkur, Los Karkeritos, or Clovkur Kurkur
Tagline: motivated chair
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$325K/s | Costo=$80M | Status=Obtainable | Sounds=Karkekar_Kurkur_Sound.wav,Kurkurk.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Karkerkar Kurkur is a Secret Brainrot. It costs $80M and generates $325K/s.

Karkerkar Kurkur is an aqua green chair with hands, legs, and large feet. It has big eyes with a slightly open mouth along with a nose. It has very-hard-to-see moving eyebrows that are more visible when it has a mutation.

Karkerkar Kurkur is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtaining it through Admin Abuse.

- Getting it from Backrooms Event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Karkerkar Kurkur is one of the few Brainrots that have a special path animation when spawning.

- Karkerkar Kurkur has a ritual where you can spawn Los Karkeritos by using 4 of these brainrots to start a musical chairs game.
- This is also the first brainrot to have itself an entire minigame for the ritual, and the one that doesn't summon a special biome. However, this ritual is currently broken.

- Karkerkar Kurkur is one of the only brainrots to have eyes shaped like ones from a human, with the others are Rang Ring Bus and Te Te Te Sahur. All of them are Indonesian Brainrots.

- If you look closely, the only thing that is moving in Karkerkar Kurkur are its eyebrows.
--- KARKERKAR KURKUR ---
motivated chair

### Krupuk Pagi Pagi
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Krupuk_Pagi_Pagi
Avvisi: stub, Indonesia Event
Tagline: You won't get any of my pollock roe crackers even if you beg!
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$290K/s | Costo=$60M | Status=Obtainable (Aura Farm Boat) | Update=21 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Sounds=Krupuk_PagiPagi.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Krupuk Pagi Pagi is a Brainrot God rarity Brainrot that can be obtained from the Aura Farm Boat, which spawns when the Indonesian Event is activated.

Krupuk Pagi Pagi is a Krupuk (deep fried cracker), specifically Krupuk Ikan (fish cracker) that is drinking tea or coffee in a white mug.

Once the Indonesia Event starts, it may spawn on the Aura Farm Boat, letting you take it. It has an NPC version driving/dancing the boat, and it can spawn on the boat too.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Krupuk Pagi Pagi name is roughly translated to “Morning Cracker Cracker”. This refers to Indonesian people routine of eating cracker and drinking tea or coffee in the morning before starting activity.
- Since Krupuk is an Indonesian dish, many players who are unaware as to what food Krupuk Pagi Pagi is supposed to be think that he's a pancake.
--- KRUPUK PAGI PAGI ---
You won't get any of my pollock roe crackers even if you beg!

### La Anniversary Grande

--- OVERVIEW ---
La Anniversary Grande appears as a fusion of multiple Brainrots:

- Lirilì Larilà's head colored to be a cake, with whipped cream and a cherry on its head.

- Trippi Troppi's legs, sprouted in front of Tung Tung Tung Sahur's torso and Lirilì Larilà's side body.

- Boneca Ambalabu's tire, which is colored red (likely resembling red velvet cake) and head in a cake form with a blue and pink party hat.

- Tralalero Tralala, which now colored pink with a pink candle on its head, similar to Tralalita Tralala.

- Tung Tung Tung Sahur, who is wearing a pink suit and holding his iconic bat.

La Anniversary Grande is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From the Taco Truck.
- Crafting Recipe
- 1x La Grande Combinasion

- 1x Lavadorito Spinito

- 1x 1x1x1x1

- Stealing, a Core Feature.

- La Anniversary Grande is the first Limited Quantity Brainrots and La Grande Combinasion reskin to be released after Tung Tung Tung Sahur's 2nd removal.

- La Anniversary Grande is the first Limited Quantity Brainrots to include Lavadorito Spinito and 1x1x1x1 as its craft material.

- La Anniversary Grande is the first La Grande Combinasion that has lower stats than its earlier reskin, which is La Easter Grande.

[241/519]
### La Casa Boo
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/La_Casa_Boo
Avvisi: Halloween exclusive
Non confondere con: Esok Sekolah, Esok Goala, La Ginger Sekolah and Los Sekolahs
Tagline: want some candy?
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$100M/s | Costo=$40B | Status=Unobtainable (Spooky Lucky Block) | RarestMutation=Divine(2) | RarestTrait=Sombrero(1248) | Update=22 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Ritual=No | Sounds=LCboo.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
La Casa Boo appears to be a haunted house, colored green and its roof being purple with windows and a roof, similiar to Esok Sekolah. It is holding a bag like the ones you see in Trick-Or-Treats, filled with candy, it has only 1 eye, lastly, it has a mouth with sharp teeth and a large tongue sticking out, and bare legs with sharp claws.

La Casa Boo is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting it from the Spooky Lucky Block with a 0.3% chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- La Casa Boo's translation from Indonesian to English is “The Boo House”. The name is meant to be "The Spooky House", since "boo" is onomatopoeia for shout or shriek that spooks.
- If you translate it from Italian to English, you will get "The House Boo" as result.

- In the Limited Trick or Treating event, La Casa Boo is the rarest brainrot to encounter and gives the most Candy Corns, that is being 50.

- SpyderSammy leaked that there's only 34,091 La Casa Boo that exist.

--- OVERVIEW ---
La Easter Grande is a Secret Brainrot that costs $12.5B and generates $55M/s.

La Easter Grande appears as a fusion of multiple Brainrots:

- The head of Lirilì Larilà with a purple color and the shape of an egg, absent of eyes. The head was also chipped on its top right.

- The tire on Boneca Ambalabu, which is reskinned to be a blue egg with green stripes.

- Trippi Troppi's fins/legs, which are a light cream/peach-ish color, and are sticking out the side of Bunny Bunny Bunny Sahur's body and Boneca Ambalabu's tire/egg.

- Tralalero Tralala's head as an arm with an egg-yellow color instead of the regular blue.

- Bunny Bunny Bunny Sahur on the side of La Easter Grande, holding a basket of many colored Easter Eggs.

- A baby chicken, laying on top of Bunny Bunny Bunny Sahur, in replacement of where Boneca Ambalabu's face and Lirilì Larilà clock would usually be.

- Crafting it in the Taco Truck with this recipe
- 1x Tictac Sahur

- 1x Noo my Eggs

- 1x La Grande Combinasion

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- La Easter Grande was Leaked by Sammy after he asked if they should add a La Easter Grande in a Poll and most voted Yes. Sammy then said "alright that decides it" "la easter grande on tuesday :3".

- La Easter Grande is the first seasonal reskin of La Grande Combinasion to include an official reskin of Tung Tung Tung Sahur.
- La Easter Grande is also the first seasonal reskin with seasonal version of Tralalero Tralala that doesn't match the La Grande Combinasion reskin, in this case, Bunny Tralala. This is because Bunny Tralala was released AFTER the release of La Easter Grande.

- As of March 31, 2026, La Easter Grande is currently the second best Limited Quantity Brainrot, even surpassing Nacho Spyder by $5M/s.
- This is also the second best Limited Quantity seasonal reskin of La Grande Combinasion.

- La Easter Grande is one of the only brainrots to have stats known before release, with the other are being Ginger Gerat and Cerberus.

- La Easter Grande shares animations with La Lucky Grande.

- Sammy restocked 50K La Easter Grande in the Taco Truck during the Update 45 Admin Abuse, however it sold out almost immediately, meaning barely any people got to actually spawn theirs.

- Tralalero Tralala's left head seems visibly damaged, and his head appears to be hurt and bleeding, and its leg appears to have turned into bone.

- Half of Lirilì Larilà's cactus appears to be turned into bone, and its head seems to be missing some parts, but its clock remains in perfect condition.

- Boneca Ambalabu's head appears to have half its head turned into bone, alongside the wheel that turned into a ribcage.

- There were originally 500,000 La Extinct Grande in stock.
- SpyderSammy had bought one, then refilled it back to 500,000, making it 500,001.

- SpyderSammy then after it sold out quickly, put 350,000 back into stock making it 850,001.

- La Extinct Grande is the first Limited Quantity Brainrots. It is also the first La Grande Combinasion reskin.

- There are TWO misspellings of La Extinct Grande in the game, the first being the "La Extinct Grande". Its audio is an AI voice that said, "Extinct La Grande" and the thumbnail said La Grande Extinct.

- La Extinct Grande and La Anniversary Grande are the only La Grande Combinasion reskin that isn't based on Seasonal Event.

- Burguro from Burguro And Fryuro is located below the structure.

- Fryuro from Burguro And Fryuro are located on top of Burguro.

La Food Combinasion is/was obtained from the following ways:

- All of La Food Combinasion materials are having income higher than $40M/s. Ketchuru and Musturu makes $42.5M/s, Garama and Madundung makes $50M/s, and Burguro And Fryuro makes $150M/s.

- La Food Combinasion is the only Brainrot in Taco Lucky Block that doesn't have Mexican element on its design. Instead, La Food Combinasion components are based on burger, French fries, ketchup, mustard, salt, and honey, all are American culinary signature.

### La Grande Combinasion
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/La_Grande_Combinasion
Tagline: 1 la grande with chicleteira for a la grande... makes no sense.
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$10M/s | Costo=$1B | Status=Obtainable | Update=04 | Creator=La T | Ritual=No | Sounds=La-Grande-Combinasion%27s_Sound..mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
La Grande Combinasion is a Secret brainrot that produces $10M/s and costs $1B.

La Grande Combinasion is a fusion of 5 Brainrots:

- The top consists of Lirilì Larilà’s head on the top left and Boneca Ambalabu's head with Lirilì Larilà’s alarm clock on top right, on top of Tung Tung Tung Sahur. Trippi Troppi's legs stick out of Lirilì Larilà‘s body.

- The middle consists of Boneca Ambalabu's body on the left and Tung Tung Tung Sahur's body on the right. Tralalero Tralala sticks out of Boneca Ambalabu's body, Trippi Troppi's legs stick out of Tung Tung Tung Sahur's body.

- The right leg belongs to Tralalero Tralala, the left leg belongs to Tung Tung Tung Sahur who is wearing Lirilì Larilà’s sandal.

- Lirilì Larilà's green body part is found near Tung Tung Tung Sahur's leg albeit small.

- Bombardino Crocodilo is on one of the legs in the original video but not in steal a brainrot. (Its hard to see in the original video.)

La Grande Combinasion is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From the Red Carpet.

- From the Admin Lucky Block with a 0.5% (1 in 200) chance.

- From Sammy's Base.

- From the Backrooms Event.

- From the Cyber Craft Machine.
- Crafting Recipe
- 1x La Grande Combinasion

- 1x Chicleteira Bicicleteira

- From the LTM

- From the Brainrot Trader.
- Crafting Recipe
- 1x Rang Ring Bus

- 1x Chicleteira Bicicleteira

- or
- 2x Chicleteira Bicicleteira

- 1x Quesadilla Crocodila

- or
- 2x Noo my Candy

- or
- 1x Pot Hotspot

- 1x 67

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- On leak La Grande Combinasion's name was La Grande Combinazione

- La Grande Combinasion is the first brainrot to be a fusion of different Brainrots.
- There are many Combination Brainrots, however La Grande Combinasion is the first and the original.

- La Grande Combinasion was leaked on 06/19/25 (July 19 2025) from Sammy, making it the first leaked Brainrot.

- La Grande Combinasion's full name is Trippa Troppa Tralala Lirilira Tung Tung Sahur Boneca Tung Tung Tralalero Trippa Troppa Crocodina. To truncate it, it was simply called La Grande Combinasion.
- In the end of the full name of the original La Grande Combinasion, it has the last name of Bombardiro Crocodilo, even though Bombardiro Crocodilo is not in their design.

- La Grande Combinasion is the Brainrot with the most obtainment methods, at a whopping 8 ways.

- Tralalero Tralala, Tung Tung Tung Sahur, and Lirilì Larilà are the only brainrots part of the La Grande Combinasion that are not Rare.
- However, Tung Tung Tung Sahur was formerly Rare before its removal on September 13th, 2025. That would've left Tralalero Tralala and Lirilì Larilà the only ones to be breaking this rule, being a Brainrot God and a Common respectively.

- Despite Tung Tung Tung Sahur was removed on September 13, 2025, before readded on November 29, 2025 only to be removed again on April 25, 2026, La Grande Combinasion wasn't removed or have its design altered since La Grande Combinasion is a distinct character from Tung Tung Tung Sahur, and the original creator of Tung Tung Tung Sahur, @noxaasht, doesn't own the rights to La Grande Combinasion, since it wasn't their creation.

- La Grande Combinasion was used to be the best brainrot until Update 06 that came Garama and Madundung.

- La Grande Combinasion has many reskins like.
- La Extinct Grande

- La Spooky Grande

- La Jolly Grande

- La Romantic Grande

- La Lucky Grande

- La Easter Grande

- La Anniversary Grande

- La Summer Grande

- And more possibly upcoming.
--- LA GRANDE COMBINASION ---
1 la grande with chicleteira for a la grande... makes no sense.

La Spooky Grande was a limited Secret brainrot. This brainrot has sold out and is no longer obtainable with no chance of a restock. It was exclusive to the Witching Hour.

La Spooky Grande appears as a fusion of multiple Brainrots:

- Lirilì Larilà's head with the skin of a pumpkin.

- Boneca Ambalabu's tire with bandages wrapped around it.

- Trippi Troppi's legs.

- Zombie Tralala sticking out as an arm.

- Tung Tung Tung Sahur with sharp teeth and a suit, holding a spiked bat.

La Spooky Grande is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from a Limited Stock
- Recipe:
- 1x Vampira Cappucina

- 1x Zombie Tralala

- 1x Frankentteo

- 1x La Vacca Jacko Linterino

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
This section is a trivia section. Please relocate any relevant information into other sections of the article.

- This is a Limited Stock Brainrot confirmed by Sammy. It had 750,000 available to stock during Sammy's admin abuse on Saturday's Halloween update.

- The La Spooky Grande was sold out at around 10 PM EST on the same day it came out.

- Just like La Extinct Grande, this brainrot has a limited stock, meaning it was very likely for this brainrot to be sold out quickly.

- For some reason he costs less than La Extinct Grande, his past version but makes more income.

- Mummy Ambalabu, the Halloween reskin of Boneca Ambalabu which was added later, doesn't has its head turned into square Jack-o'-lantern in contrast to Boneca Ambalabu reskin in La Spooky Grande.

[256/519]
### La Supreme Combinasion
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/La_Supreme_Combinasion
Avvisi: Limited to Fuse Machine
Non confondere con: La Sahur Combinasion, La Secret Combinasion, or La Grande Combinasion. For other use, see La (disambiguation) 
Tagline: La Drip Combinasion
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$200M/s | Costo=$200B | Status=Unobtainable (Fuse Machine) | RarestMutation=Bloodrot(16) | RarestTrait=Galactic(58) | Update=10 | Creator=@random.rush6 | Ritual=No | Sounds=La_Supreme_Combinasione.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
La Supreme Combinasion's old income used to be $40M/s costing $7B, however it has been buffed to $200M/s costing $200B. It could've been obtained from the Fuse Machine which is currently removed from the update, as well as not being present in the new fuse.

La Supreme Combinasion is a mix of a specific amount of brainrots that can be seen sorted out in specific places of the structure:

- Brr es Teh Patipum appears to be the main torso for the brainrot, maintaining the structure stable and holding its arms to its chest.

- Pot Hotspot appears to be the head for the brainrot, being ontop of Brr es Teh Patipum and being seen holding its phone, as well as keeping Lirilì Larilà's clock afloat with it's other hand.

- Piccione Macchina can be seen aside Brr es Teh Patipum in its left side, having feather particles, seen having a large, oversized wooden leg, and having a curious look to it's face.

- Bulbito Bandito Traktorito appears to be aside Brr es Teh Patipum, being on its right side, being seen wearing similiar accessories to Gangster Footera, and also having a smug grin/smirk.

- Pakrahmatmamat can be seen below Brr es Teh Patipum, having a foot loosely below it wearing a slipper.

- Garama and Madundung can be seen below Bulbito Bandito Traktorito, being aside Pakrahmatmamat, and being a little smaller than in the original design.

La Supreme Combinasion is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Fuse Machine.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- La Supreme Combinasion used to make $40M/s and cost $7B before. It was buffed to it's current stats ($200M/s and $200B) after the exist counts of La Supreme Combinasion was revealed to be around ~6,800.
- Even though La Supreme Combinasion contains Garama and Madundung, pre-buff La Supreme Combinasion somehow generated less income than Garama and Madundung, which generates $50M/s. If we sum all the base income from every brainrot present in the combinasion it will equal to a final $53.3M/s, something quite disappointing considering the $40M/s base that it had.
- If the "brainrot income addition" logic is taken into account, this brainrot should still be worse than La Secret Combinasion, due to that combination having a Spaghetti Tualetti, a brainrot that already generates $60M/s alone. When summing up all the base incomes of La Secret Combinasion, it gives in total $92.8M/s, which when substracting the $53.3M/s from it, gives a $39.5M/s difference in total.

- The brainrot's full name is Garamararaman Piccionepot Orcalero Mat-Macchina Hotrahmat Parktungspot Orcapark Footrahpatipum Brgangsteresteh, but it was shortened to "La Supreme Combinasion".
- La Supreme Combinasion is designed as amalgamation of the most popular second generation of Italian Brainrots, much like La Grande Combinasion is amalgamation of the most popular first generation of Italian Brainrots.

- The full name also mentions Orcalero Orcala and Gangster Footera, even though his model does not appear in the combination. It's likely a mistake in the model since Piccione Macchina wears Orcalero Orcala's shoe in the original photo. Despite this, there is no single Gangster Footera design trace in both of original photo and in La Supreme Combinasion model.

- La Supreme Combinasion is the only Combinasion Brainrot that is consisted of 6 Brainrots, 7 if Lirilì Larilà that is represented by the clock was taken into account.

- Pot Hotspot's phone is bigger than his normal version's phone, and the color of his head is darker too.

- La Supreme Combinasion was the final brainrot added to the 2025 Fuse Machine 2 weeks before it was removed on September 6th.
--- LA SUPREME COMBINASION ---
La Drip Combinasion

--- OVERVIEW ---
La Taco Combinasion is a Limited Stock Secret Brainrot. It costs $5B and produces $35M/s.

La Taco Combinasion appears as a fusion of multiple Brainrots:

- Chihuanini Taconini, whose head is on top of the Nooo My Hotspot.

- Nooo My Hotspot, whose body is on the side.

- Bombardini Tortinii, whose face can be seen in the middle of the big taco, and whose wings can be seen next to the Chihuanini Taconini.

- Mariachi Corazoni, whose upper half and legs can be seen around the big taco, and whose moccasins can be seen being held by La Cucaracha.

- La Cucaracha, who is on the side, holding Mariachi Corazoni's moccasins.

- It also has Tipi Topi Taco's tail

La Taco Combinasion is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From the Taco Truck when it had stock.
- Crafting Recipe
- 1x Quesadilla Crocodila

- 1x Burrito Bandito

- 1x Los Nooo My Hotspotsitos

- 1x Mariachi Corazoni

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- La Taco Combinasion is considered the hardest Limited Quantity Brainrots to get due to it first stocking on October 21st and selling out on November 4th, 2025. (2 weeks)
- Additionally La Taco Combinasion required a Burrito Bandito which at the time was 0.5% on Taco Lucky Block, and a Mariachi Corazoni with a 1% from the piñata.

- Nobody knows why SpyderSammy used the same recipe as the Chipso and Queso since Chipso and Queso are barely sold during its debut. This also making it the first time a Limited Quantity Brainrot reusing exactly the same crafting recipe as previous Limited Quantity.

- La Taco Combination is a combination brainrot with Mariachi Corazoni and Bombardini Tortinii in the middle, Chihuanini Taconini and Nooo My Hotspot on the right, La Cucaracha on the right and the tail of Tipi Topi Taco at the back.

### Lerulerulerule
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Lerulerulerule
Tagline: I have NO idea why this is my favourite brainrot
STATS: Rarita=Mythic | Income=$8.7K/s | Costo=$3.5M | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | Update=13 | Creator=@alexey_pigeon | Ritual=No | Sounds=Lerulerulerulesound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Lerulerulerule is a Mythic brainrot that costs $3.5M and generates $8.7K/s.

Lerulerulerule is a muscular humanoid animal-plant hybrid Brainrot. It appears an anthropomorphized cactus with the head of a penguin, wearing a cowboy hat, boots and a belted denim shorts.

Lerulerulerule is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Lerulerulerule is one of the, if not the most common spawned Mythic Brainrots, due to the fact, in practice, users noted it spawns more often than most characters on its tier, and surveys have been made. The most likely reason that its RoadWeight, that dictate the probability for it to spawn on Red Carpet, was accidentally set into 0.705 instead its intended 0.075.
- This making Lerulerulerule more common than most Legendary and Epic Brainrots.

- Lerulerulerule’s real name is Penguinelli Cactussini.
--- LERULERULERULE ---
I have NO idea why this is my favourite brainrot

[272/519]
### Limited Quantity Brainrots
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Limited_Quantity_Brainrots
Avvisi: Only obtainable at specific times; have to be crafted to obtain (outside of Stealing).
--- TRIVIA ---
- Boppin Bunny and Festive 67 are the only limited quantity brainrots that can be bought with real money.

- La Extinct Grande was the first limited, and Tacorita Bicicleta was the first Taco themed limited.

- Steakini Fattini was the first Youtuber brainrot, the second was Caylusaurus.
--- BRAINROT INFORMATION ---
### La Extinct Grande

- (Stock of 500,000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE; OUT OF STOCK)

La Extinct Grande was a limited stock Secret Brainrot being added in the Extinct Event. It made $23.5M/s. To obtain it, you had to have a Extinct Ballerina, Extinct Tralalero, and a Extinct Matteo to give to the archaeologist.

La Extinct Grande
- It is a part of the Combinasion Family.

- It was the first limited stock brainrot.

- Fun fact this is the rarest limited quantity Brainrot!

### Tacorita Bicicleta

- (Stock of 1,000,000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE; OUT OF STOCK)

Tacorita Bicicleta was a limited stock Secret Brainrot being added on Taco Tuesday 09/16/25. It made $16.5M/s. To obtain it, you had to have a Capi Taco, Bombardini Tortinii, and a Quesadilla Crocodila to feed to Fat Sammy.

Tacorita Bicicletera
- It has a Los variant, being the Los Tacoritas.

### Perrito Burrito

- (Stock of 2,500,000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE; OUT OF STOCK)

Perrito Burrito was a limited stock Secret Brainrot being added on Taco Tuesday 09/30/25. It made $1M/s. To obtain it, you had to have a Chihuanini Taconini, Job Job Job Sahur, and a La Cucaracha to give to the Taco Truck, although they spawned it on taco tuesday 10/21/2025.

Perrito Burrito
- During the Taco Tuesday, Sammy spawned a Job Job Job Sahur to help people get it; which caused too many people to try to spawn it at the same time causing the servers to break; leading to sammy removing it until Saturday 10/04/25.

- Sammy has spawned this once to make up for the Taco Truck breaking.
- in his own words he said "that's the best thing I've spawned yet"

### Chillin Chili

- (Stock of 500,000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE; OUT OF STOCK)

Chillin Chili was a limited stock Secret Brainrot being added on Taco Tuesday 09/30/25. It made $25M/s. To obtain it, you had to have a Quesadilla Crocodila, 67, and a Los Nooo My Hotspotsitos to give to the Taco Truck.

Chillin Chili
- It’s the second Brainrot to require a 67 with the first one being Los Primos.

### La Spooky Grande

- (Stock of 750,000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE; OUT OF STOCK)

La Spooky Grande is a limited stock Secret Brainrot being added in the Witch Fuse update. It made $24.5M/s. To obtain it, you had to have a Vampira Cappuccina, Zombie Tralala, Frankentteo, and a La Vacca Jacko Linterino. Then you'd have to give the brainrots to the Witching Hour Event NPC.

La Spooky Grande
- Sammy triggered the Witching Hour Event 10 times during the Witch Fuse Admin Abuse event, however some are complaining that the La Vacca Jacko Linterino was more rare than the other brainrots to get.

- It is the second limited stock Brainrot that is a Combinasion/La Grande, with the first one being the La Extinct Grande.

### Quesadillo Vampiro

- (Stock of 900,000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE; OUT OF STOCK)

Quesadillo Vampiro was a limited stock Secret Brainrot. It made $3.5M/s. To obtain it, you had to obtain a Los Jobcitos, Graipuss Medussi and Perrito Burrito. Then you'd have to give the brainrots to the Taco Truck.

Quesadillo Vampiro
In The Taco Tuesday 10/21/2025 Sammy Spawned a Graipuss Medussi and Perrito Burrito to help Everyone.

This Brainrot ran out of stock fast, though needing Los Jobcitos to spawn it.

This is the only brainrot that is related to quesadillas other than family members of Quesadilla Crocodilla.

### Chipso and Queso

- (Stock of 250,000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE; OUT OF STOCK)

Chipso and Queso is a limited stock Secret Brainrot. It made $25M/s. To obtain it, you had to have a Mariachi Corazoni, Los Noo My Hotspotsitos and Burrito Bandito. Then you'd have to give the brainrots to the Taco Truck.

Chipso and Queso
- This is considered a hard limited-stock brainrot, as it requires Mariachi Corazoni, that is obtainable from the Piñata with 1% chance, Los Noo My Hotspotsitos that are obtainable from Taco Lucky Block with 1% chance, and Bandito Burrito that is obtainable from Taco Lucky Block with 0.5% chance

- This is the first Taco Truck / Limited stock brainrot lasting more than 2 days being in stock.

### La Taco Combinasion

- (Stock of 500,000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE; OUT OF STOCK)

La Taco Combinasion was a limited stock Secret Brainrot. It made $35M/s. To obtain it, you had to have a Quesadilla Crocodilla, Mariachi Corazoni, Los Nooo My Hotspotsitos and Burrito Bandito, 

La Taco Combinasion
- This is considered the currently hardest limited stock Brainrots due to it requiring the same Brainrots as Chipso and Queso and a Quesadilla Crocodila, causing less than 100k to sell out.

- Mariachi Corazoni was the only needed Brainrot that can be seen in its appearance.

- This Brainrot has lasted 3 days being in stock, making the longest lasting Taco Truck / Limited Stock Brainrot.

- It used to have the highest income out of any limited stock brainrot, before Swaggy Bros surpassed its income.

### Gobblino Uniciclino

- (Stock of 500,000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE: OUT OF STOCK)

Gobblino Uniciclino is a Limited Stock Secret brainrot. It costed $2.8B and had an income of $27.5M/s. Unlike many other Limited Stock brainrots, this one had a more unique way of getting it. You would have to wait in a server, and with a really low spawn chance rate, Gobblino Uniciclino would spawn.

Gobblino Uniciclino
- This is one of only Limited Stock brainrot to have a different way of obtaining it, the others being Festive 67 and Boppin Bunny. The others are only obtained through crafting them.

### W or L

- (Stock of 300,000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE; OUT OF STOCK)

W or L is a limited stock Secret brainrot. It made $30M/s. To obtain it, you had to have a Los Quesadillas, Los Burritos, Cuadramat and Pakrahmatmamat and Los 67 to craft it.

W or L
- This is the 3rd typographic brainrot in the game, the others being 67, and Los 67.

### Festive 67

- (Stock of 50.000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE; OUT OF STOCK)

Festive 67 was a limited stock Secret Brainrot added on 13/11/25 during an Admin Abuse. It made 67m/s. To obtain it, you had to buy the Festive 67 plush on the official website.

- It's Christmas reskin of 67

- This is the 2nd Limited Quantity Brainrot to be obtained a way different from crafting, the other being Gobblino Uniciclino

### La Jolly Grande

- (Stock of 500,000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE; OUT OF STOCK)

La Jolly Grande was a limited stock Secret Brainrot added on December 6, 2025 at 3:00PM EST during an Admin Abuse. It made $30M/s. To obtain it, you had to have a Ballerina Peppermintina, a Reindeer Tralala, a Santteo, and a List List List Sahur to give to Sammy. Or you could get it from the Christmas Spin. It also does the same amount as W or L

La Jolly Grande
- It is the third limited stock Brainrot that is a Combinasion/La Grande, with the second one being the La Spooky Grande.

- Sammy also added 100k stock to the Christmas roulette

### Swaggy Bros

- (Stock of 300,000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE; OUT OF STOCK)

Swaggy Bros was a limited stock Secret Brainrot added on 16/12/2025 during an Admin Abuse. It made $40M/s. To obtain it, you had to have a Swag Soda, a Los Burritos, a 67, and a Los 25 to give to the Taco Truck.

Swaggy Bros
- Many players thought that Chillin Chili would be part of the crafting recipe, but it was not.

### Tuff Toucan

- (Stock of 300,000) (CURRENTLY UNOBTAINABLE; OUT OF STOCK)

Tuff Toucan was a new limited stock Secret Brainrot added on 1/1/2026 during an Admin Abuse. It made $26M/s. To obtain it, you had to have a Tootini Shrimpini, a Rocco Disco, and a Bunito Bunito Spinito to give to the Tuff Toucan.

Tuff Toucan
- It has the same cost and income as Mieteteira Bicicleteira.

- It is likely based off Jake From Subway Surfers, the guy who you play as.

- This is another rare limited quantity brainrot as it only has 300K of stock. Other rare limited quantity brainrots that have 300k in stock or less are W or L, Swaggy Bros, and Chipso and Queso.

La Romantic Grande

[274/519]
### Lirilì Larilà
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Liril%C3%AC_Laril%C3%A0
Non confondere con: Cacto Hipopotamo, Elefanto Frigo, Strawberry Elephant, Cocofanto Elefanto or Tirilikalika Tirilikalako
Tagline: rarer then a garama btw.
STATS: Rarita=Common | Income=$3/s | Costo=$250 | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | Update=01 | Creator=capybarawt | Sounds=Lirililarila.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Lirilì Larilà is a Brainrot and costs $250 and generates $3/s, making it a reliable choice for early-game income. While not especially producing a lot of money, its low cost and easy availability ensure that most players encounter it early in their progression. 

Lirilì Larilà is an elephant with a cactus body wearing two brown sandals. It also has a flying clock while in its idle animation, but not elsewhere.

Lirilì Larilà is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
This section is a trivia section. Please relocate any relevant information into other sections of the article.

- Lirilì Larilà is found in La Karkerkar Combinasion along with La Grande Combinasion.

- The original concept art of Lirilì Larilà included a clock floating above its head, but the main game excludes this detail until it is in its idle animation.
- However, when this Brainrot is part of La Grande Combinasion, the clock is visible once again.
- If you zoom inside the model, you can see the clock is inside its body. This become more apparent with Lirilì Larilà with Cyber mutation, since its body is translucent, allowing you to view the clock inside its body without zooming.

- This is also the case with the Phantom mutation.

- Lirilì Larilà is one of the Brainrots found on La Grande Combinasion.
- Lirilì Larilà is the only Common Brainrot to show up in La Grande Combinasion.

- Lirilì Larilà is the only Brainrot to have tone marks.

- People joke about a Lirilì Larilà with the Strawberry trait, as when it has the Strawberry trait, it looks like Strawberry Elephant. A similar case can be found with a Cocofanto Elefanto with the Strawberry trait.

### List List List Sahur
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/List_List_List_Sahur
Avvisi: Only obtainable from Winter Hour, a Seasonal Event.
Non confondere con: Job Job Job Sahur, Love Love Love Sahur, Luck Luck Luck Sahur, Easter Easter Easter Sahur, or Los Jobcitos
Tagline: Sand sand sand took my place at being the ugliest reskin ;(
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$2M/s | Costo=$550M | Status=Unobtainable (Winter Hour) | Ritual=No | Sounds=Listlistlist.ogg,Christmasspawn.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
List List List Sahur is a Secret Brainrot added on December 6th, 2025 at 3 PM EST along with the Santa's Fuse.

List List List Sahur takes the appearence of a colorful paper with the word "LIST" on top of it. It has a joyful smile with red cheeks and a mix of a light green and red. It is seen holding a list, containing the names of Strawberry Elephant, Dragon Cannelloni, Garama and Madundung, Spaghetti Tualetti and Meowl. Its appearance is similar to Job Job Job Sahur's.

List List List Sahur is/was obtained from the following ways:

- A low chance to spawn from the Winter Hour event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- List List List Sahur was the hardest to obtain out of the 4 Christmas Event brainrots.

- List List List Sahur was used to craft the limited La Jolly Grande.

- List List List Sahur's wish list contains: Strawberry Elephant, Dragon Cannelloni, Garama and Madundung, Spaghetti Tualetti and Meowl.[1]

- This Brainrot has the same income and price as La Sahur Combinasion and Telemorte.

- Before that La Jolly Grande was firstly out of stock, this brainrot was highly demanded due to people needing it to craft the former one.

- Almost no one keeps it anymore, because it is no longer useful for the recipe of La Jolly Grande and now has greater collector value, possibly good trade value, due to it being Limited.

[276/519]
### Los 25
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Los_25
Avvisi: Obtainable from the Festive Lucky Block and a Seasonal Event.
Non confondere con: 25, 67, Los 67, Festive Lucky Block, 1x1x1x1, or Guest 666
Tagline: Maybe it should be called 75 since it's three 25s...
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$10M/s | Costo=$1.5B | Status=Unobtainable | Sounds=BrainrotLos_T......_Five_2.mp3
--- APPEARENCE ---
Los 25 are composed of three mini version 25. They are sharing same experssion, with the only difference being the eye colors each one has. The middle one has blue eyes, the left one has golden eyes, and the right one has purple eyes. 

Los 25 is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtaining it from the Festive Lucky Block with a 2.5% chance.

- Obtaining it from Santa's Factory.

--- OVERVIEW ---
Los 67 was released on October 4, 2025. It has a cost of $2.75B and an income of $22.5M/s. 

Los 67 depicts three theoretical children of 67. They can be seen expressing their emotions with different faces and actions. The one in the middle can be seen blushing, while doing the famous "67" gesture with its hands, displaying a "happy" expression. The one on the right can be seen doing a fighting stance, displaying a "tough" expression. The one on the left can be seen slightly less energetic then the other ones, displaying a "sad" or "tired" expression. 

Los 67 is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting it in the Los Lucky Blocks with a 0.5% chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Los 67 makes exactly 3x the income of its theoretical parent, 67, so it is one of the few Los/Las Brainrots that has an accurate Income. This brainrot includes three 67s, and a 67 generates $7.5M/s. Los 67 generates $22.5M/s, and $7.5M/s × 3 = $22.5M/s, making this brainrot numerically accurate, unlike most other Los/Las Brainrots.

- Los Chicleteiras Ritual is also easier to do than 1x1x1x1 Ritual Event, since the only requirement are two Chicleteira Bicicleteira instead of four Guerriro Digitales, and the Los Chicleteiras Ritual is not restricted on specific time.

Los Combinasionas is a baby version of La Grande Combinasion, and all of the brainrots except Trippi Troppi can be seen turning into baby counterparts. They can be seen sorted out in specific parts of the structure:

- In the right, a Los Tungtungtungcitos can be seen, beneath the baby version of Boneca Ambalabu. We see his counterpart to the right of him.

- In the middle, the wheel of a baby version of Boneca Ambalabu can be seen there. It's head can be seen above the Los Tungtungtungcitos.

- On the left, the cactus of a baby version of Lirili Larila can be seen, along with its head being above it, and it's clock besides it.

- Below the baby version of Lirili Larila, we see the brainrot Los Tralaleritos. One of them is being fused with the baby version of Lirili Larila, and the other one is to the left of the model. An unusual fin can be seen on the Tralalerito.

Los Combinasionas is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Similar to the last one, despite it having the same income as Nuclearo Dinosauro, Los Combinasionas is significantly more common.

- In the game's thumbnail, Los Combinasionas' name is spelt Los Combinations.

- Even though Los Combinasionas includes baby versions of Lirilì Larilà and Boneca Ambalabu, these two do not exist in-game separately. They are only in Los Combinasionas.
- Lirilì Larilà's clock in Los Combinasionas is yellow instead of gray.

- Los Combinasionas was originally planned to make $12.5M/s, but later it got swapped with $15M/s.

- Los Combinasionas does not have the legs from Trippi Troppi on it.

- Los Combinasionas has 2 reskins, those being Los Spooky Combinasionas and Los Jolly Combinasionas.

- Unlike with Ketupat Bros, even when putting in all the required brainrots into the Summer Fuse, you still only have a 50% chance of fusing Los Fruits, the same chance as getting a Los Sweethearts.
- However, with Ketupat Bros, if you put in the required brainrots (Ketupat Kepat and Ginger Gerat), you had an 100% chance of getting Ketupat Bros from the Fuse Machine.

--- OVERVIEW ---
Los Matteos is a Secret Brainrot that released in 15th August of 2025. It has a price of $80M and produces $325K/s. It can be obtained by doing the Matteo Ritual, which will then activate the Matteo's Hat event for 2 minutes and summon Los Matteos.

- Los Matteos has brighter fur color than its original counterpart Matteo.
--- OBTAINMENT ---
Los Matteos can be summoned by doing the Matteo Rituals which requires three Matteos and players. First, those users grab a Matteo and stack on top of each other's heads (can be done anywhere). If done right, green glowing orbs should appear and a big tree should emerge where the Matteos were, activating the Matteo's Hat event for 2 minutes and the Los Matteos will be summoned on the Red Carpet.

Los Mobilis appears as two different Brainrots. On the right is Los Nooo My Hotspotsitos, a mini burrito with limbs and holding a phone, and on the left is Los Hotspotsitos, a mini skeleton with phone as head and also holding a phone.

- Los Mobilis' name comes from the English-to-Spanish translation from "The Mobiles" to "Los Mobilis", however the correct translation is "Los Móviles".

Los Noobinis resembles baby versions of Noobini Pizzanini, retaining visual elements from it. Like their adult version, they resemble the ROBLOX Noob avatar with a big pizza, (compared to their head size), on their heads. 

Unlike Noobini Pizzanini, Los Noobinis’ shirts have sleeves. The Noobini on the left is sitting and appears sad. The middle Noobini is smiling and seems positive, opposite to the one on the left. The Noobini on the right looks shocked while crouching and punching the air as if it were in Minecraft. All three Noobinis have pink cheeks, and they have large eyes like most other Baby Brainrots.

Los Noobinis is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Craft Machine.

- 1 Carrotini Brainini

- Getting from the Cyber Craft

- 3 Noobini Pizzanini

- 1 Tracoducotulu Delapeladustuz

- Stealing, a Core Feature.

- Los Noobinis is the first, and currently the only, baby Brainrot that isn't a Brainrot God or Secret.

- Los Noobinis is based off a Common Brainrot while the others are based off of Brainrot God and higher. (Los Tungtungtungcitos as an exception because Tung Tung Tung Sahur was a Rare (Now a Secret). Same with Las Cappuchinas because Ballerina Cappuccina is a Legendary)
- Because of this, Los Noobinis is the lowest income Baby Brainrot.

- The Noobini on the right of Los Noobinis appears to be crouching up and down and punching, very similarly to the Players in Minecraft.

- Los Noobinis has gotten devalued due to SpyderSammy bringing it back in the Cyber Craft Machine, making many collectors both mad and angry.
- The reason for Sammy bringing it back is probably because it wouldn't make sense for a Los version of the worst Brainrot in the game to be somewhat rare, and also probably due to the fact it nearly has 1M exists.

STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$31M/s | Costo=$3.75B | Status=Obtainable (Fishing) | RarestMutation=Cyber(2) | RarestTrait=Fireworks(13352) | Update=25 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Ritual=No | Sounds=LossoundPrimos.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Los Primos is a Secret added on September 27, 2025, with the Craft Machine update, giving $31M/s. The cost for Los Primos is $3.75B.

Los Primos consists of a happy Tralalerito from Los Tralaleritos and a happy Orcalito from Los Orcalitos. The Los Tralaleritos has black eyes shaded with a faint colour of blue and brown, with the Los Tralaleritos wearing blue sneakers. Instead, the Los Orcalitos has black eyes with a shade of blue, with the Los Orcalitos wearing white sneakers. Both are the happy variants of respective brainrots.

Los Primos is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtaining it from the Craft Machine when it was available.
- Craft Machine Recipe:
- Los Orcalitos

- Los Tralaleritos

- 67

- Los Bros

- Obtaining it from the Fishing Event with a small chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Los Primos is the best Brainrot craftable in the Craft Machine pre-28/02/2026 buff. (And will stay that way as the Craft Machine is gone.)

- Los Primos is the Spanish/Portuguese word for "The Cousin". It's also referring to their status as the primary (Primus) animals in sea food chain, since Tralalerito and Orcalito respectively are based on shark and orca, the apex predators of the sea.

- Los Primos was the last Brainrot Sammy added to the Craft Machine before it was removed.

- Los Primos requires a 67 to craft, possibly referring to cousins usually being portrayed as the "brainrotted one".

- There is a chance that Los Primos is in every Mutation since fishing is ran once per Mutaton and was in the Craft Machine.

- Only 1 person has a Phantom Los Primos
--- LOS PRIMOS ---
We have aura! Unlike those Lovebirds over there

--- OVERVIEW ---
Los Sekolahs is a Secret brainrot, costing $45B to buy, making $110M/s, and is obtained from Los Lucky Blocks with a 0.25% to get so you need to open about 400 or more Los Lucky Blocks.

Los Sekolahs are the baby versions of Esok Sekolah. They are mini humanoid schoolhouses with limbs and a face, with its tongue sticking out and carrying sign with "9" written on it. They can be seen expressing their emotions with different faces. The one in the middle can be seen smiling and happy. The one in the right can be seen having a scheming face and mischievious. The one on the left can be seen with a crying face and sad.

Los Sekolahs is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting it from the Los Lucky Blocks with a very low chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Los Sekolahs is the fourth brainrot from the Secret Lucky Block to be a Los Variant. The first is Los Hotspotsitos, second being Los Tortus and third being Los Spaghettis.

- Los Sekolahs makes $110M/s, despite Los Spaghettis makes $70M/s and Spaghetti Tualetti is rarer and better than Esok Sekolah in Secret Lucky Block. This might be because Los Sekolahs is added after Los Spaghettis.

- The Plants Vs Brainrots version of Los Sekolahs was Los Sekolitos, but they were removed and replaced with Los Casettatatatata prior to the addition of Los Sekolahs. This making Los Sekolahs a Brainrot that has been existed first on Steal a Brainrot's competitor, before being added to Steal a Brainrot.

- Los Sekolahs was leaked by SpyderSammy over 26 days ago meaning it is the longest time for a brainrot to be released after it is leaked, beating Mi Gatito's record which has a record of 25 days.

--- OVERVIEW ---
Los Spyderinis is a Secret Brainrot released on August 23rd, 2025. This brainrot can only be obtained from the Sammyni Ritual. You can do the Sammyni Ritual by making a square with four Sammyni Spyderinis. This ritual also triggers the Sammyni Invasion event. It was formerly obtainable from the Admin Lucky Block and from Sammy's Base. But it was removed from the Admin Lucky Block due to lack of space.
--- TRIVIA ---
- This brainrot was originally going to be Los Spiderinis, which required you to do a ritual with an unknown amount of Chimpanzini Spiderinis likely the same amount as now.

- This Brainrot is based off of a Brainrot which used to be Chimpanzini Spiderini, which is Sammyni Spyderini.

- Sammyni Spyderini was brought back along with Gattatino Nyanino and Unclito Samito.

- Along with the Los Chicleteiras and Los Karkeritos this is one of the only brainrots' rituals that requires more/less than 3 of its kind.

- Although it is more expensive than Los Tralaleritos, it still makes less money than it.

- This is one of the rarest ritual brainrots as almost no-one does the ritual.

- This brainrot used to be in the Admin Lucky Block, but it was removed from the Admin Lucky Block and was replaced by Guerriro Digitale.

- This brainrot costs the same as Torrtuginni Dragonfrutini, despite making more

- This brainrot is used in one of the Los Sigmas recipe.
--- LOS SPYDERINIS ---
Sammy's kids

|

Los Spyderinis appear to be 3 baby versions of Sammyini Spyderini, with the one on the middle doing the :3 face, the one on the left frowning, and the one on the right smiling. --- OVERVIEW ---
Los Sweethearts is a Secret Brainrot that makes $16.5M/s and costs $2.2B

Los Sweethearts contains two brainrots, consisting of a duo. Its depicted as a duo between a happy Los Tralaleritos, and a happy Las Tralaleritas. Both of these characters are seen wearing tennie shoes, and consist of a blue and pink. They are seen spinning while holding their hands while going to the player's base. 

Los Sweethearts is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Fusing it from the Fuse Machine using Los Tralaleritos, Las Tralaleritas, Cupid Hotspot, and Noo my Heart from the Heart Lucky Block with a 50% chance. However, this method doesn't guarantee you will get it, as other players have ended up with a Chill Puppy, Spinny Hammy or Bacuru and Egguru.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Los Sweethearts is a Valentine duo of Los Tralaleritos and Las Tralaleritas. As such, it was leaked along with the Valentine's Base, Rose Base, Cupid Hotspot, and Rosetti Tualetti.

- The singular Las Tralaleritas has dots on its bow, unlike the original design, which was a plain pink bow. This bow design can also be seen in Los Trios.

- Los Sweethearts is hard to get, because the crafting recipe is two brainrots from Heart Lucky Block and Heart Lucky Block is no longer obtainable as of Update 39, and it can only be crafted from 2026 Fuse Machine.

URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Los_Tungtungtungcitos
Avvisi: Los Lucky Blocks Exclusive.
Non confondere con: Tung Tung Tung Sahur, Bunny Bunny Bunny Sahur, Los Jobcitos, Los Combinasionas, Los Spooky Combinasionas, or Los Jolly Combinasionas
Tagline: Los Soncitos
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$210K/s | Costo=$37.5M | Status=Obtainable (Los Lucky Blocks, Admin Abuse) | Ritual=No | Sounds=Los_Tungtungtungcitos.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Los Tungtungtungcitos is a Brainrot God. They were obtainable from the Fuse Machine. Los Tungtungtungcitos costs $37.5M and produces $210K/s. 

They appear to be mini versions of Tung Tung Tung Sahur, with the one on the middle smiling, the one on the left bored and the one on the right smiling aswell. They are holding tiny wooden bats and wearing blue shoes, and The one on the left produces green lightning particles, the one on the middle produces red and the one on the right produces blue. 

Los Tungtungtungcitos is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Los Lucky Blocks

- Spawning with a low chance during the Tung Tung Attack event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Los Tungtungtungcitos is one of two Brainrots that contains Tung Tung Tung Sahur as it was removed. The other Brainrot are La Grande Combinasion, if not counting La Grande Combinasion reskin.

- During the event "Tung Tung Attack", Los Tungtungtungcitos has a 0.5% chance to spawn.

- Los Tungtungtungcitos is the only Los Brainrot that it's worse than its original counterpart version, it is not following the Los versions always being better than the parent rule.
- This is because on its release, Tung Tung Tung Sahur was still a Rare.
--- LOS TUNGTUNGTUNGCITOS ---
Los Soncitos

[325/519]
### Love Love Bear
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Love_Love_Bear
Non confondere con: Money Money Reindeer, Money Money Puggy, Los Puggies, Rosey and Teddy, or Bearito Cabinito
Tagline: no longer a revenant
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$225M/s | Costo=$225B | Ritual=No | Sounds=Love_Love_Bear.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Love Love Bear is a Secret Brainrot that is obtainable from the Cupid's Machine.

Love Love Bear appears similar to Money Money Puggy, however it is a red teddy bear covered in Valentine's cards with writing saying things such as "I Love You", "Cute", "Be Mine" and "Sweet". Love Love Bear also holds a rose inside their mouth.

Love Love Bear is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Cupid's Machine.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Love Love Bear is an insanely detailed reskin of Money Money Puggy.

- Love Love Bear was leaked by SpyderSammy on February 6th, the same day Lovin Rose and La Romantic Grande were leaked.

- Love Love Bear is obtainable after getting the Lovin Rose from the Cupid's Machine. Since Lovin Rose is already rare at 0.5%, the love love bear is extremely rare, at 0.1% of getting it, assuming it is back-to-back.

- Love Love Bear's income got buffed 3 times $75M/s in release, to $140M/s at one week after Valentine's Event was held, and finally $225M/s after Valentine's Event was concluded.

- Love Love Bear is a male, but a lot of people mistake him as female.
--- LOVE LOVE BEAR ---
no longer a revenant

--- OVERVIEW ---
Lovin Rose is an anthropomorphic petal cone. It can be seen wearing a white uniform accompanied by red buttons, along with a red belt with the shape of a bow, and arms and legs which are seen having a plant-like form. They can be seen wearing red tennie shoes, while doing the "peace out" hand-sign with both their hands, and having a happy expression. They are wearing glasses with the form of hearts, and have rose-like hair.

Lovin Rose is/was obtained from the following ways:

- It is a Valentines version of Chillin Chili.

- It is obtainable from the Cupid Machine, with an 0.25% chance, but buffed to 0.50% on 2/10/26.

- This is a brainrot needed for the Cupid's Machine (Cupid Hotspot and Lovin Rose).

- After getting it from the Cupid's Machine, you'll have a chance of getting Love Love Bear.

- This brainrot currently has the same stats as Fragola La La La.

Lumaca Malefica is a snail Brainrot with same color and anatomy as Snailenzo, but without the car part attached on. Lumaca Malefica wearing a black witch hat with purple ribbon and crescent moon accessory on top of its shell, and wielding a magic staff.

Lumaca Malefica is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Stealing, a Core Feature.

- That also means that Lumaca Malefica wears the witch hat, although not in the Witch Fuse.

- Lumaca Malefica is a direct Italian translation for "Maleficent Snail". This making it one of very few Brainrots in the game that have Italian name that are not written in Brainrot version of Italian.

[330/519]
### Luv Luv Luv
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Luv_Luv_Luv
Non confondere con: Dul Dul Dul, Skull Skull Skull, Dug dug dug, Sand Sand Sand, Gold Gold Gold, or Doi Doi Do
Tagline: Shouldn't have gambled on love
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$282.5K/s | Costo=$48.25M | Status=Unobtainable (Heart Lucky Block) | Update=37 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Ritual=No | Sounds=LuvLuvLuvsound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Luv Luv Luv is a New World Monkey like Dul Dul Dul except it has side ponytail with pink ribbon as hairstyle. Its face are covered with make up. Luv Luv Luv wears female pink school uniform with golden buttons and red bowtie, alongside pink backpack and pink shoes. 

Luv Luv Luv is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting it from Heart Lucky Block.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Luv Luv Luv is the second different variant of Dul Dul Dul, with the first being Skull Skull Skull. Both are Seasonal Variant of Dul Dul Dul, and are Brainrot God, in contrast to Dul Dul Dul's Secret Rarity.

- While Dul Dul Dul and Skull Skull Skull are modeled after Indonesian elementary student and thus wear Indonesian school uniform for male, Luv Luv Luv is instead modeled after Japanese elementary student, and thus wear Japanese school uniform for female.
- Actual Indonesian school uniform for female has shirt that is restricted in white color, making Indonesian school uniform are impossible to have the top and bottom clothing parts has same color, and most importantly, skirt that covers entire lower body part.

- Japanese school uniform for female, in other hand, are common to have the top and bottom clothing parts shares a same color, and the skirt usually only covers the thighs part.
--- LUV LUV LUV ---
Shouldn't have gambled on love

[332/519]
### Malame Amarele
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Malame_Amarele
Avvisi: Craft Machine Exclusive.
Non confondere con: Gangster Footera or Brr Brr Patapim
Tagline: Wait, this brainrot exists
STATS: Rarita=Epic | Income=$140/s | Costo=$23.5K | Status=Unobtainable (Craft Machine) | RarestMutation=Radioactive(5) | Update=15 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Ritual=No | Sounds=Malamesound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Malame Amarale has the appearance of a yellow triangular creature with small arms and big feet, it also has large, sorrowful eyes.

Malame Amarele is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From the Craft Machine.
- Crafting Recipe
- 2x Gangster Footera (formerly 2x Tung Tung Tung Sahur)

- 1x Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur

- 1x Brr Brr Patapim

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Malame Amarele is a Brainrot version of the word "Malamé Amarelo", a word that actually comes from a Brazilian TikTok spam comment which means "Yellowish Stain" in English.

- Malame Amarele's crafting recipe used to use Tung Tung Tung Sahurs, but that has been replaced with Gangster Footeras after Tung Tung Tung Sahur are removed.

- There are 5 Malame Amarele with the Radioactive mutation. This is possible due to people not opening the Craft Machine until much later, allowing Malame Amarele to get this mutation. This trick is named Time Machine.
--- MALAME AMARELE ---

--- OVERVIEW ---
Mangolini Parrocini is an Epic Brainrot obtainable from the Craft Machine that costs $38.5K and generates $235/s. It was accidentally added to the Brainrot Trader by Sammy on November 22, 2025 during Admin Abuse.

Mangolini Parrocini takes on the appearance of a parrot and features mango-like colors, including yellow, green, and orange.

Mangolini Parrocini is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Crafting it in the Craft Machine.
- Crafting Recipe
- 1x Pipi Kiwi

- 1x Pipi Avocado

- 1x Boneca Ambalabu

- 1x Perochello Lemonchello

- From the Brainrot Trader.
- Crafting Recipe
- 2x Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur

- 2x Tric Trac Baraboom

- or
- 2x Trulimero Trulicina

- 1x Brr Brr Patapim

- or
- 2x Trulimero Trulicina

- or
- 1x Bandito Bobritto

- 1x Avocadini Guffo

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- SpyderSammy accidentally added it to the Brainrot Trader during an Admin Abuse.

- Mangolini Parrocini is one of the rarest Brainrots to obtain from the Craft Machine, as it requires Pipi Avocado to be crafted, and Pipi Avocado has become unobtainable after the Fuse Machine got deleted.
- If Mangolini Parrocini was not added in the Brainrot Trader, it could have been buffed since it required a Pipi Avocado (unobtainable at that time) to craft it.

### Mariachi Corazoni
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Mariachi_Corazoni
Avvisi: Admin Abuse Exclusive
Non confondere con: Los Amigos, Los Mariachis
Tagline: shaka shaka shaka!!!
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$12.5M/s | Costo=$1.75B | Sounds=Mariachicorazoni.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Mariachi Corazoni is a Secret Brainrot that was released on September 30, 2025, as part of the Mexico update along with its event. It costs $1.7B to purchase and its income is $12.5M/s.

Mariachi Corazoni has a blue-ish skeleton-like body, two moccasins, and a Sombrero. The eyes are red hearts. This brainrot was originally inspired by Miguel, the person who also contributed to some of the animations for the game's brainrots.

Mariachi Corazoni is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting it from the Piñata with a 1% chance.

- Stealing it from the Sammy's Base Event with a rare chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Mariachi Corazoni is based off the Day of the Dead, a Mexican holiday.

- This Brainrot looks similar to Tostarenans from the Nintendo video game Super Mario Odyssey.
--- MARIACHI CORAZONI ---

[336/519]
### Mastodontico Telepiedone
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Mastodontico_Telepiedone
Avvisi: A Lucky Block exclusive Brainrot.
Non confondere con: Telemorte, Chimnino, Baskito, or Globa Steppa
Tagline: why am I being kicked - Globa Steppa
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$275K/s | Costo=$47.5M | Status=Obtainable (Brainrot God Lucky Block) | Ritual=No | Sounds=MastodonticoTelepiedonesound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Mastodontico Telepiedone is a Brainrot God that's only obtainable from the Brainrot God Lucky Block. They have a price of $47.5M and an income of $275K/s. 

Mastodontico Telepiedone is a brown CRT TV box with legs and juggling Earth like a soccer ball. The TV screen showing a static noise.

Mastodontico Telepiedone is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Brainrot God Lucky Block.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Mastodontico Telepiedone's full name is "Il Mastodontico Telepiedone Planetario".

- Mastodontico Telepiedone is the second rarest Brainrot from the Brainrot God Lucky Block, with 5% chance from the Brainrot God Lucky Block.

- Mastodontico Telepiedone is a heavy Brainrot as Mastodontico Telepiedone is literally kicking the Earth with his foot, as if the Earth is as light as a soccer ball.

- Mastodontico Telepiedone, Matteo, and Tralalero Tralala are the only Brainrot Gods that consistently have seasonal variant.
- On Halloween, their counterparts were Telemorte, Frankentteo, and Zombie Tralala respectively.

- On Christmas, their counterparts were Chimnino, Santteo, and Reindeer Tralala respectively.

- On Easter, their counterparts were Baskito, Buntteo, and Bunny Tralala.
--- MASTODONTICO TELEPIEDONE ---
why am I being kicked - Globa Steppa

[337/519]
### Matteo
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Matteo
Avvisi: Admin Abuse exclusive.
Non confondere con: Carloo, Alessio, Antonio, Extinct Matteo, Frankentteo, Santteo, Patteo, Buntteo, or Los Matteos
Tagline: "Matteeoooooooo" 🗣️🔥
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$50K/s | Costo=$10M | Status=Unobtainable (Admin Abuse) | Sounds=Matteo.mp3,MatteoApperanceSound.mp3,MatteoPortalOpening.mp3,Matteeeeeoooooo!!!.mp3
--- TRIVIA ---
- Matteo is the first human Brainrots. The second one being Antonio.

- Matteo has the second most reskins amongst other Brainrots, tied with Tralalero Tralala, with 4 reskins. La Grande Combinasion has the most with 8 reskins.

- Matteo has its own ritual, which requires 3 players holding Matteo on top of each other, and it spawns Los Matteos alongside the Matteo event which can give brainrots the Matteo Hat trait.
- Matteo is the only Brainrot with ritual that has the vertical formation to trigger the ritual instead an usual horizontal formation.

- Matteo is the first Brainrot in Steal a Brainrot to have an actual human name, which is translated to Matthew.

- Matteo, Tralalero Tralala & Mastodontico Telepiedone are the only Brainrot God that consistently have seasonal variant.
- On Halloween, their counterpart are Frankentteo, Zombie Tralala, and Telemorte respectively.

- On Christmas, their counterpart are Santteo, Reindeer Tralala, and Chimnino respectively.

- On St. Patrick's, Matteo 's counterpart is Patteo. Tralalero Tralala and Mastodontico Telepiedone doesn't have St. Patrick's reskin.

- On Easter, their counterpart are Buntteo, Bunny Tralala, and Baskito respectively.

- This pattern stopped in the summer.

- Matteo is the first Brainrot to change the map setting by its presence. Trees will grow in the map before Matteo spawns. If the trees are Rainbow, it is guaranteed that the Matteo that will be spawned is Rainbow.
- Matteo is one of <20 Brainrots with custom spawn sound. Matteo has the only spawn effect shouting its name as the sound.
--- MATTEO ---
"Matteeoooooooo" 🗣️🔥

Signifiers | 

  |
--- OVEREVIEW ---
Matteo is a Brainrot God (also named Matthew in English) only spawned by Admin events. It has a price of $10M and an income of $50K/s. 

Matteo is a dwarf with brown fur covering its body. It wear black top hat, black sunglasses, and black tie.

Matteo is/was obtained from the following ways:

- During Admin Abuse.

- From the Backrooms Event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.

### Megalodon Family
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Megalodon_Family
Avvisi: stub
Non confondere con: Tralalero Tralala (Disambiguation)
--- INTRODUCTION ---
The Megalodon Family refers to brainrots who are based off a megalodon, or look alike. All the current Brainrots in this family are all coincidentally Secrets. The first ever brainrot in the Megalodon Family is the Tralaledon itself, being the first and original version of the brainrot, released on May 15, 2025. This might be the only Family Brainrot to be unobtainable.

### Meowl
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Meowl
