--- TRIVIA ---
This section is a trivia section. Please relocate any relevant information into other sections of the article.

- Meowl is currently the second-best Brainrot obtainable through normal gameplay, behind Strawberry Elephant, and tied with Headless Horseman.

- Meowl was buffed six times as well, from $275M/s, to $300M/s, to $400M/s, to $450M/s, to $500M/s then finally $600M/s. Along with its price, too, buffed by the billions.

- While having the Meowl Brainrot in your base, you unlock an Exclusive Base only obtainable whilst it is in your base, like other OG's.
- If someone is holding the Meowl in their hands, the Base will disappear; however, it will be re-equipped again if the Meowl is dropped.

- Meowl's name is a portmanteau of "meow" and "owl", hence its appearance as a cat-owl fusion.

- Meowl is the only OG brainrot that doesn't cost 1000 times more than it produces.

- There is only 105 Rainbow Meowls

- Meowl is SpyderSammy's favorite Brainrot.
- According to him, the best mutation, visual-wise, for Meowl is Cyber, and the best trait, visual-wise for Meowl is Strawberry.
--- MEOWL ---
I'm a new soul, I came to this strange world

[341/519]
### Mi Gatito
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Mi_Gatito
Non confondere con: Los Mi Gatitos, Gattatino Neonino, Gattatino Nyanino, Gattito Tacoto, Los Gattitos, or Meowl
Tagline: ay mi gatito miau miau
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$3.2M/s | Costo=$725M | Status=Unobtainable | Update=36 | Creator=Princesita Kelly | Sounds=Mi_Gatito.wav
--- OVERVIEW ---
Mi Gatito is a brainrot that gives $3.25M/s and costs $725M to purchase.

Mi Gatito is depicted as a humanoid ginger cat.

Mi Gatito was first spawned on Saturday, January 31st 2026 then Taco Tuesday, February 3rd 2026, and finally on Saturday, February 7th, 2026. 

Mi Gatito is/was obtained from the following ways:

- When spawned via SpyderSammy . Only spawned 3 times.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Mi Gatito was teased on January 31, 2026, at 6:33 PM EST inside the Community Server, writing “AY MI GATITO MIAU MIAU AY MI GATITO MIAU MIAU” along with a video of this brainrot.

- During Taco Tuesday, Sammy playfully said, "ay mi gatito miau miau :3," referencing this bit of brainrot.

- Mi Gatito is inspired by the song “Ay Mi Gatito” by Princesita Kelly. It also draws a lot of influence from “MONTAGEM MIAU”, a funk remix of Princesita Kelly’s track.
- The original song was launched in 2010, but it began to really gain attraction during late 2025 - early 2026.

- Despite alot of people predicting it to be an OG, Mi Gatito is turned out to not be an OG but rather a mid-tier secret, probably because the remix "MONTAGEM MIAU" released only a few months ago in 2025.

- "Mi Gatito" translates to "My Little Cat", or ''My Kitty'' when translated in English.

- During Taco Tuesday (30/06/2026), a person asked SpyderSammy to spawn Mi Gatito, however, SpyderSammy refused to spawn it as he said he couldn't spawn it again.
--- MI GATITO ---
ay mi gatito miau miau

[342/519]
### Mieteteira Bicicleteira
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Mieteteira_Bicicleteira
Avvisi: Witch Fuse Exclusive., part_of_family
Famiglia: Bicicleteira Family
Non confondere con: Chicleteira Bicicleteira, Chicleteirina Bicicleteirina, Chicleteira Noelteira, Chicleteira Cupideira, or Los Chicleteiras
Tagline: absolute aura
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$26M/s | Costo=$2.75B | Status=Unobtainable (Witch Fuse) | Sounds=Mieteteira_Bicicleteira.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Mieteteira Bicicleteira is a Secret brainrot that costs $2.75B and generates $26M/s. He was obtainable from the Witch Fuse feature. 

Mieteteira Bicicleteira appears to be Chicleteira Bicicleteira in a Grim Reaper costume. It is holding a sickle and sporting vampire teeth with blood dripping from the side of its mouth, The Bubblegum is also changed to grey and white. It has a black bubblegum nose replacing its Yellow bubblegum nose, it retains its black pupils, but now has red on the edges The bike also contains a basket full of Halloween candy that includes variations of candy canes and lolipops.

Mieteteira Bicicleteira is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Fusing from the Witch Fuse.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- While Mieteteira Bicicleteira is shown standing on top of his bike on his render in leak, his walking animation and idle animation doesn't show him standing. Instead, he shared the animation with his regular counterpart, Chicleteira Bicicleteira.

- Mieteteira Bicicleteira is colloquially known as "reaper bike". This is mainly due to the difficulty of spelling this brainrot's name.
- Additionally, Mieteteira Bicicleteira is named after Mietere (Italian word for reap) and Bicicletta (Italian word for bike).

- Mieteteira Bicicleteira needed items worth more than 2B+ to stand a chance in Witch Fuse
--- MIETETEIRA BICICLETEIRA ---
absolute aura

--- OVERVIEW ---
Money Money Puggy is a Secret Brainrot that costs $2.6B and produces $21M/s.

Money Money Puggy is a pug wearing stacks of dollar bills. Their ears are made of dollars bills and they have a gold collar and gold straps, They also have gold coins on the sides of their cheeks. 

Money Money Puggy is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Obtaining it from Sammy's Base with a relatively low chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Money Money Puggy was released on September 27th.

- The Los version of this Brainrot, Los Puggies, released on November 8th, 2025. It used to be a stock item by the Brainrot Dealer, but then became a trade-exclusive Brainrot by the Brainrot Trader.
- It was supposed to have a variant called Money Meow, but it was eventually scrapped and replaced with Los Puggies.

- When Money Money Puggy was first released, its eyes were facing at a different angle. When it released, its eyes were changed to face.

- Money Money Puggy was originally called Money Muh Money Money

- Money Money Puggy was needed for Caylusaurus as well as Nuclearo Dinossauro and Burrito Bandito.

- It has the same status as Churrito Bunnito.

Noo La Polizia is Los Nooo My Hotspotsitos that wears police uniforms. The middle Polizia is making a happy face while holding a walkie-talkie. Its left equivalent is happy while holding both handcuffs and what appears to be a small baton. Its right equivalent is distraught while holding a flashlight and a notebook.

Noo La Polizia is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From the Brainrot Dealer for $67M or  499.

- From the Brainrot Trader.
- Crafting Recipe
- 1x Ballerino Lololo

- 1x Tralalero Tralala

- 1x Gattatino Nyanino

- or
- 1x Brasilini Berimbini

- or
- 2x Trenostruzzo Turbo 3000

- or
- 2x Vampira Cappuccina

- 1x Chihuanini Taconini

- Stealing, a Core Feature.

- Noo La Polizia was teased in the community server, alongside Pirulitoita Bicicleteira and Cooki and Milki.

While the police in the meme is portrayed as human policeman, Steal a Brainrot rendition of Noo La Polizia portraying them as variant of Los Nooo My Hotspotsitos.

- Noo La Polizia is the first 'Noo' Brainrot to not be in Secret rarity. Due to this, Noo La Polizia is a worse version of both of its original version, which is Nooo My Hotspot and Los Nooo My Hotspotsitos.

### Noo my Candy
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Noo_my_Candy
Avvisi: Trick or Treating Exclusive., part_of_family
Famiglia: Halloween Brainrots
Non confondere con: Nooo My Hotspot, Noo my Present, Noo my examine, Noo my Heart, Noo my Gold, Noo my Eggs, or Los Candies
Tagline: Candy Candy
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$5M/s | Costo=$900M | Status=Unobtainable | Sounds=NooMyCandy.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Noo my Candy is a Secret brainrot that was added on 10/25/2025. It costs $900M and has a base income of $5M/s.

Noo my Candy is an orange bucket with Jack-o'-lantern mouth. It has black limbs with hand making a begging gesture, while also looking sad. Candies are scattered in front of him.

Noo my Candy is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Riding the Roller-Coaster with it in the Trick or Treating event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Noo my Candy was relatively difficult to obtain; you had to get on the roller coaster, and there was a 1% chance of getting it by buying it at the entrance or buying it on the roller coaster.
- Since there's no incentive for player to ride on roller coaster, Noo my Candy become even much harder to obtain. Trick or Treating's spiritual successor, Gingerbread Town, would later gives you an incentive to ride on sleigh, since it still give you hefty sum of Candy Cane even if you doesn't get Money Money Reindeer.

- Noo my Candy was added 6 days before Halloween.

- Noo my Candy exists dropped when the Brainrot Dealer came out; to make a La Grande Combinasion you needed two Noo My Candy, and a lot of people spent them on that, since La Grande Combinasion wasn't as cheap as it is now.
--- NOO MY CANDY ---

Noo my examine is a Secret Brainrot that costs $525M and makes $1.7M/s.

Noo my examine is an exam paper with math questions written on it. All the questions are ticked wrong and an "Ⓕ" is written on the paper as the grade. It holds a red pencil with a blue end and uses blue sneakers.

Noo my examine is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Dul Dul Dul ritual.

- Noo my examine's model has "Examen" wrote on it instead supposed "Examine", which led to it colloquially called "Noo My Examen".

- Noo my examine is very rare, only having around 10K exists. This is because practically no one does the ritual anymore. This also explains why there are no phantom Noo my examines in existence

[360/519]
### Noobini Pizzanini
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Noobini_Pizzanini
Non confondere con: Noobini Santanini or Los Noobinis
Tagline: i i'm rarer than strawberry elephant 100% real no fake
STATS: Rarita=Common | Income=$1/s | Costo=$25 | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | RarestMutation=Phantom(96918) | Update=01 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Ritual=No | Sounds=Noobini_Pizzanini_Sound.wav
--- OVERVIEW ---
Noobini Pizzanini is visually based on the classic R6 rig of Roblox Noob avatar, with a pizza placed on top of its head. It has the most basic designs and animation in the game, visually mirroring its low value and rarity.

Noobini Pizzanini is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Los Noobinis, a Los version of Noobini Pizzanini, isn't obtainable through Ritual. It was instead obtained from the Craft Machine and Cyber Craft prior to the machines removal.

- Noobini Pizzanini has the shortest break even point between Brainrot's income and its cost, taking only 25 seconds in 1x multiplier to break even.

- With the Sleepy Trait applied, Noobini Pizzanini should make $0.5/s. However, the game rounds all incomes, so it actually makes $1/s rounded, therefore Noobini Pizzanini is the only Brainrot that does not get affected by the Sleepy Trait.
- If Noobini Pizzanini had the Sleepy Trait and Bloodrot Mutation, its income would still be $1/s, since Bloodrot Mutation doubled its income into $2/s, before divided by half by Sleepy Trait.

- This also makes Noobini Pizzanini doesn't receive income effect from Gold Mutation, as Noobini Pizzanini with Gold Mutation would make $1.25/s, which rounded into $1/s. Similarly, this makes Noobini Pizzanini with Diamond Mutation makes $2/s by rounding the $1.5/s result from multiplier.

- If you have never purchased a Noobini Pizzanini, the game displays an arrow pointing to one when it spawns, along with the message ‘Go buy a Noobini Pizzanini’.
--- NOOBINI PIZZANINI ---
i i'm rarer than strawberry elephant 100% real no fake

[362/519]
### Nooo My Hotspot
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Nooo_My_Hotspot
Avvisi: Only obtainable during Admin Abuse
Non confondere con: Hotspot (disambiguation), Pot Hotspot, Los Nooo My Hotspotsitos, Los Hotspotsitos, Los Mobilis, Noo my Candy, Noo my Present, Noo my Heart, Noo my Gold, Noo my Eggs, or Noo my examine
Tagline: give me liberty give me fire give me wi-fi or i'll retire
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$1.5M/s | Costo=$500M | Status=Obtainable (Fat Sammy, Admin Abuse) | Ritual=No | Sounds=NoooMyHotspot.mp3,NOOOHOTSPOOOT!!!ahTE.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Nooo My Hotspot is the rarest Taco Tuesday brainrot, and it is a Secret. It can spawn on the Red Carpet with $500M cost and has an income of $1.5M/s.

Nooo My Hotspot is a burrito with black limbs and is sad. It holding a white phone while kneeling, and in front of it is a Wi-Fi signal, symbolizing Wi-Fi connection.

Nooo My Hotspot is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from Fat Sammy with a 2.5% chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Nooo My Hotspot is sometimes referred to as Hotspotini Burrito, due to the popular roblox game, Plants & Brainrots, However, Steal a Brainrot decided to use its most used name.

- All of Nooo My Hotspot's reskins (excluding it's Los version, Los Nooo My Hotspotsitos) have 2 "O"s in the "No", despite Nooo My Hotspot having 3.

- Despite not being a limited quantity, Nooo My Hotspot is considered to be one of if not the rarest Taco Tuesday brainrots, as nobody wants to give Fat Sammy tacos since it is tedious, the chance to get Nooo My Hotspot is only a 2.5%, and sometimes Sammy forgets to spawn Fat Sammy entirely most of the time.

- This is the only "Noo my" brainrot to have the initial in "My" capitalized.
--- NOOO MY HOTSPOT ---
give me liberty give me fire give me wi-fi or i'll retire

[365/519]
### Odin Din Din Dun
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Odin_Din_Din_Dun
Non confondere con: Eggdin Egg Egg Dun, Jacko Jack Jack, Fragola La La La, or Gym Bros
Tagline: Couldn't be cooler
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$75K/s | Costo=$15M | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet, Backrooms Event) | Update=01 | Creator=@noxaasht (previous creator)@SebasMZ30 (current creator) | Sounds=Dindindindun.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Odin Din Din Dun is a Brainrot God. It costs $15M and has an income of $75K/s.

Odin Din Din Dun is an orange with muscular orange limbs and making bodybuilding pose. It wear white-red-black Air Jordans.

Odin Din Din Dun is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From the Red Carpet.

- From the Escape Tsunami LTM.

- From the Backrooms Event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Odin Din Din Dun's full name is 'Udin Din Din Din Dun, Madin Din Din Dun'.
- Udin is a common Indonesian name. It's pronounced as 'woo-din' or 'oh-din' by non-native speaker, akin to the Norse god, hence Odin Din Din Dun.

- You need an Odin Din Din Dun in order to unlock Rebirth 12.

- Odin Din Din Dun is the only Brainrot God without particle effects.

- When mutated, the Odin Din Din Dun has a higher value percentage per Mutation than normal brainrots.

- Odin Din Din Dun used to be the best brainrot in the game, back when Secrets didn't exist during the game launch.

- In the old updates, Odin Din Din Dun’s design was smaller.

- Odin Din Din Dun used to make $350K/s when it was added in-game, but later got nerfed to $75K/s.
--- ODIN DIN DIN DUN ---
Couldn't be cooler

### Orangutini Ananassini
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Orangutini_Ananassini
Tagline: i was ur best friend in june, 2025
STATS: Rarita=Mythic | Income=$2.1K/s | Costo=$400K | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | Update=02 | Creator=@alexey_pigeon | Ritual=No | Sounds=Anananassinisussund.mp3,Oldorange.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Orangutini Ananassini is an animal-food hybrid brainrot. Its concept is about an orangutan fused with a pineapple. The orangutan can visually be seen having the leaves of the pineapple on top of its head, while having a blank stare and having anthropomorphic features. It can be seen having its torso replaced by a giant, oversized, pineapple.

Orangutini Ananassini is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Orangutini Ananassini used to make $1.7K/s until around the Yin & Yang update when it was buffed to $2K/s. When Divine Fuse update was dropped, its income is buffed once again to $2.1K/s.

- Orangutini Ananassini tends to be a material for Mythics in the Craft's machines

- The "Ananasini" part in Orangutini Ananassini's name comes from the Italian word "Ananas", which means "Pinneapple".
- This would make sense because this brainrot is a combination of an orangutan and a pineapple.
--- ORANGUTINI ANANASSINI ---

[369/519]
### Orcalero Orcala
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Orcalero_Orcala
Avvisi: A Lucky Block Brainrot.
Non confondere con: Orcalita Orcala, Los Orcalitos, or Orcaledon
Tagline: tralalero tralala NO NO NO! Orcalero Orcala!
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$100K/s | Costo=$25M | Status=Obtainable (Brainrot God Lucky Block and from the Fishing Event) | Ritual=Yes | Sounds=Orcaleroorcala.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Orcalero Orcala is a Brainrot God that costs $25M and generates $100K/s. It can be obtained from the Brainrot God Lucky Block with a 30% chance.

Orcalero Orcala is similar to Tralalero Tralala, the only difference is that Orcalero Orcala is a cetacean & wears black and white sneakers. Orcalero Orcala also looks the exact same with the Yin Yang Mutation. The only difference is that it removes the studs and makes it look brighter than it was before.

Orcalero Orcala is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Brainrot God Lucky Block.

- Fishing from the Fishing Event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Orcalero Orcala was available to be obtained with the Lava Mutation in Lava Spin.

- Orcalero Orcala has a ritual, which makes its baby Brainrot counterpart, Los Orcalitos spawn, alongside summoning Shark Fin Trait. To start the ritual, four players has to carry or steal Orcalero Orcala, and the players has to be in line horizontally.

- On Sammy's teaser, he said "Next update's SECRET" which most likely implies that Orcalero Orcala was originally planned to be a Secret rarity Brainrot but was later changed before release. Though this could also be a reference to Pot Hotspot, which is a Secret, or he just want to say secret in literal way.

- Despite Orcalero Orcala is described as male in its origin, Orcalero Orcala have a curved dorsal fin instead of triangle one. Male orca is identified with its triangle dorsal fin, while female orca is identified with its curved dorsal fin. This making Orcalero Orcala technically a female Brainrot.

- Orcalero Orcala will receive a plush very soon.
--- ORCALERO ORCALA ---
tralalero tralala NO NO NO! Orcalero Orcala!

[370/519]
### Orcalita Orcala
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Orcalita_Orcala
Avvisi: stub
Non confondere con: Tralalita Tralala, Orcalero Orcala, Los Orcalitos, or Orcaledon
Tagline: waiting for las orcalitas
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$240K/s | Costo=$45M | Status=Obtainable (Fishing, Admin Abuse only) | Ritual=No | Sounds=Orcalita_Orcala_Official_Sound.wav
--- APPEARANCE ---
A pink version of Orcalero Orcala, with a bow tie and a lipstick, wearing Nike shoes, as Orcalero Orcala does. Her scheme is reminiscent of Tralalita Tralala.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Orcalita Orcala was leaked by Sammy with the message "Since everyone was asking for it.”

- Orcalero Orcala is actually a female, signified by the curved fin dorsal. Male orca are identified with its triangle fin dorsal, while female orca are identified with its curved fin dorsal.
- This would technically make Orcalita Orcala the first female reskin of an already female Brainrot.
--- OBTAINMENT ---
Orcalita Orcala could've been obtained from the Craft Machine by the following items:

- 2 Orcalero Orcala

- Tralalita Tralala

- Espresso Signora

When it was brought back to Cyber Craft, it use this recipe:

- Orcalero Orcala

- Tralalita Tralala

- 2 Girafa Celestre

Currently, it is obtainable through Fishing, and was a part of the Aquatic Index. However, Fishing is now Admin Abuse exclusive, as it no longer happens hourly.

[371/519]
### Pakrahmatmamat
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Pakrahmatmamat
Avvisi: stub
Non confondere con: Pakrahmatmatina, Cuadramat and Pakrahmatmamat, or Chrismasmamat
Tagline: wilder than wild woody
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$215K/s | Costo=$37.5M | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | Sounds=Pakrahmatmamatsound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Pakrahmatmamat is a Brainrot God added on August 23, 2025. It costs $37.5M to purchase and produces $215K/s. 

Pakrahmatmamat is a wooden pencil with face on it. It has two detached human feet, and produces scribble and pencil symbols as its particle effects. 

Pakrahmatmamat is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Pakrahmatmamat, along with $100T is needed for the 15th Rebirth.

- Pakrahmatmamat's particle effects briefly form scribble-like symbols during spawning sequences, a detail noted by players after release.

- Its full name is "Pakrahamama-ma-mat-mat-mat-mamatung", but it was shortened to "Pakrahmatmamat".
- Pakrahmatmamat is based on an common Indonesian teacher name, "Pak Rahmat". Rahmat is an Arabic and Indonesian word for "Grace".
--- PAKRAHMATMAMAT ---
wilder than wild woody

### Pancake and Syrup

Avvisi: stub

--- OVERVIEW ---
Pancake and Syrup is a Secret Brainrot that costs $50B (formerly $100B) and generates $125M/s.

Pancake and Syrup appears as a stack of pancakes and a bottle of maple syrup, both have face and legs. The pancake is distressed and the syrup is happy.

Pancake and Syrup is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtaining from buying SAB Merch, as mentioned by Sammy.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Pancake and Syrup was Leaked by Sammy along with 2 brainrots: Hopilikalika Hopilikalako and Rico Dinero.

- This is one of the rarest brainrots in the game, being the second rarest from the now-unavailable DLC codes. It is likely (however unconfirmed) that <500 of these exist in the entire world.
- As of the most recent exist count leak, 379 Pancake and Syrups exist, however this is slightly outdated.

- Just like Rico Dinero and Arcadragon, the Pancake and Syrup yielded 155m/s and cost 100B, but that value was lowered and its price cut in half.

- This Brainrot currently shares the same stats as Antonio and La Secret Combinasion.

[382/519]
### Perochello Lemonchello
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Perochello_Lemonchello
Avvisi: stub
Tagline: La Ultimate Temu Dragon Canneloni 🤑🤑
STATS: Rarita=Epic | Income=$160/s | Costo=$27.5K | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | Sounds=Lemonyummysound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Perochello Lemonchello is an 
Epic Brainrot. Its chance of spawning is about 0.66%. (10/1515)

Perochello Lemonchello is an animal-food hybrid brainrot. It consists of a parrot fused with a lemon. The parrot can be seen colored yellow, with soaring wings, a greyish beak, shining eyes, and two small grey feet. It can be seen having a half-cut lemon encasted into its torso.

Perochello Lemonchello has a chance of appearing on the Red Carpet. It can be purchased for $27.5K. Afterward, the brainrot will head to the buyer's base. However, another player can buy it for 150% of its base cost, and it will change its direction to that player and so on.

The second way of obtaining it is by stealing from another player, which is a Core Feature in the game.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Perochello Lemonchello seems to be based on a Cockatiel, because of the crest and the fact some cockatiels are yellow.

- Perochello Lemonchello is sometimes called the "temu dragon" as it and Dragon Cannelloni have similar animations.

- Perochello Lemonchello has the same eyes as Strawberry Elephant
--- PEROCHELLO LEMONCHELLO ---
La Ultimate Temu Dragon Canneloni 🤑🤑

[383/519]
### Perrito Burrito
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Perrito_Burrito
Avvisi: Limited Quantity Brainrot.
Non confondere con: Chihuanini Taconini, Los Chihuaninis, Burrito Bandito, or Los Burritos
Tagline: Ima eat my Burrito now OH SHOOT MY DOG WAS IN THAT
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$1M/s | Costo=$250M | Status=Unobtainable (Out of Stock) | Ritual=No | Sounds=PerritoBurritosound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Perrito Burrito is a Limited Quantity Secret Brainrot added on September 30, 2025. It costs $250M and generates $1M/s.

Perrito Burrito is an animal-food hybrid Brainrot that appears to be an adorable puppy wrapped inside a burrito. It is most likely inspired by a real-life Dachschund, making it a pun of hot dog.

Perrito Burrito is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From the Taco Truck when it had stock.
- Crafting Recipe
- 1x Chihuanini Taconini

- 1x La Cucaracha

- 1x Job Job Job Sahur

- From Taco Tuesday when Sammy spawned it for everyone.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Perrito Burrito is the Limited Quantity Brainrots with most stock ever, with 2,500,000 Stock.

- On 3 November 2025, at Taco Tuesday Admin Abuse, Sammy gave one Perrito Burrito to everyone who attended the Admin Abuse. This making it the first time a Limited Quantity Brainrot was spawned for everyone, with the second being Caylusaurus.
- This was due to Sammy spawning a Job Job Job Sahur at 30 September 2025, causing many people to craft Perrito Burrito at once, breaking the game server.

- To counter the overabundance of Perrito Burrito, Quesadillo Vampiro was introduced on 21 October 2025, serving as sink for excess Perrito Burrito. Sammy spawned the second Perrito Burrito to every server to help players crafting Quesadillo Vampiro.
--- PERRITO BURRITO ---
Ima eat my Burrito now OH SHOOT MY DOG WAS IN THAT

--- OVERVIEW ---
Pipi Corni is a Common Brainrot that costs $1.75K and generates $14/s.

Pipi Corni appears as a dormouse with its torso replaced by a piece of corn. The dormouse in Pipi Corni is doing the ":3" face.

Pipi Corni is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Fusing it in the 2025 Fuse Machine.

- Fusing it in the 2026 Fuse Machine.

- Fusing it in the Summer Fuse Machine.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Before the 2026 Fuse Machine was released, Pipi Corni was insanely valuable, since the 2025 Fuse Machine was released in Update 10 (when not many players even played the game). Also, since it's a Common, not many people bothered to keep it. But, when the Fuse Machine returned for 2026, it was devalued a ton. Its value suffered even more when it was reintroduced in Summer Fuse.

- Pipi Corni was the first Common Brainrot to come from a Fuse Machine.

- Pipi Corni is the first Common Brainrot to not come from the Red Carpet.

- Pipi Corni along with other fuse brainrots between Common - Legendary were brought back twice in the Fuse Machine and the Summer Fuse.

- Pipi Corni is used in a recipe to craft Los Cornis
--- PIPI CORNI ---
property of Bambi Bambi Bambi

### Pipi Kiwi
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Pipi_Kiwi
Avvisi: part_of_family
Famiglia: Pipi Family
Non confondere con: Raccooni Jandelini, Pipi Corni, Pipi Avocado, Pipi Potato, or Pi Pi Watermelon
Tagline: glorious king (not)
STATS: Rarita=Common | Income=$13/s | Costo=$1.5K | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | Update=01 | Creator=@lifewatching1 | Sounds=Pipikiwi.mp3,Pipi_Kiwi_old_sound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Pipi Kiwi costs $1.5K and makes $13/s.

Pipi Kiwi's appearance consists of a raccoon head, legs with human feet, and a raccoon striped tail, and the torso is a kiwi.

Pipi Kiwi is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Pipi Kiwi is the first Pipi Brainrot in the game.

- The word "pipi" is a Māori word for a baby or infant.

- Pipi Kiwi is the second best Common Brainrot below Pipi Corni, another Pipi Brainrot, and the best Red Carpet Common Brainrot.
- Due to this, Pipi Kiwi with Mutations or Traits has 15% chance to inherit the Mutations and Traits in Fuse Machine, the highest inherit chance reserved only for Brainrot with highest income in their Rarity. Using this knowledge, one can use three Pipi Kiwi with Mutation in Fuse Machine and combining it with Brainrot God to get mutated Mythic, or Secret to get mutated Brainrot God.

Popcuru and Fizzuru are bag of popcorn and cup of soda (also known as fizz in slang, or a fizzy drink) which have faces and two human legs. The popcorn (Popcuru) is happy, and the soda (Fizzuru) is sad, and can be seen crying.

- Popcuru and Fizzuru is based on popcorn and soda, two quintessential food and beverage in cinema theater.

- Popcuru and Fizzuru makes the same income as Bunny and Eggy.

### Pot Hotspot
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Pot_Hotspot
Avvisi: Secret Lucky Block Exclusive.
Non confondere con: Nooo My Hotspot, Los Nooo My Hotspotsitos, John Pork, Los Hotspotsitos, Cupid Hotspot, or Santa Hotspot
Tagline: wiffy pls i need to watch slop
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$2.55M/s | Costo=$600M | Status=Obtainable (Secret Lucky Block) | Ritual=No | Sounds=Pot_Hotspot_Sound.mp3,PotHotspot.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Pot Hotspot resembles a skeletal figure with a phone embedded in his skull. Pot Hotspot has a sad expression while holding a phone. The phone has the Wi-Fi logo and text reading "Wi-Fi" displayed on it.

Pot Hotspot is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Secret Lucky Block.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Pot Hotspot is an Indonesian Brainrot created by TikTok user @dytzz88 on the 8th of March, 2025. The original Brainrot is sometimes referred to as "Hotspot Anomali". Pot Hotspot is meant to be a personification of Wi-Fi freeloaders, especially Wi-Fi from someone's personal hotspot.

- Pot Hotspot has been in 2 combinations, those being La Supreme Combinasion and La Secret Combinasion. This making Pot Hotspot the only Brainrot that become main part of two different Combinasion.
- Coincidentally, Pot Hotspot is on the top of both the Combinasion, serving as head partfor the Combinasion.

- Pot Hotspot's phone for the head has a lighter shade in the La Secret Combinasion than in this brainrot. Pot Hotspot's phone for the head is also bigger in the La Supreme Combinasion than in this brainrot.

Pretzo Robo appears as an orange and blue robot with its torso replaced by a pretzel and having two antennas on its head, accompanied with two crystal shards on its shoulder and having two pretzel mechanical-like shoes. - Crafting Recipe:

- 1x Gattatino Nyanino

- Stealing, a Core Feature.

- SpyderSammy confirmed in one Admin Abuse that there are more Money Money Bros that have been crafted than that of Pretzo Robo.

- It is likely that Pretzo Robo will be buffed. SpyderSammy has responded with "maybe". This is because Pretzo Robo requires Ginger Cisterna, a Santa's Fuse Exclusive Brainrot as its craft material. [408/519]
### Raccooni Jandelini
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Raccooni_Jandelini
Avvisi: Admin War Exclusive
Non confondere con: Pipi Kiwi or Rocco Disco
Tagline: im just a bebeh
STATS: Rarita=Common | Income=$12/s | Costo=$1.3K | Status=Unobtainable (Admin Abuse War, Cyber Craft Machine) | Update=13 | Creator=BRAZILIAN SPYDER | Ritual=No | Sounds=RaccooniJandelinisound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Raccooni Jandelini makes $13/s and costs $1.3K to purchase off the Red Carpet when it was available.

Raccooni Jandelini appears to have a body of a raccoon and a head of a monkey wearing a red-colored hat with a yellow-colored crown around. Raccooni Jandelini's appearance is representing the famous game developer Jandel, and mocking how rare Raccoons are in the Roblox experience Grow A Garden.

Raccooni Jandelini is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying off the Red Carpet when it was spawned in.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Raccooni Jandelini was released during the Admin Abuse War, between Sammy and Jandel, in August 23rd of 2025.
- SpyderSammy used the brainrot Raccooni Jandelini to make fun of Jandel in the Admin Abuse War.

- At the same time, Chimpanzini Spiderini is reverted back to Sammyni Spyderini. This is meant to pit Raccooni Jandelini, a Common Brainrot representing Jandel, and Sammyni Spyderini, a Secret Brainrot representing Sammy.

- Sammy spawned Raccooni Jandelini for 2 days, in August 23rd of 2025 and in August 24th of 2025.

- Raccooni Jandelini is the smallest Brainrot, because he is a raccoon.

- Raccooni Jandelini was stocked inside the Cyber Craft Machine at 5th May 2026 Taco Tuesday by 1K units, costing 4 Noobini Pizzaninis and it sold out in less than a minute.
- This means that a Cyber Raccooni Jandelini is technically possible, as the Cyber Event was running when Sammy added Raccooni Jandelini to the Cyber Craft Machine. This also means that an all Traits Raccooni Jandelini is possible, as you could've fused 4 all Trait Noobinis.

- When Sammy added Raccooni Jandelini in the Cyber Craft Machine, he consistently referring Raccooni Jandelini as "loser", possibly referencing how Grow a Garden, Plants vs. Brainrots, and Garden Horizons, all are Jandel's game, are irrelevant and eclipsed by Steal a Brainrot.

- Raccooni Jandelini was secretly nerfed from $14/s to $12/s for unknown reasons.

- People previously believed this brainrot was rare, until Sammy released the exist counts, dropping all of its demand.
--- RACCOONI JANDELINI ---
im just a bebeh

[410/519]
### Rang Ring Bus
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Rang_Ring_Bus
Avvisi: Full name contains a slur.
Tagline: scary level: 101%
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$6M/s | Costo=$1.1B | Status=Obtainable (Admin Abuse) | Sounds=Ranringbusususususmp3.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Rang Ring Bus is a Secret Brainrot that costs $1.1B and has an income of $6M/s. It is exclusive to the Panjat Pinang event.

Rang Ring Bus is a black bus, with a human face in the front, and 6 pairs of human legs on its sides.

Rang Ring Bus is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtaining it from the Panjat Pinang with a 1% chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Based on the original image, Rang Ring Bus appears to be a Mercedes-Benz Tourismo, a common type of bus used by many bus and travel company in Indonesia.

- Rang Ring Bus' full name is "Rang Ring Reng Bus Ireng," the name was truncated to make it short.
- Ireng means "black" in Javanese

- In Indonesian "hitam" means black (silent H) when describing the color.

- The text on the license plate reads “STEAL516”, with 516 referring to May 16th 2025, the day Steal a Brainrot was released.

- The eyes, specifically the pupils of Rang Ring Bus change depend on Mutation, more notably Galaxy and Yin Yang.
--- RANG RING BUS ---
scary level: 101%

[411/519]
### Rebirth
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Rebirth
--- TRIVIA ---
- Before Rebirth 14 was added, Rebirth 8 required a Cocofanto Elefanto, and Rebirth 13 a Ballerino Lololo. Cocofanto Elefanto was upgraded to Rebirth 9 and all brainrots got downgraded to one rebirth down after Rebirth 14 was added.
- Ballerino Lololo was removed from the rebirths since Rebirth 14 was added, due to its lower spawn rate compared to high-tier Brainrot God,such as Tractoro Dinosauro, Cacasito Satalito, Pakrahmatmamat, Aquanaut, and even La Vacca Saturno Saturnita, a Secret.

- Between Rebirths 5-16 you only need 1 brainrot!

- Rebirth 1 used to need a Tung Tung Tung Sahur, but was replaced with a Gangster Footera when Noxa copyright claimed Tung Tung Tung Sahur. This is because every Tung Tung Tung Sahur were replaced by Gangster Footera upon removal.

- 

- Rebirth 9 is the first rebirth to require a Brainrot God as a requirement, and Rebirth 15 is the final rebirth to use a Brainrot God as its requirement.

- Rebirth 8 is the final rebirth to use a Mythic as its requirement.

- Rebirth 11 is the final rebirth to give you a slap.
- If you count the Gummy Bear as a slap, Rebirth 14 would be the last rebirth to give you a slap

- Rebirth 16 is the first rebirth to use a Secret as its requirement.

- Both Common and OG rarities are not required for rebirthing due to being very easy or very difficult to get.

- Any Brainrots that are still heading to your base will go back to the red carpet once you rebirth.

- If someone is stealing a brainrot and the person rebirths, the brainrot disappears.

- Rebirth 1 does not give an additional slot and is the only rebirth that doesn't.

- Rebirth 2 gives the base a second floor, and Rebirth 10 gives the base the third floor, which is useful in keeping valuable Brainrots safe, as it is hard to steal a Brainrot kept at the higher floor.

- Rebirth 17 is the first Rebirth to require 2 secrets. It is also the first double-digit rebirth to require 2 brainrots.
- It was reverted in Rebirth 18 as the requirement got buffed to only needing 1 brainrot.
--- STRATEGIES ---
- Before rebirthing, it's recommended to let a trusted person or alternative account (on another device or tab) steal your most valuable brainrots. This way, when you rebirth, you can get them back and regain your progress.

- You can also collect the next rebirth(s)' requirements and keep them on an alternate account or give it to a trusted person and get it back whenever you want. This will save your time.

- It's smart to look at this page then collect all of the required Brainrots all at once, so you can rebirth faster! (Store them on an alt account, using your phone or a laptop/computer.)

--------------------------------------------------

[412/519]
### Red Carpet
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Red_Carpet
--- OVERVIEW ---
The Red Carpet is a studded carpet where Brainrots spawn and walk across to the other side. People can buy Brainrots from it.

Also known as the Conveyor Belt. Most of the Brainrots in the game are coming out from the Cave (the entrance), walking down the Red Carpet, before disappeared in other end of Red Carpet.
--- APPEARANCE ---
The Red Carpet is a studded red carpet, It can change colors and even multiply during Events & Admin Abuse.
--- TRIVIA ---
- During Christmas, Gold Elf was the only brainrot that doesn’t have a RoadWeight. Instead, it had a 1/500 (0.2%) chance of spawning in on the red carpet for every brainrot that spawns.

- Cooki and Milki used to be obtainable on the red carpet before being put into Santa's Fuse.
--- MECHANICS ---
Brainrots come walking in down the red carpet. You can buy one, and the Brainrot will go to your base. However, other people can buy it when it walks to your base and can buy it for 150% of its base cost, and it will change its direction to that player and so on. Any Brainrot from any rarity can come.

When a Brainrot God, Secret, Lucky Block, or OG brainrot spawns, there will be an in-game announcement. A Brainrot God or Secret announcement will only appear in your server, while OG announcement will also be shown globally through Live Spawns panel next to the entrance. Mythic Lucky Blocks have no announcement when spawned.
--- SPAWN RATES ---
These spawn rates are the real ones extracted from the game files. These are internally named as "RoadWeight" and these are not % or X/X chances (if it was so, there would be only Noobini Pizzanini that can spawn in the red carpet due to its spawn rate that is 100, which wouldn't make sense. But as we know, the higher the value, the more often a brainrot will spawn.) However, since from September 6th, 2025 the OG spawn rates are stored in ServerStorage folder which can't be extracted by the decompilers, the ones for the latest OG brainrots can't be 100% exact (if a spawn rate is an estimation, it'll be mentioned).

#### Guarranted brainrots after a certain time:

- Legendary: 5 minutes

- Mythic: 15 minutes

- Brainrot God: 45 minutes (Estimated due to the fact that they spawn easier than a few months ago even if their spawn rates were the same in the game files.)

#### RoadWeights of some Mutations :

- Gold : 7

- Diamond : 3

- Rainbow : 0.2
--- STRATEGIES ---
Good Brainrots don't usually spawn in the red carpet, but when they do, you'll know, since their name will be said aloud. Brainrot God Lucky Blocks, Secret Lucky Blocks, OG, and Secret will be mentioned in chat. If you are playing in public servers, focus on stealing from other player's bases.

When an Admin Abuse happens, Sammy will increase the Server Luck and spawn a lot of weathers/events which can give special Traits to Brainrots making them even more valuable. He will also occasionally spawn good Brainrots, so make sure you watch out.

The brainrot most spawned by Sammy is the La Vacca Saturno Saturnita. He says "someone said la vaca" before spawning it. La Vacca Saturno Saturnita can also be obtained from the red carpet, if you're lucky.

--- OVERVIEW ---
Ref Ref Ref Sahur is a Secret brainrot that costs $650M and generates $2.7M/s.

Ref Ref Ref Sahur appears as a metal pipe with a human face, arms, and legs. It is wearing a referee's outfit, which includes the hat and the shirt/pants. It is wearing black gloves, holds a yellow checkered flag and has a gray whistle in its mouth.

- Obtaining when a Red Card is given out in a live World Cup match.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.

- This is the 3rd reskin of To to to Sahur. The others Being Cupid Cupid Sahur and Ho Ho Ho Sahur.

Reindeer Tralala is/was obtained from the following ways:

### Reinito Sleighito
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Reinito_Sleighito
Avvisi: Festive Lucky Block exclusive.

--- OVERVIEW ---
Reinito Sleighito is a Secret brainrot that was released along with the Festive Lucky Block. It costs $60B and generates $140M/s.

Reinito Sleighito is an animal-vehicle hybrid brainrot that takes the appearence of a brown deer mixed with a sleigh. The horns are colored red and white akin to candy cane, and Reinito Sleighito carries colorful present on its trunk.

Reinito Sleighito is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtained from the Festive Lucky Block with a 0.1% chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Reinito Sleighito is the brainrot with the most 1 of 1's. It has three 1 of 1's. (Divine, Cyber, Phantom)

- Reinito Sleighito's former name was "Slitta Sprinta" according to the original poll where it was mentioned in.

- Reinito Sleighito is the rarest brainrot from Festive Lucky Block.

- Reinito Sleighito has low value because sometimes Sammy brings back the North Pole Event.
- Since North Pole Event has begun to brought back more frequently, it is possible to obtain Reinito Sleighito in every Mutations if you managed to obtain mutated Festive Lucky Block.

- Due to North Pole Event being held during the 1 Year anniversary, Reinito Sleighito possibly has existing 1YR and Cyber versions.
--- REINITO SLEIGHITO ---
Dashing through the snow...

### Rhino Helicopterino
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Rhino_Helicopterino

--- OVERVIEW ---
Rhino Helicopterino is a Mythic brainrot from the Craft Machine that generates $11K/s and costs $4.1M. 

Rhino Helicopterino is a rhino which is fused with a helicopter, which is green. The rhino is grey, and his forelimbs and hindlimbs are visible; The blades of the helicopter are black. 

Rhino Helicopterino is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting from the Craft Machine
- Crafting Recipe:
- 2x Rhino Toasterino

- 2x Bombardiro Crocodilo

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Rhino Helicopterino is the only Mythic Brainrot from the Craft Machine to be added during the Extinct Event.

- Rhino Helicopterino could get buffed to around $30M/s due to it having around the same exist count as a Dug dug dug.
- Due to this demand, on Taco Tuesday on the 14th of April, SpyderSammy made a poll of who should get buffed between Centrucci Nuclucci or Rhino Helicopterino, but sadly Centrucci Nuclucci won by 200K votes.

- Rhino Helicopterino model in Index menu is very tiny compared to other Brainrots.

- Alot of players have sold this brainrot because they thought it was not needed for future use and that it was only done for indexing purposes. This causes the exist count of said brainrot to drop significantly, potentially increasing it's value and demand, notably for collectors.
--- RHINO HELICOPTERINO ---
I might be on your alt and you don't know it...

[417/519]
### Rhino Toasterino
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Rhino_Toasterino
Avvisi: stub
Non confondere con: Rhino Helicopterino
Tagline: Rhino Helicopterino's poorer brother
STATS: Rarita=Mythic | Income=$2.15K/s | Costo=$450K | Status=Obtainable | Sounds=Sound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Rhino Toasterino is a Mythic Brainrot. It costs $450K and has a base income of $2.15K/s.

### Rico Dinero
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Rico_Dinero

--- OVERVIEW ---
Rico Dinero is a Brainrot leaked by SpyderSammy in the Community Server. It currently costs $7.5B and has a base income of $42.5M/s.

Rico Dinero is an anthropomorphic Wallet. It has a happy and delightful expression, along with grey boots and a stack of bills and coins stored.

Rico Dinero is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtaining from buying SAB Merch, as mentioned by SpyderSammy.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- While Rico Dinero was seen in a poll previously, making it a Poll Brainrot, many of Steal a Brainrot competitor games has similar anthropomorphic Wallet concept.
- On Plants vs. Brainrots, the wallet Brainrot is known as Smug Walletino.

- On Break a Lucky Block, the wallet Brainrot is known as Walletini No Monini.

- Rico Dinero was Leaked alongside Pancake and Syrup and Hopilikalika Hopilikalako.

- Rico Dinero is Spanish word translated to English as "Plenty of Money", hence the wallet design.

- Rico Dinero had its income be leaked a few hours before it originally released, having $55M/s as income, however it has been changed to $42.5M/s when it was released.

- This Brainrot has the same stats as Ketchuru and Musturu, Tirilikalika Tirilikalako, and Gym Bros and possibly Los Tangcitos.

Sammyni Fattini resembles the game creator SpyderSammy, more specifically his variant called "Fat Sammy". Sammyni Fattini wears the Spyder Chain, along with white headphones and a red tophat. Sammyni Fattini wears a red shirt, accompanied by red pants, and red shoes. Sammyni Fattini holds a taco, while smiling.

Sammyni Fattini is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Sammyni Fattini is based off of the Fat Sammy event usually seen during Taco Tuesday which explains why he holds a taco. This making Sammyni Fattini is the first Brainrot to be based on an Events.

- Sammyni Fattini has differences between its model and Fat Sammy, its inspiration.

- For some reason, he does not have his signature spider on his eye like the original. However, a Sammyni Fattini with Spider Trait makes it has the signature spider on his eye.

- He does not have the white band on his hat aswell as he does not have red katanas on his back, plus the L and R are missing from the Clockwork Headphones.

- This brainrot was used for Los Admins.

Sammyni Spyderini appears to be a spider with a yellow head and the game's developer, SpyderSammy's face and 6 red and black legs. Sammyni Spyderini also produces a cobweb aura.

Sammyni Spyderini is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Sammyni Spyderini's description is "Un Ragno Molto Molto Velenoso E Molto Spaventoso", which translates to "A very, very poisonous and very scary spider" in Italian.

- Sammyni Spyderini is the only brainrot in the index when you put your finger or cursor over it, it literally says nothing.

- Sammyni Spyderini was the first brainrot obtainable through sammy spawning it in Admin Abuse

- 1x Brri Brri Bicus Dicus Bombicus

- 1x Glorbo Fruttodrillo

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- At the time of Signore Carapace's debut, barely anyone has this Brainrot, because it required 2x Penguino Cocosino, which almost nobody had back then since Penguino Cocosino being considered bad in income.
- Penguino Cocosino is also a rare Epic from Fuse Machine, making it even harder to obtain. Furthermore, since Craft Machine was introduced after Fuse Machine, there's no way to obtain new Penguino Cocosino for crafting Signore Carapace. Even when Penguino Cocosino made its return in 2026 Fuse Machine, it was returned 2 months after Craft Machine removal, of which Signore Carapace was unobtainable by that time.

- Crafting Signore Carapace was also considered not worth it, since the comparison between its income and its material income are $-225/s.

- This contributes to Signore Carapace becoming the 3rd rarest Brainrot with only 353 existing. 2nd place goes to Kraken with 280 existing, and 1st place goes to Headless Horseman with 54 existing.

- When Signore Carapace got its first buff, Signore Carapace got the 2nd biggest buff (with the first being Tirilikalika Tirilikalako) in all of Steal A Brainrot history, having its income increased from $1.3K/s all the way to $105M/s, which the new income makes roughly 80,769x more than original, beating Tung Tung Tung Sahur's record of 60,000x and just right below Tirilikalika Tirilikalako's record of around 94,444x.
- After Signore Carapace's second buff, that buffed its income from $105M/s to $275M/s, Signore Carapace got the biggest buff in all of Steal a Brainrot history, which the new income makes roughly 211,538x more than original.

- When Signore Carapace got buffed from a Legendary to a Secret, its size has now also changed to be much more larger to fit the size standard of Secret Brainrot.

- Though the dragon brainrots are the best secrets, Signore Caparace makes more than Dragon Cannelloni.

- Signore Carapace is one of five buffed brainrots on Update 40.
--- SIGNORE CARAPACE ---
Lil bro finally graduated 🥹

[438/519]
### Skibidi Toilet
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Skibidi_Toilet
Non confondere con: Spaghetti Tualetti, Rosetti Tualetti, Los Spaghettis, or Toiletto Focaccino
Tagline: skibidi dop dop yes yes
STATS: Rarita=OG | Income=$450M/s | Costo=$450B | Status=Obtainable | RarestMutation=Cyber(7) | Update=31 | Creator=Alexey Gerasimov (@DaFuq!?Boom!) | Ritual=No | Sounds=SkibidiToilet.mp3,Skibidi_Toilet_spawn_effect.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Skibidi Toilet has an income of $450M/s and costs $450B.

Skibidi Toilet is a white toilet with human head sprouted from toilet bowl. The human head has short black hair and black eyes.

Skibidi Toilet is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
This section is a trivia section. Please relocate any relevant information into other sections of the article.

- Skibidi Toilet has been buffed 3 times; From $300M/s,- $350M/s,- $400M/s, and finally $450M/s.

- Skibidi Toilet comes from a YouTube webseries of the same name made by Alexey Gerasimov (A.K.A DaFuq!?Boom!) on February 7th, 2023 in Source Filmmaker (SFM) animation software by Valve, and no AI was used in the making, technically making it an OG.
- After Invisible Narratives is taking over, Skibidi Toilet is made in Unreal Engine, which caused outrage in the Skibidi Toilet community.

- SpyderSammy has hinted at adding Skibidi Toilet many times:
- It was first hinted by him in the September 20th Admin Abuse, although he may also have referred to Toiletto Focaccino, who was released shortly after.

- It was then also hinted in the 4th of November Admin Abuse when Sammy announced "🚽🚽🚽" and then said "new OG soon?".

- It was then confirmed in the December 6th Admin Abuse for the Santa's Fuse, first, saying "Guess who is the next OG?", after replying, "🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽🚽", confirming that it is the next OG coming.

- On December 8th, SpyderSammy anounced in the official Discord server fr Steal a Brainrot that Skibidi Toilet will be arriving soon to the game.

- On December 15, 2025 at 2:20PM EST, Sammy released a poll on the Community Server relating to the rarity of Skibidi Toilet, since many people argued that it shouldn't be an OG due to how it was made in 2023, being more recent than Strawberry Elephant and Meowl. however it was chosen that it would be an OG.

- The decision to include Skibidi Toilet in Steal a Brainrot was a collaborative effort between SpyderSammy and Adam Goodman, CEO of Invisible Narratives, the company that owns Skibidi Toilet's IP. Although the issue has been met with controversy over the issue, fans have expressed displeasure with Invisible Narratives' decision.

- Skibidi Toilet's walking animation is similar to that of Toiletto Focaccino.

- Skibidi Toilet's spawn sound is similar to the sound that is heard when you flush a toilet.
- Additionally, this is one of the causes of Skibidi Toilet's death in the original series.
--- SKIBIDI TOILET ---
skibidi dop dop yes yes

- He is the first Brainrot variant that makes less than their original counterpart that is not Los brainrots.

- Skull Skull Skull is the only non-Aquatic Index Halloween brainrot obtainable outside of Halloween event, due to his obtain requirement was moved from Grave Event to Escape Tsunami LTM, held from 24/01/2026 at 3:00PM EST to 04/04/2026 at 5:00PM EST.

### Spyder Elephant

Non confondere con: Strawberry Elephant

--- OVERVIEW ---
Spyder Elephant is a OG brainrot that was released during the 1 Year Anniversary in Update 51.

Spyder Elephant has the same appearance as Strawberry Elephant, except its body is covered with VVS diamonds, like the Spyder Chain, instead of strawberry skin.

Spyder Elephant is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Purchasing the Spyder Chain from Spyder Simulators.
--- TRIVIA ---
This section is a trivia section. Please relocate any relevant information into other sections of the article.

- Spyder Elephant is the first unstealable Brainrot, and due to this, it is hidden from the Index. Spyder Elephant is also the first ever OG to be obtained by using Robux.
- Spyder Elephant is also the only Brainrot that can't be traded due to this unique feature, though it can be traded technically by using the UGC Trading Feature bundled with Roblox Plus, since the ownership of Spyder Elephant is bound to a Roblox accessory.

- Considering  100 is equal to $1 USD, the estimated minimum cost to bought a Spyder Elephant is $50,000 USD, assuming it was bought when the accessory price was still  5,000,000.

- Spyder Elephant is the only Brainrot to have a trait instantly added to the Brainrot when obtained. A Spyder Elephant comes with the Spider trait applied on it.

- Since there are only 25 Spyder Chain that are on sale, only 25 Spyder Elephant will ever exist in the game.

- This also makes it the RAREST Brainrot in the game, taking Headless Horseman's place.

- Spyder Elephant is the best Brainrot in the game, giving $1B/s or $4.5B/s considering every Spyder Elephant has Spider trait. This making Spyder Elephant is the first Brainrot that generates at least a billion.

- Spyder Elephant is the first reskin of an OG. Interestingly, Spyder Elephant is the reskin of Strawberry Elephant, the first OG in Steal a Brainrot.

- Spyder Elephant shares the Strawberry Event, and its Sound Effects with Strawberry Elephant.
- It shares the Strawberry Event, because for an unknown reason when it spawns from an Admin, the event starts too.

- Spyder Elephant's exist counts have been leaked, there is 14 existing right now. This means 11 owners of the Spyder Chain haven't joined the game yet, as the Spyder Elephant is only given if the player is detected to have the item equipped or in their Accessory inventory.

- Spyder Elephant is the most expensive brainrot by Robux, as the Spyder Chain is  5,000,000, Beating Celestial Pegasus' Record of  4,798,000.
--- SPYDER ELEPHANT ---
With you forever…

- Steakini Fattini is the first Brainrot in the game that is based on a streamer.

- Steakini Fattini is a Limited Quantity Brainrots, with 50,000 stock on start and another 50,000 stock after the first stock are out.

- Before the debut, Steak spawned Steakini Fattini with the the traits and Mutations in the table below.

Stoppo Luminino is an exclusive Mythic Brainrot that could only be obtained through the Brainrot Trader and the Brainrot Dealer.

Stoppo Luminino takes the appearance of a traffic light, holding a stop sign. It’s coloured light grey with some black gradients. It wears brown boots and a pair of white gloves. The green light has a happy face, the yellow one is disjoyous, and the red one is furious.

[455/519]
### Strawberry Elephant
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Strawberry_Elephant
Non confondere con: Spyder Elephant, Lirilì Larilà, Cocofanto Elefanto, Strawberrelli Flamengelli, Strawberrita, or Elefanto Frigo
Tagline: And on and on we'll go!
STATS: Rarita=OG | Income=$750M/s | Costo=$750B | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | RarestMutation=Phantom(1) | RarestTrait=Spider(34) | Update=14 | Creator=mzic2403 | Ritual=No | Sounds=Strawberry_Elephanta.mp3,Strawberry_Elephant_Spawns.wav
--- OVERVIEW ---
Strawberry Elephant is an OG brainrot that released on 8/30/25. It can be obtained on the Red Carpet for it to spawn with an extremely low chance.

Strawberry Elephant is an elephant but with strawberry skin as its skin.

Strawberry Elephant is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Getting it from Codes.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
This section is a trivia section. Please relocate any relevant information into other sections of the article.

- Strawberry Elephant is the second best Brainrot in the whole game. right before Spyder Elephant. To maintain this status, Strawberry Elephant has been buffed 6 times; it went from $250M/s - $300M/s - $350M/s - $500M/s - $550M/s - $750M/s. It was also the biggest addition to income adding it by $500M/s.
- This Brainrot has been buffed the most times.

- If taking Spyder Elephant, which was added in Update 51 into account, Strawberry Elephant used to be the best Brainrot in the whole game. However, since Spyder Elephant is an Exclusive Brainrot, Strawberry Elephant is still the best Brainrot in the whole game.

- Strawberry Elephant was first made in 2007 by a user named mzic2403 in a Photoshop competition in worth1000 (now Design Crowd), with the prompt being "Hide an Elephant!".
- Strawberry Elephant would then gained attention in 2023 in form of brainrot memes about it, usually with caption "Have a strawberry morning" in Arabic added on its image. In 2025, Sammy added it as an OG.

- Strawberry Elephant is usually accompanied and associated with the song "On & On", which is why its very iconic phrase is "and on and on we'll go".

- According to the Book in the Trade Plaza, it has 1270 Strawberry Elephants, including:
- 574 Gold, 267 Diamond, 83 Rainbow, 30 Candy, 12 Lava, 13 Galaxy, 15 Yin-YangYin Yang, 27 Radioactive

, 22 Cursed, 26 Divine, 3 CyberCyber, and 1 Phantom.
--- STRAWBERRY ELEPHANT ---
And on and on we'll go!

--- TRIVIA ---
This section is a trivia section. Please relocate any relevant information into other sections of the article.

- Described as a fearsome "tough soldier" and a "heroine", she is the companion of Bombardiro Crocodilo and wife of Glorbo Fruttodrillo according to the lore on the actual Italian Brainrot Wiki.
- To reflect her gender in the lore, its original name which is "Svivino Bombombino" is renamed as Svinina Bombardino in Steal a Brainrot.

- The Bombardiro Crocodilo's in the Bombardiro Raid drop Svinina Bombardino's. If they touch the ground, they explode; if they touch a Brainrot, they get a trait.

- Svinina Bombardino is one of the only Common Brainrots to be female, along with Pipi Corni.

### Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Ta_Ta_Ta_Ta_Sahur
Non confondere con: Tung Tung Tung Sahur, Ti Ti Ti Sahur, Te Te Te Sahur, Job Job Job Sahur, La Sahur Combinasion, Tictac Sahur, Bambu Bambu Sahur, Pop Pop Sahur, Karker Sahur, Bunny Bunny Bunny Sahur or To To To Sahur
Tagline: The Guy from The Beauty and the Beast...
STATS: Rarita=Rare | Income=$55/s | Costo=$7.5K | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | Update=01 | Creator=@__chenesacc__ | Sounds=Tatatatatatatatatatsahur.mp3,Ta_Ta_Ta_Sahur_Audio.wav,TaSahurVl.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur is a Rare Brainrot. It costs $7.5K and generates $55/s.
--- APPEARANCE ---
Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur appears to be a brown teapot, with a concerned expression including big blue eyes. It has human legs on the bottom, and a human hand connected to its handle.

Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur is an Indonesian Brainrot with similar theme as Tung Tung Tung Sahur, an anthropomorphic brown object that roaming in the dawn, but not created by @noxaasht, the creator of Tung Tung Tung Sahur. Due to this, Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur is the first Tung Tung Tung Sahur clone.
- Since Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur's owner, @__chenesacc__, doesn't put Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur under copyright, this made Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur doesn't have the same threat of being removed unlike Tung Tung Tung Sahur, that is removed twice.

- Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur is the only Sahur that has four syllabes before "Sahur".
--- TA TA TA TA SAHUR ---
The Guy from The Beauty and the Beast...

[463/519]
### Tacorillo Crocodillo
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Tacorillo_Crocodillo
Avvisi: stub, Limited Quantity Brainrot
Tagline: beware the swamp
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$12.5M/s | Costo=$1.5B | Status=Unobtainable (Out of Stock) | Ritual=No | Sounds=Tacorillo_Crocodillo_sOUND.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Tacorillo Crocodilo is a bright green crocodile with a lighter underbelly and prominent scales. Tacorillo Crocodillo wears a large, colorful Mexican hat and brown sandals. His tail has a peculiar layered design reminiscent of meat, tomato, cheese, and lettuce.

Tacorillo Crocodillo is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtaining from Taco Truck.
- Crafting Recipe:
- 1x Quesadilla Crocodila

- 1x Burrito Bandito

- 1x Los Quesadillas

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Sammy removed Tacorillo Crocodilo from the Taco Truck despite it still being in stock, this is mainly due to the fact that La Lucky Grande took its place. However when La Lucky Grande ran out of stock, Sammy said that the taco truck had "no tacos left" marking the end of Tacorillo Crocodilo's appearance.
- This is mainly because Tacorillo Crocodilo has little to no demand and incentive to craft, since its material and stock are very abundant for a Limited Quantity Brainrots.

- Tacorillo Crocodilo initially was stocked by 1,000,000, however it was taken off from Taco Truck when it was still ~400,000 left in stock.

- While many Taco themed Brainrots has clear taco design in its design, Tacorillo Crocodilo name comes from its taco-like back and tail, which is subtler than most Taco themed Brainrots.
--- TACORILLO CROCODILLO ---
beware the swamp

- Tacorita Bicicleta is the Limited Quantity Brainrots with the second most amount of stock, which is 1,000,000 on stock. To solve Tacorita Bicicleta overabundance, Los Tacoritas was introduced later on as sink for excess Tacorita Bicicleta.

### Tictac Sahur
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Tictac_Sahur

Tagline: The Underappreciated Club: you're appreciated enough.

--- OVERVIEW ---
Tictac Sahur is a Secret Brainrot that costs $6B and gives $37.5M/s.

Tictac Sahur is an anthropomorphic brown analog alarm clock with gray bells and hammer. It has face with serious stare and a moustache, and is riding an unicycle. Tictac Sahur hasa rotating aura in the form of antique clock pattern behind it. 

Tictac Sahur is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying it from the Red Carpet.

- Trading with Someone In the Trading Plaza.

- When Sammy spawns it (Sammy only spawned it once on Easter, For La Easter Grande).

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Tictac Sahur was confirmed in Roblox/Discord along with Dug dug dug, Sigma Girl, To to to Sahur and Elefanto Frigo.

- Tictac Sahur makes the 2nd most income per second out of the Sahur Brainrots, and is the 2nd rarest out of any Sahur Brainrot, behind Jolly Jolly Sahur, a reskin of Tictac Sahur.

- Even though the income is worse than that of Garama and Madundung, Tictac Sahur's RoadWeight is lower, meaning it has a lower spawn chance. The same goes for Tang Tang Keletang, Ketupat Kepat, Ketchuru and Musturu, and Lavadorito Spinito. (Nuclearo Dinossauro is an exception since its RoadWeight is the same as Garama and Madundung's)

- Tictac Sahur is a material for Nacho Spyder and La Easter Grande, making Tictac Sahur very valuable when these brainrots were on stock. As such, this brainrot is the first $30M/s brainrot that consistently used as craft material for Limited Quantity Brainrots.

--- OVERVIEW ---
Tirilikalika Tirilikalako is a Secret Brainrot that makes $42.5M/s and costs $7.5B and was formerly a Legendary brainrot. It costed $75K and generated $450/s before getting buffed.

Tirilikalika Tirilikalako appears to be a chicken with an air conditioner for a body. It also has robot legs and a cord dangling off of its body.

Tirilikalika Tirilikalako is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Crafting it in the Craft Machine, which is no longer available.
- Crafting Recipe:
- 1x Cacto Hipopotamo

- 1x Penguino Cocosino

- 2x Cappuccino Assassino

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- At the time of Tirilikalika Tirilikalako's debut, barely anyone has this brainrot, because it required one Penguino Cocosino, which almost nobody had back then since Penguino Cocosino being considered bad in income.
- Penguino Cocosino is also a rare Epic from Fuse Machine, making it even harder to obtain. Furthermore, since Craft Machine was introduced after Fuse Machine, there's no way to obtain new Penguino Cocosino for crafting Tirilikalika Tirilikalako. Even when Penguino Cocosino made its return in 2026 Fuse Machine, it was returned 2 months after Craft Machine removal, of which Tirilikalika Tirilikalako was unobtainable by that time.

- Crafting Tirilikalika Tirilikalako was also considered not worth it, since the comparison between its income and its material income are $-50/s.

- Tirilikalika Tirilikalako used to be a Legendary Brainrot that made $450/s and costed $75K to purchase.

- Tirilikalika Tirilikalako is one of five buffed brainrots on Update 40.

- Tirilikalika Tirilikalako has one the longest names in the game. Due to this, it's one of the few Brainrots in the game that have 2-second long TTS sound.

- Tirilikalika Tirilikalako is the first Brainrot to be released that is based on a chicken.

- As of February 28, 2026, Tirilikalika Tirilikalako now makes nearly 94,444x the income than before, making Tirilikalika Tirilikalako receive one of the biggest buffs ever out of every Brainrot in the entire game, before Signore Carapace got its second buff

- 0 Tirilikalika Tirilikalako's Exist With The Fireworks

- Tirlikalika tirlilikaliko has 8,111 existing, making it lose value by a small bit, this is because before the exist counts where fixed it used to show 4,849.

- Tirilikalika Tirilikalako has an Easter reskin called Hopilikalika Hopilikalako. You could have crafted Kalika Bros using Tirilikalika Tirilikalako and Hopilikalika Hopilikalako.

--- TRIVIA ---
- Toiletto Focaccino was released on September 27th, 2025 3PM EST along with other brainrots like Money Money Puggy & Tang Tang Keletang.

- Toiletto Focaccino full name is "Tre Tigri Triste Fanno Tripli Tric Trac Tra Tre Tronchini Tristi".
- Tre Tigri Triste means "Three Sad Tigers". It's a popular Brazilian tongue twister, since Toiletto Focaccino's creator, @ofuscabreno, is Brazilian.

- Toiletto Focaccino is the most expensive Mythic brainrot that can be obtained from the Red Carpet.

- Toiletto Focaccino has the same spawn chance as Cocofanto Elefanto and Mythic Lucky Block to spawn on the Red Carpet.

--- OVERVIEW ---
Tralaledon is a Secret brainrot that was added on September 6, 2025. It costs $3B, and has a base income of $27.5M/s

Tralaledon is a resemblance of Tralalero Tralala, but instead in a mutated version. Its depicted as a stereotypical megalodon, with two shining, black eyes, accompanied by sharp teeth, sharp black claws, fins, and a blue and white scheme.

Tralaledon is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Crafting it in the Craft Machine.
- Crafting Recipe:
- 3x Tralalero Tralala.

- 1x Nuclearo Dinossauro.

- Getting it from Fishing with a relatively low chance.

- Tralaledon is a brainrot that is in the Aquatic Index and can be obtained via Fishing.

- It's a high-tier Brainrot with medium demand. While many people seek it out for its rarity and design, there are few units available. Its rarity significantly decreases if Sammy hosts the fishing event. As a result, its demand has been decreasing, which is why it's not as well-remembered as Los Bros, Los Primos, or La Sahur Combinasion.

- Tralaledon is the most valuable member of the Megalodon family despite producing the least amount of income.

[490/519]
### Tralalero Tralala
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Tralalero_Tralala
Tagline: the brainrot that started it all.
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$50K/s | Costo=$10M | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | RarestMutation=Bloodrot(70318) | Ritual=No | Sounds=Tralalelo_Tralala.mp3,Tralala.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Tralalero Tralala is a Brainrot God Brainrot, with a cost of $10M and an income of $50K/s. 

Tralalero Tralala is a blue shark with 3 elongated side fins creating legs. It wears blue shoes, has a blank stare, and no visible teeth. 

While Tralalero Tralala is a grey shark, the shade can be perceived as blue, resulting on many portrayal of Tralalero Tralala as blue shark. 

Tralalero Tralala is/was obtained from the following ways:

- From the Red Carpet.

- From the Fishing Event.

- From the Escape Tsunami LTM.

- From the Backrooms Event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Tralalero Tralala was the first Brainrot to have a Los version.

- Tralalero Tralala is shown as one of the DJs in the concert event as a realistic version along with Chimpanzini Bananini, and replaced Tung Tung Tung Sahur in the center after he was removed.

- Tralalero Tralala is notorious for its dialogue which contained blasphemy in Christianity and Islam which is considered offensive in religious laws.

- Tralalero Tralala is one of the first Brainrot God in the game, alongside Cocofanto Elefanto. Both are added on Update 01.

- Many people who played before the Bloodmoon Event says that Tralalero Tralala did $200K/s.
- This may have been the old multiplier of the Bloodrot mutation was 4x multiplier before changed to 2x, but this is very unlikely.

- Tralalero Tralala is over a year old now. This is because Tralalero Tralala is the first Italian Brainrot ever made, debuted on January 13th, 2025.

- Tralalero Tralala, Matteo, and Mastodontico Telepiedone are the only Brainrot God that consistently have seasonal variants.
- On Halloween, their counterparts are Zombie Tralala, Frankentteo, and Telemorte respectively.

- On Christmas, their counterparts are Reindeer Tralala, Santteo, and Chimnino respectively.

- On Easter, their counterparts are Bunny Tralala, Buntteo, and Baskito respectively.

- For each of their Brainrot variant, Tralalero Tralala variant always generated the lowest income, with Matteo variant generating higher income than Tralalero Tralala variant, but lower than Mastodontico Telepiedone variant, which always generates the highest income out of the three.
--- TRALALERO TRALALA ---
the brainrot that started it all.
--- RAINBOW MACHINE NPC ---
Tralalero was an old NPC that resembled the old Rainbow Tralalero Tralala. It was used for the Rainbow Machine's debut and has never returned since its removal.

Though the Rainbow Machine Event can be activated through Admin Abuse, the Rainbow Machine and Tralalero do not return with it during the event, since they were part of the map, and the rainbow that mutates the Brainrots just appears to come out of the ground.

Tralalero upon player interaction: TRA-LA-LA! You smell that? That's the smell of gold melting into chaos!

A menu appears with 3 responses.

- What are you doing here?

- How does this machine work?

- Nevermind

If the player chooses: What are you doing here?

Tralalero responds by saying:

I found this magical hunk of junk while chilling at the bottom of the ocean. 

No idea how it works and i don't care all i know you feed it golden brainrots and it shoots a rainbow in the sky.

If the player chooses: How does this machine work?

Tralalero responds by saying:

Steal golden brainrots from random players and bring them back to me so we can power this thing up!

If the player chooses: Nevermind

Tralalero says:

Fine.

"Fine.""TRA-LA-LA!""hunk of junk""No idea how it works""We can power this thing up!"The NPC. It uses the old Rainbow animation.

[499/519]
### Trippi Troppi
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Trippi_Troppi
Non confondere con: Trulimero Trulicina or Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa
Tagline: Troppa Trippa
STATS: Rarita=Rare | Income=$15/s | Costo=$2K | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet) | RarestMutation=Phantom(33936) | RarestTrait=Claws(26024) | Sounds=Tripitropi.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Trippi Troppi appears to be a mix between a cat and a shrimp, with it having the body of a shrimp but the face and ears of a cat and legs of a shrimp.

Trippi Troppi is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Trippi Troppi is the first Rare Brainrot in the index meaning it's the cheapest one.

- Both of Trippi Troppi are required for Rebirth, with Trippi Troppi is required for Rebirth 1, and Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa is required for Rebirth 14.

- Trippi Troppi was a Brainrot that is in the Aquatic Index and could be obtained via Fishing.
--- ORIGIN ---
Trippi Troppi (full name Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa) is a Brainrot that have two distinct and separate version, a common trend for early Italian Brainrot. The original Trippi Troppi is the fish-bear version, while the more popular and iconic one is the cat-shrimp version.

The iconic cat-shrimp version was added first in Steal a Brainrot in Update 01, simply named Trippi Troppi. The original fish-bear version was then added later under the name Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa.

[500/519]
### Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Trippi_Troppi_Troppa_Trippa
Non confondere con: Trippi Troppi
Tagline: i was once useful...
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$175K/s | Costo=$30M | Status=Obtainable (Red Carpet, Backrooms Event) | Ritual=No | Sounds=TrippiTroppiTroppaTrippsound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa is a Brainrot God that costs $30M and generates $175K/s per second.

Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa appears as a fat bipedal bear with the head of a green piranha.

Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Fishing from the Fishing Event.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa has the same name as Trippi Troppi, although Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa is actually the original version of Trippi Troppi.
- This making it the first brainrot in the game to have two separate versions, altough some people refer to Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa as "Troppa Trippa" to avoid confusion.

- Both of Trippi Troppi are required for Rebirth, with Trippi Troppi is required for Rebirth 1, and Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa is required for Rebirth 14.

- Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa is a brainrot that is in the Aquatic Index and can be obtained via Fishing.
--- ORIGIN ---
Trippi Troppi (full name Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa) is a Brainrot that have two distinct and separate version, a common trend for early Italian Brainrot. The original Trippi Troppi is the fish-bear version, while the more popular and iconic one is the cat-shrimp version.

Since the iconic cat-shrimp version was added first in Steal a Brainrot with the name Trippi Troppi, the original fish-bear version that added later on is named Trippi Troppi Troppa Trippa.

Tuff Toucan is a toucan with humanoid characteristics, such as standing up on two legs and having arms. It can be seen wearing a jacket, with a colorful scheme, consisting of yellow, green, red, and blue colors spreading around it. It can be seen wearing light-blue shoes, along with pointing up towards the sky with its hands.

Tuff Toucan is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Tuff Toucans's income is $26M/s to represent the new year, 2026!

- In one way or another, Tuff Toucan might be a New Year's version of Tukanno Bananno.

- After Tuff Toucan was released, there wasn't a Limited Quantity Brainrot for over a month, finally being ended by La Romantic Grande.

- Tuff Toucan is the last Limited Quantity Brainrot that is not obtained from the Taco Truck.
