[504/519]
### Tung Tung Tung Sahur
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Tung_Tung_Tung_Sahur
Avvisi: Removed from the game., part_of_family
Famiglia: Category
Non confondere con: To to to Sahur, Ti Ti Ti Sahur, Ta Ta Ta Ta Sahur, Te Te Te Sahur, Los Tungtungtungcitos, or Bunny Bunny Bunny Sahur
Tagline: do not worry friend, for i will always be tung tung tung sahere
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$1.5M/s | Costo=$500M | Status=Removed | Update=01 | Creator=@noxaasht | Ritual=No | Sounds=Tung_Tung_Tung_Sahur_OFFICIAL_SOUND.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Tung Tung Tung Sahur appears to be a tall piece of light-brown wood resembling a bat with a smiling face holding what appears to be a bat of some sort. He has two long legs and thin eyebrows, and is in a sort of standing pose.

Tung Tung Tung Sahur is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Buying from the Red Carpet.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Tung Tung Tung Sahur used to have the biggest buff in the game, as its income was increased by 60,000x, and its cost up by 160,000x. However Tung Tung Tung Sahur's buff was surpassed by the bigger buffs of brainrots such as Tirilikalika Tirilikalako, Antonio, Signore Carapace, and Elefanto Frigo.

- Tung Tung Tung Sahur is holding a piece of wood, which while resembling a baseball bat, may very well not be. It is ridiculous to assume that he is holding a bat just because he holds one in his original image.

- Tung Tung Tung Sahur was removed from the game entirely on September 13th 2025 at 19:00 UTC due to trademark issues. Sammy preferred to remove the character to avoid the game from getting taken down or having any trouble with Roblox's Moderation and the creator's rights, but Sammy brought it back into the game during Admin Abuse in November 29th 2025.
- The proclaimed creator of Tung Tung Tung Sahur, Noxa, made a copyright claim for the character, and has supposedly asked Brainrot games to buy licensing for the Brainrot.

- While there are some Brainrots that incorporated Tung Tung Tung Sahur design like La Grande Combinasion, Los Tungtungtungcitos, and all of the variations, these Brainrots were not removed alongside Tung Tung Tung Sahur for not being the character itself and thus not copyrighted.

- If the player had a Tung Tung Tung Sahur before it was removed, it would have been replaced by Gangster Footera. It would also transfer the Mutations and Traits from this Brainrot to the Gangster Footera.
- Due to this, Rebirth 1 used to require a Tung Tung Tung Sahur, but was replaced with a Gangster Footera.

- is an Admin Abuse Exclusive event featuring Tung Tung Tung Sahur. During the event, a giant version of him with glowing red eyes and an angry expression spawns behind the Cave Entrance. The map is altered with portals emitting green mist on the wall, and Los Tungtungtungcitos with red eyes and bats would occasionally attack players and inflict the trait to Brainrots. A Brainrot with trait would have their eyes glowing in red.
- After Tung Tung Tung Sahur removal, the trait is renamed into Zombie, possibly because glowing red eyes is also a visual trope associated with enraged zombie. The icon of Zombie trait, however, still portraying Tung Tung Tung Sahur.

- Tung Tung Tung Sahur is often referred to as “Triple T” in slang.

- Tung Tung Tung Sahur was removed from the game twice, the first time is on the 13/09/2025 and the second time is on 25/04/2026.
- The reason why it was deleted for the second time is due to a federal "custody battle".
--- TUNG TUNG TUNG SAHUR ---
do not worry friend, for i will always be tung tung tung sahere

[507/519]
### Urubini Flamenguini
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Urubini_Flamenguini
Avvisi: Admin Abuse and Limited Time Mode exclusive
Tagline: He got drip.
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$150K/s | Costo=$30M | Status=Obtainable (Admin Abuse, Backrooms Event) | Sounds=Flamenguinisound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Urubini Flamenguini is a Brainrot God that released on August 15, 2025. It costs $30M and earns $150K/s in it's base. 

Urubini Flamenguini is a vulture wearing a red & black sports shirt and red & black sneakers.

Urubini Flamenguini is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Getting it from the Backrooms Event.

- From the Escape Tsunami LTM.

- Participating in Admin Abuse.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Urubini Flamenguini is based on the Brazillian soccer/football team "CR Flamengo", which has vulture as their mascot, with Urubini Flamenguini itself is made by official Flamengo's TikTok account @flamengo. This making Urubini Flamenguini one of the few Brazilian Brainrots in the game.
- In 1960s, rival teams were comparing Flamengo supporters with vulture, a black scavenger bird, meant as mockery with racist intention. At 1st June 1969, four Flamengo supporters, Luiz Octávio Vaz Pires, Romilson Meirelles, Victor Ellery, and Erick Soledade, released a real vulture with Flamengo flag tied on its foot in the Maracanã Stadion in a match against Botafogo, one of Flamengo rivals. The vulture is soaring high across the stadium, and Flamengo won the match 2-1 against Botafogo. Since then, vulture become the mascot of Flamengo, and their training ground stadium is colloquially known as Ninho do Urubu (The Vulture's Nest).

- The red and black coloring for Urubini Flamenguini is the Flamengo's shield colors, known as "Rubro-Negro".

- The 9 on Urubini Flamenguini's shirt is based on the number of "Pedro Guilherme Abreu dos Santos" shirt when he's playing for Flamengo.
--- URUBINI FLAMENGUINI ---
He got drip.

Vampira Cappucina closely resembles Ballerina Cappuccina but with a vampire-inspired design. She wears a flowing black dress paired with a red overcoat, with bat hanged on her right hand. Her eyes have a crimson glow, and traces of red liquid—possibly blood—can be seen around her mouth.

- Interestingly, Vampira Cappucina lacks the third "c" in "Cappuccina", possibly because "cappuccino" is often written without the third "c" by non native speaker, resulting in "cappucino".

- The red aura around Vampira Cappucina's mouth is a nod to the “cursed elegance” theme common in Halloween Brainrots.

- Vampira Cappuccina didn't have teeth when she was debuted. The teeth were added later.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Yess my examine one of the only five brainrots that is not a Los Brainrots that is also obtained via a ritual. The other are Noo my examine, 1x1x1x1, John Doe and Guest 666.
- All of them are obtainable with set probability in their respective rituals.

- When Yess my examine was first added, many had once assumed that the ritual was done with Job Job Job Sahurs because of its paper like appearance.

- There is an unconfirmed 74% chance you will obtain this from the Dul Dul Dul Ritual, With the other 26% going to Noo my examine.

- In Yess my examine's model, "Examen" is written wrong in the game instead saying "Examine" on the brainrot's name. This led to it colloquially called "Yess My Examen".

- There’s one wrong problem being marked as correct in the report, being 9+10=21, which is a meme reference.
--- YESS MY EXAMINE ---
An A? Wheres that A+?

[517/519]
### Yeti Claus
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Yeti_Claus
Avvisi: stub, Santa's Fuse Exclusive
Tagline: we can be more rarer
STATS: Rarita=Brainrot God | Income=$257.5K/s | Costo=$45.7M | Sounds=Yeticlaus.ogg
--- OVERVIEW ---
Yeti Claus is a Brainrot God that was released on December 6, 2025. It has a cost of $45.7M and a base income of $257.5K/s.

Yeti Claus is depicted as a yeti wearing Santa's outfit and is riding a red snowmobile.

Yeti Claus is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Fusing it in the Santa's Fuse.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Yeti Claus is the first brainrot thats a cryptid being The Yeti.

- Yeti Claus has the same income & cost as Ginger Globo. This making it the first Fuse Machine Brainrot that shared the same income & cost as another Fuse Machine Brainrot in the same Fuse Machine, in this case, Santa's Fuse.

- On the last week of Santa's Fuse, Yeti Claus is replaced with Buho de Noelo.
--- YETI CLAUS ---
we can be more rarer

### Zibra Zubra Zibralini
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Zibra_Zubra_Zibralini
Avvisi: Exclusive to the Mythic Lucky Block.
Non confondere con: Girafa Celestre, Tigrilini Watermelini, or Gorillo Watermelondrillo

--- OVERVIEW ---
Zibra Zubra Zibralini is a Mythic Brainrot obtained only through the Mythic Lucky Block.

Zibra Zubra Zibralini is a zebra head attached to a watermelon with 4 horse legs, with the front legs wearing brown boots.

Zibra Zubra Zibralini is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtaining it from the Mythic Lucky Block with a 30% chance.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- For a brief period of time after Lucky Blocks (and Zibra Zubra Zibralini) debut in Update 07, Zibra Zubra Zibralini also used to be able to spawn on Red Carpet, alongside obtained from aforementioned Mythic Lucky Block before it was patched on Update 08. This making it the only Lucky Block Brainrot that can spawn naturally.

[519/519]
### Zombie Tralala
URL: https://stealabrainrot.fandom.com/wiki/Zombie_Tralala
Avvisi: Exclusive to Fishing and the Witching Hour Event.
Non confondere con: Tralalero Tralala, Extinct Tralalero, Reindeer Tralala, Tralalita Tralala, Los Tralaleritos, Las Tralaleritas, Eviledon or Tralaledon
Tagline: He is scared of peas
STATS: Rarita=Secret | Income=$500K/s | Costo=$100M | Status=Admin Abuse Exclusive (Fishing Event) | Sounds=ScreenRecording_10-17-2025-22-57-35_1_3.wavSpawn,Halloween_Effect_Spawn_Sound.mp3
--- OVERVIEW ---
Zombie Tralala is a Secret Brainrot added to Steal a Brainrot on 10/11/25. He first appeared as Witching Hour Event Brainrot. This brainrot combines both Halloween and zombie aesthetics while retaining the iconic traits of Tralalero Tralala.

Zombie Tralala is/was obtained from the following ways:

- Obtaining from the Witching Hour Event.

- Obtaining from Fishing.

- Stealing, a Core Feature.
--- TRIVIA ---
- Zombie Tralala's design references Frankenstein's monster, keeping in theme with the Halloween event.
- Despite the name of this Brainrot, Zombie Tralala and Frankentteo share the same concept, with the only difference being the Zombie Tralala is reskin of Tralalero Tralala, and Frankentteo is reskin of Matteo.

- Zombie Tralala is a brainrot that is in the Aquatic Index and can be obtained via Fishing.
--- ZOMBIE TRALALA ---
He is scared of peas
